February 12, 2026

RISE: Self-Improving Robot Policy with Compositional World Model

Abstract (English): Despite the sustained scaling on model capacity and data acquisition, Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models remain brittle in contact-rich and dynamic manipulation tasks, where minor execution deviations can compound into failures. While reinforcement learning (RL) offers a principled path to robustness, on-policy RL in the physical world is constrained by safety risk, hardware cost, and environment reset. To bridge this gap, we present RISE, a scalable framework of robotic reinforcement learning via imagination. At its core is a Compositional World Model that (i) predicts multi-view future via a controllable dynamics model, and (ii) evaluates imagined outcomes with a progress value model, producing informative advantages for the policy improvement. Such compositional design allows state and value to be tailored by best-suited yet distinct architectures and objectives. These components are integrated into a closed-loop self-improving pipeline that continuously generates imaginary rollouts, estimates advantages, and updates the policy in imaginary space without costly physical interaction. Across three challenging real-world tasks, RISE yields significant improvement over prior art, with more than +35% absolute performance increase in dynamic brick sorting, +45% for backpack packing, and +35% for box closing, respectively.

摘要（中文）: 尽管模型容量和数据获取能力持续扩展，视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在接触密集型和动态操作任务中依然脆弱，微小的执行偏差都可能累积成失败。虽然强化学习（RL）为实现鲁棒性提供了一条有原则的路径，但物理世界中的在线策略RL受到安全风险、硬件成本和环境重置的限制。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了RISE，一个通过想象进行机器人强化学习的可扩展框架。其核心是一个组合世界模型，该模型（i）通过可控的动力学模型预测多视角未来，并且（ii）使用进度价值模型评估想象的结果，为策略改进产生信息丰富的优势函数。这种组合式设计允许状态和价值分别由最适合但不同的架构和目标进行定制。这些组件被集成到一个闭环自改进管道中，该管道持续生成想象的轨迹，评估优势函数，并在想象空间中更新策略，无需代价高昂的物理交互。在三个具有挑战性的真实世界任务中，RISE相比现有技术取得了显著改进，在动态砖块分拣方面性能绝对提升超过 +35%，背包打包提升 +45%，箱子关闭提升 +35%。

TLDR: RISE is a framework for self-improving robot policies using a compositional world model to perform reinforcement learning in imagination, achieving significant performance gains in real-world manipulation tasks.

简要说明: RISE是一个通过组合世界模型在想象中执行强化学习，从而自我提升机器人策略的框架，在现实世界的操作任务中取得了显著的性能提升。

Authors: Jiazhi Yang, Kunyang Lin, Jinwei Li, Wencong Zhang, Tianwei Lin, Longyan Wu, Zhizhong Su, Hao Zhao, Ya-Qin Zhang, Li Chen, Ping Luo, Xiangyu Yue, Hongyang Li

ABot-M0: VLA Foundation Model for Robotic Manipulation with Action Manifold Learning

Abstract (English): Building general-purpose embodied agents across diverse hardware remains a central challenge in robotics, often framed as the ''one-brain, many-forms'' paradigm. Progress is hindered by fragmented data, inconsistent representations, and misaligned training objectives. We present ABot-M0, a framework that builds a systematic data curation pipeline while jointly optimizing model architecture and training strategies, enabling end-to-end transformation of heterogeneous raw data into unified, efficient representations. From six public datasets, we clean, standardize, and balance samples to construct UniACT-dataset, a large-scale dataset with over 6 million trajectories and 9,500 hours of data, covering diverse robot morphologies and task scenarios. Unified pre-training improves knowledge transfer and generalization across platforms and tasks, supporting general-purpose embodied intelligence. To improve action prediction efficiency and stability, we propose the Action Manifold Hypothesis: effective robot actions lie not in the full high-dimensional space but on a low-dimensional, smooth manifold governed by physical laws and task constraints. Based on this, we introduce Action Manifold Learning (AML), which uses a DiT backbone to predict clean, continuous action sequences directly. This shifts learning from denoising to projection onto feasible manifolds, improving decoding speed and policy stability. ABot-M0 supports modular perception via a dual-stream mechanism that integrates VLM semantics with geometric priors and multi-view inputs from plug-and-play 3D modules such as VGGT and Qwen-Image-Edit, enhancing spatial understanding without modifying the backbone and mitigating standard VLM limitations in 3D reasoning. Experiments show components operate independently with additive benefits. We will release all code and pipelines for reproducibility and future research.

摘要（中文）: 在不同硬件上构建通用具身智能体仍然是机器人领域的核心挑战，通常被表述为“一脑多型”范式。碎片化的数据、不一致的表示以及错位的训练目标阻碍了进展。我们提出了ABot-M0框架，该框架构建了一个系统的数据管理流程，同时联合优化模型架构和训练策略，从而能够将异构原始数据端到端转换为统一、高效的表示。我们从六个公开数据集进行清洗、标准化和平衡样本，构建了UniACT-dataset，这是一个大规模数据集，包含超过600万条轨迹和9500小时的数据，涵盖了各种机器人形态和任务场景。统一的预训练提升了跨平台和跨任务的知识迁移和泛化能力，支持通用具身智能。为了提高动作预测的效率和稳定性，我们提出了动作流形假设：有效的机器人动作并非存在于完整的高维空间中，而是存在于由物理定律和任务约束所决定的低维、平滑流形上。基于此，我们引入了动作流形学习(AML)，它使用DiT骨干网络来直接预测干净、连续的动作序列。这使得学习从去噪转变为在可行流形上的投影，从而提高了解码速度和策略稳定性。ABot-M0通过双流机制支持模块化感知，该机制将VLM语义与几何先验以及来自即插即用3D模块（如VGGT和Qwen-Image-Edit）的多视角输入相结合，增强了空间理解，而无需修改骨干网络，并减轻了标准VLM在3D推理中的局限性。实验表明，各个组件独立运行，并具有附加效益。我们将发布所有代码和流程，以实现可重复性和促进未来研究。

TLDR: The paper introduces ABot-M0, a robotic manipulation framework using a large-scale dataset (UniACT) and Action Manifold Learning (AML) with a DiT backbone to predict action sequences, enhancing generalization, efficiency, and stability across diverse robot platforms and tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ABot-M0，一个机器人操作框架，它使用大规模数据集（UniACT）和动作流形学习（AML），并结合DiT骨干网络来预测动作序列，从而提高跨各种机器人平台的泛化能力、效率和稳定性。

Authors: Yandan Yang, Shuang Zeng, Tong Lin, Xinyuan Chang, Dekang Qi, Junjin Xiao, Haoyun Liu, Ronghan Chen, Yuzhi Chen, Dongjie Huo, Feng Xiong, Xing Wei, Zhiheng Ma, Mu Xu

Scaling World Model for Hierarchical Manipulation Policies

Abstract (English): Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models are promising for generalist robot manipulation but remain brittle in out-of-distribution (OOD) settings, especially with limited real-robot data. To resolve the generalization bottleneck, we introduce a hierarchical Vision-Language-Action framework \our{} that leverages the generalization of large-scale pre-trained world model for robust and generalizable VIsual Subgoal TAsk decomposition VISTA. Our hierarchical framework \our{} consists of a world model as the high-level planner and a VLA as the low-level executor. The high-level world model first divides manipulation tasks into subtask sequences with goal images, and the low-level policy follows the textual and visual guidance to generate action sequences. Compared to raw textual goal specification, these synthesized goal images provide visually and physically grounded details for low-level policies, making it feasible to generalize across unseen objects and novel scenarios. We validate both visual goal synthesis and our hierarchical VLA policies in massive out-of-distribution scenarios, and the performance of the same-structured VLA in novel scenarios could boost from 14% to 69% with the guidance generated by the world model. Results demonstrate that our method outperforms previous baselines with a clear margin, particularly in out-of-distribution scenarios. Project page: \href{https://vista-wm.github.io/}{https://vista-wm.github.io}

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言-动作 (VLA) 模型在通用机器人操作方面前景广阔，但在域外 (OOD) 环境中仍然表现脆弱，尤其是在真实机器人数据有限的情况下。为了解决泛化瓶颈，我们引入了一种分层视觉-语言-动作框架\our{}，它利用大规模预训练世界模型的泛化能力来实现鲁棒和可泛化的视觉子目标任务分解 VISTA。我们的分层框架\our{}由作为高级规划器的世界模型和作为低级执行器的 VLA 组成。高级世界模型首先将操作任务分解为带有目标图像的子任务序列，然后低级策略遵循文本和视觉指导生成动作序列。与原始文本目标规范相比，这些合成的目标图像为低级策略提供了视觉和物理上更具基础的细节，使得跨未见过的对象和新颖场景进行泛化成为可能。我们在大规模的域外场景中验证了视觉目标合成和我们的分层 VLA 策略，并且在世界模型生成的指导下，相同结构的 VLA 在新颖场景中的性能可以从 14% 提升到 69%。结果表明，我们的方法明显优于先前的基线方法，尤其是在域外场景中。项目主页: \href{https://vista-wm.github.io/}{https://vista-wm.github.io}

TLDR: This paper introduces a hierarchical Vision-Language-Action framework that uses a world model for high-level planning and a VLA model for low-level execution, improving generalization in out-of-distribution robotic manipulation tasks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种分层的视觉-语言-动作框架，该框架使用世界模型进行高层规划，并使用VLA模型进行底层执行，从而提高了在分布外机器人操作任务中的泛化能力。

Authors: Qian Long, Yueze Wang, Jiaxi Song, Junbo Zhang, Peiyan Li, Wenxuan Wang, Yuqi Wang, Haoyang Li, Shaoxuan Xie, Guocai Yao, Hanbo Zhang, Xinlong Wang, Zhongyuan Wang, Xuguang Lan, Huaping Liu, Xinghang Li

RADAR: Benchmarking Vision-Language-Action Generalization via Real-World Dynamics, Spatial-Physical Intelligence, and Autonomous Evaluation

Abstract (English): VLA models have achieved remarkable progress in embodied intelligence; however, their evaluation remains largely confined to simulations or highly constrained real-world settings. This mismatch creates a substantial reality gap, where strong benchmark performance often masks poor generalization in diverse physical environments. We identify three systemic shortcomings in current benchmarking practices that hinder fair and reliable model comparison. (1) Existing benchmarks fail to model real-world dynamics, overlooking critical factors such as dynamic object configurations, robot initial states, lighting changes, and sensor noise. (2) Current protocols neglect spatial--physical intelligence, reducing evaluation to rote manipulation tasks that do not probe geometric reasoning. (3) The field lacks scalable fully autonomous evaluation, instead relying on simplistic 2D metrics that miss 3D spatial structure or on human-in-the-loop systems that are costly, biased, and unscalable. To address these limitations, we introduce RADAR (Real-world Autonomous Dynamics And Reasoning), a benchmark designed to systematically evaluate VLA generalization under realistic conditions. RADAR integrates three core components: (1) a principled suite of physical dynamics; (2) dedicated tasks that explicitly test spatial reasoning and physical understanding; and (3) a fully autonomous evaluation pipeline based on 3D metrics, eliminating the need for human supervision. We apply RADAR to audit multiple state-of-the-art VLA models and uncover severe fragility beneath their apparent competence. Performance drops precipitously under modest physical dynamics, with the expectation of 3D IoU declining from 0.261 to 0.068 under sensor noise. Moreover, models exhibit limited spatial reasoning capability. These findings position RADAR as a necessary bench toward reliable and generalizable real-world evaluation of VLA models.

摘要（中文）: VLA模型在具身智能领域取得了显著进展；然而，对其评估仍主要局限于模拟环境或高度受限的真实世界场景。这种不匹配造成了巨大的现实差距，其中强大的基准性能通常掩盖了在多样化物理环境中较差的泛化能力。我们指出现有基准测试实践中的三个系统性缺陷，这些缺陷阻碍了公平和可靠的模型比较。(1) 现有基准未能模拟真实世界的动态性，忽略了动态物体配置、机器人初始状态、光照变化和传感器噪声等关键因素。(2) 当前协议忽视了空间-物理智能，将评估简化为不探究几何推理的死记硬背的操作任务。(3) 该领域缺乏可扩展的完全自主评估，而是依赖于忽略3D空间结构的简单2D度量或代价高昂、有偏差且不可扩展的人工干预系统。为了解决这些局限性，我们引入了RADAR（Real-world Autonomous Dynamics And Reasoning，真实世界自主动态与推理），这是一个旨在系统评估现实条件下VLA模型泛化能力的基准。RADAR集成了三个核心组件：（1）一套基于原则的物理动态特性；（2）专门设计的明确测试空间推理和物理理解的任务；以及（3）一个基于3D度量的完全自主评估流程，无需人工监督。我们应用RADAR来审计多个最先进的VLA模型，并揭示了其表面能力之下的严重脆弱性。在适度的物理动态条件下，性能急剧下降，在传感器噪声下，3D IoU的期望值从0.261下降到0.068。此外，模型表现出有限的空间推理能力。这些发现使RADAR成为VLA模型可靠且可泛化的真实世界评估的必要基准。

TLDR: The paper introduces RADAR, a new benchmark for evaluating Vision-Language-Action models in realistic environments, addressing shortcomings of existing benchmarks by incorporating real-world dynamics, spatial-physical reasoning tasks, and autonomous 3D evaluation metrics. Results using RADAR show current models struggle under realistic conditions.

简要说明: 本文介绍了RADAR，一个新的基准测试，用于评估视觉-语言-动作模型在现实环境中的性能。它解决了现有基准测试的不足，通过整合真实世界的动态性、空间-物理推理任务，以及自主的3D评估指标。使用RADAR的结果表明，当前的模型在现实条件下表现不佳。

Authors: Yuhao Chen, Zhihao Zhan, Xiaoxin Lin, Zijian Song, Hao Liu, Qinhan Lyu, Yubo Zu, Xiao Chen, Zhiyuan Liu, Tao Pu, Tianshui Chen, Keze Wang, Liang Lin, Guangrun Wang

LAP: Language-Action Pre-Training Enables Zero-shot Cross-Embodiment Transfer

Abstract (English): A long-standing goal in robotics is a generalist policy that can be deployed zero-shot on new robot embodiments without per-embodiment adaptation. Despite large-scale multi-embodiment pre-training, existing Vision-Language-Action models (VLAs) remain tightly coupled to their training embodiments and typically require costly fine-tuning. We introduce Language-Action Pre-training (LAP), a simple recipe that represents low-level robot actions directly in natural language, aligning action supervision with the pre-trained vision-language model's input-output distribution. LAP requires no learned tokenizer, no costly annotation, and no embodiment-specific architectural design. Based on LAP, we present LAP-3B, which to the best of our knowledge is the first VLA to achieve substantial zero-shot transfer to previously unseen robot embodiments without any embodiment-specific fine-tuning. Across multiple novel robots and manipulation tasks, LAP-3B attains over 50% average zero-shot success, delivering roughly a 2x improvement over the strongest prior VLAs. We further show that LAP enables efficient adaptation and favorable scaling, while unifying action prediction and VQA in a shared language-action format that yields additional gains through co-training.

摘要（中文）: 机器人领域的一个长期目标是开发一种通用策略，该策略可以在新的机器人硬件上实现零样本部署，而无需针对每个硬件进行适配。尽管经过大规模多硬件预训练，现有的视觉-语言-动作模型(VLA)仍然与其训练硬件紧密耦合，并且通常需要昂贵的微调。我们引入了语言-动作预训练(LAP)，这是一种简单的方案，直接用自然语言表示底层机器人动作，从而使动作监督与预训练的视觉-语言模型的输入-输出分布对齐。LAP不需要学习分词器，不需要昂贵的标注，也不需要针对特定硬件的架构设计。基于LAP，我们提出了LAP-3B，据我们所知，它是第一个在没有任何特定硬件微调的情况下，对先前未见过的机器人硬件实现显著零样本迁移的VLA。在多个新型机器人和操作任务中，LAP-3B实现了超过50%的平均零样本成功率，比以往最强的VLA提高了大约2倍。我们进一步表明，LAP可以实现高效的适配和良好的扩展性，同时将动作预测和视觉问答(VQA)统一成一种共享的语言-动作格式，从而通过协同训练产生额外的收益。

TLDR: The paper introduces Language-Action Pre-training (LAP) for Vision-Language-Action models, enabling zero-shot transfer to new robot embodiments by representing robot actions in natural language, achieving significant performance gains over existing methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了语言-行动预训练（LAP）方法，通过用自然语言表示机器人动作，使视觉-语言-行动模型能够零样本迁移到新的机器人载体，并且在现有方法上取得了显著的性能提升。

Authors: Lihan Zha, Asher J. Hancock, Mingtong Zhang, Tenny Yin, Yixuan Huang, Dhruv Shah, Allen Z. Ren, Anirudha Majumdar

SAGE: Scalable Agentic 3D Scene Generation for Embodied AI

Abstract (English): Real-world data collection for embodied agents remains costly and unsafe, calling for scalable, realistic, and simulator-ready 3D environments. However, existing scene-generation systems often rely on rule-based or task-specific pipelines, yielding artifacts and physically invalid scenes. We present SAGE, an agentic framework that, given a user-specified embodied task (e.g., "pick up a bowl and place it on the table"), understands the intent and automatically generates simulation-ready environments at scale. The agent couples multiple generators for layout and object composition with critics that evaluate semantic plausibility, visual realism, and physical stability. Through iterative reasoning and adaptive tool selection, it self-refines the scenes until meeting user intent and physical validity. The resulting environments are realistic, diverse, and directly deployable in modern simulators for policy training. Policies trained purely on this data exhibit clear scaling trends and generalize to unseen objects and layouts, demonstrating the promise of simulation-driven scaling for embodied AI. Code, demos, and the SAGE-10k dataset can be found on the project page here: https://nvlabs.github.io/sage.

摘要（中文）: 具身智能体在现实世界中的数据采集成本高昂且不安全，因此需要可扩展、逼真且可用于模拟器的3D环境。 然而，现有的场景生成系统通常依赖于基于规则或特定于任务的流程，从而产生伪影和物理上无效的场景。 我们提出了SAGE，一个代理框架，给定用户指定的具身任务（例如，“拿起一个碗并将其放在桌子上”），能够理解意图并自动大规模生成可用于模拟的场景。 该代理将用于布局和对象合成的多个生成器与评估语义合理性、视觉真实性和物理稳定性的评估器相结合。 通过迭代推理和自适应工具选择，它会自我优化场景，直到满足用户意图和物理有效性。 生成的环境逼真、多样化，并且可以直接部署在现代模拟器中进行策略训练。 纯粹基于此数据训练的策略表现出明显的扩展趋势，并能推广到未见过的物体和布局，证明了模拟驱动的扩展对具身人工智能的潜力。 代码、演示和SAGE-10k数据集可以在项目页面上找到：https://nvlabs.github.io/sage。

TLDR: SAGE is an agentic framework for generating realistic and scalable 3D environments for embodied AI by iteratively refining scenes based on user intent and physical constraints, demonstrating promising generalization for policies trained on this data.

简要说明: SAGE是一个agentic框架，用于生成逼真且可扩展的3D环境，以用于具身智能。它通过迭代地根据用户意图和物理约束细化场景来实现，并展示了在此数据上训练的策略具有良好的泛化能力。

Authors: Hongchi Xia, Xuan Li, Zhaoshuo Li, Qianli Ma, Jiashu Xu, Ming-Yu Liu, Yin Cui, Tsung-Yi Lin, Wei-Chiu Ma, Shenlong Wang, Shuran Song, Fangyin Wei

ST4VLA: Spatially Guided Training for Vision-Language-Action Models

Abstract (English): Large vision-language models (VLMs) excel at multimodal understanding but fall short when extended to embodied tasks, where instructions must be transformed into low-level motor actions. We introduce ST4VLA, a dual-system Vision-Language-Action framework that leverages Spatial Guided Training to align action learning with spatial priors in VLMs. ST4VLA includes two stages: (i) spatial grounding pre-training, which equips the VLM with transferable priors via scalable point, box, and trajectory prediction from both web-scale and robot-specific data, and (ii) spatially guided action post-training, which encourages the model to produce richer spatial priors to guide action generation via spatial prompting. This design preserves spatial grounding during policy learning and promotes consistent optimization across spatial and action objectives. Empirically, ST4VLA achieves substantial improvements over vanilla VLA, with performance increasing from 66.1 -> 84.6 on Google Robot and from 54.7 -> 73.2 on WidowX Robot, establishing new state-of-the-art results on SimplerEnv. It also demonstrates stronger generalization to unseen objects and paraphrased instructions, as well as robustness to long-horizon perturbations in real-world settings. These results highlight scalable spatially guided training as a promising direction for robust, generalizable robot learning. Source code, data and models are released at https://internrobotics.github.io/internvla-m1.github.io/

摘要（中文）: 大型视觉-语言模型（VLMs）在多模态理解方面表现出色，但在扩展到具身任务时却表现不足，在具身任务中，指令必须被转化为低级运动动作。我们引入了ST4VLA，一个双系统视觉-语言-动作框架，它利用空间引导训练来将动作学习与VLMs中的空间先验对齐。ST4VLA包括两个阶段：（i）空间基础预训练，通过来自网络规模和机器人特定数据的可扩展的点、框和轨迹预测，为VLM提供可迁移的先验知识，以及（ii）空间引导动作后训练，通过空间提示鼓励模型生成更丰富的空间先验来指导动作生成。这种设计在策略学习期间保留了空间基础，并促进了空间和动作目标之间的一致优化。经验表明，ST4VLA相对于原始VLA取得了显著改进，在Google Robot上的性能从66.1提升到84.6，在WidowX Robot上的性能从54.7提升到73.2，从而在SimplerEnv上建立了新的最先进结果。它还展示了对未见物体的更强的泛化能力，对释义指令的理解能力，以及在真实世界环境中对长时程扰动的鲁棒性。这些结果表明，可扩展的空间引导训练是实现鲁棒、可泛化机器人学习的一个有希望的方向。源代码、数据和模型已发布在https://internrobotics.github.io/internvla-m1.github.io/。

TLDR: The paper introduces ST4VLA, a Vision-Language-Action framework that uses spatially guided training to improve robot action learning and achieves state-of-the-art performance on robot manipulation tasks with improved generalization and robustness.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ST4VLA，一个视觉-语言-动作框架，通过空间引导训练来改进机器人动作学习，并在机器人操作任务上实现了最先进的性能，具有更强的泛化性和鲁棒性。

Authors: Jinhui Ye, Fangjing Wang, Ning Gao, Junqiu Yu, Yangkun Zhu, Bin Wang, Jinyu Zhang, Weiyang Jin, Yanwei Fu, Feng Zheng, Yilun Chen, Jiangmiao Pang

DexImit: Learning Bimanual Dexterous Manipulation from Monocular Human Videos

Abstract (English): Data scarcity fundamentally limits the generalization of bimanual dexterous manipulation, as real-world data collection for dexterous hands is expensive and labor-intensive. Human manipulation videos, as a direct carrier of manipulation knowledge, offer significant potential for scaling up robot learning. However, the substantial embodiment gap between human hands and robotic dexterous hands makes direct pretraining from human videos extremely challenging. To bridge this gap and unleash the potential of large-scale human manipulation video data, we propose DexImit, an automated framework that converts monocular human manipulation videos into physically plausible robot data, without any additional information. DexImit employs a four-stage generation pipeline: (1) reconstructing hand-object interactions from arbitrary viewpoints with near-metric scale; (2) performing subtask decomposition and bimanual scheduling; (3) synthesizing robot trajectories consistent with the demonstrated interactions; (4) comprehensive data augmentation for zero-shot real-world deployment. Building on these designs, DexImit can generate large-scale robot data based on human videos, either from the Internet or video generation models. DexImit is capable of handling diverse manipulation tasks, including tool use (e.g., cutting an apple), long-horizon tasks (e.g., making a beverage), and fine-grained manipulations (e.g., stacking cups).

摘要（中文）: 数据匮乏从根本上限制了双臂灵巧操作的泛化能力，因为灵巧手的真实世界数据采集成本高昂且劳动密集。作为操作知识的直接载体，人类操作视频为扩展机器人学习提供了巨大的潜力。然而，人类手和机器人灵巧手之间巨大的具身差异使得直接从人类视频进行预训练极具挑战性。为了弥合这一差距，并释放大规模人类操作视频数据的潜力，我们提出了一套名为 DexImit 的自动化框架，该框架可以将单目人类操作视频转换为物理上合理的机器人数据，无需任何附加信息。DexImit 采用四阶段生成流程：（1）以接近度量的尺度从任意视角重建手-物体交互；（2）执行子任务分解和双臂调度；（3）合成与演示的交互一致的机器人轨迹；（4）进行全面的数据增强以实现零样本真实世界部署。基于这些设计，DexImit 能够基于人类视频（无论来自互联网还是视频生成模型）生成大规模的机器人数据。DexImit 能够处理各种操作任务，包括工具的使用（例如，切割苹果）、长程任务（例如，制作饮料）以及精细操作（例如，堆叠杯子）。

TLDR: The paper, DexImit, proposes a framework to learn bimanual dexterous manipulation by converting monocular human manipulation videos into robot data, enabling zero-shot real-world deployment without additional information.

简要说明: DexImit论文提出了一种框架，通过将单目人类操作视频转换为机器人数据来学习双手灵巧操作，从而实现零样本真实世界部署，而无需额外信息。

Authors: Juncheng Mu, Sizhe Yang, Yiming Bao, Hojin Bae, Tianming Wei, Linning Xu, Boyi Li, Huazhe Xu, Jiangmiao Pang

VLA-JEPA: Enhancing Vision-Language-Action Model with Latent World Model

Abstract (English): Pretraining Vision-Language-Action (VLA) policies on internet-scale video is appealing, yet current latent-action objectives often learn the wrong thing: they remain anchored to pixel variation rather than action-relevant state transitions, making them vulnerable to appearance bias, nuisance motion, and information leakage. We introduce VLA-JEPA, a JEPA-style pretraining framework that sidesteps these pitfalls by design. The key idea is \emph{leakage-free state prediction}: a target encoder produces latent representations from future frames, while the student pathway sees only the current observation -- future information is used solely as supervision targets, never as input. By predicting in latent space rather than pixel space, VLA-JEPA learns dynamics abstractions that are robust to camera motion and irrelevant background changes. This yields a simple two-stage recipe -- JEPA pretraining followed by action-head fine-tuning -- without the multi-stage complexity of prior latent-action pipelines. Experiments on LIBERO, LIBERO-Plus, SimplerEnv and real-world manipulation tasks show that VLA-JEPA achieves consistent gains in generalization and robustness over existing methods.

摘要（中文）: 在互联网规模的视频上预训练视觉-语言-动作（VLA）策略极具吸引力，但现有的潜在动作目标通常学习到错误的东西：它们仍然锚定于像素变化，而不是与动作相关的状态转换，这使得它们容易受到外观偏差、干扰运动和信息泄露的影响。我们引入了VLA-JEPA，一个设计上规避这些陷阱的JEPA风格预训练框架。其核心思想是\emph{无泄露状态预测}：目标编码器从未来帧生成潜在表示，而学生通路只看到当前观测值——未来信息仅用作监督目标，绝不作为输入。通过在潜在空间而非像素空间中进行预测，VLA-JEPA学习了对相机运动和无关背景变化具有鲁棒性的动力学抽象。这产生了一个简单的两阶段方案——JEPA预训练后接动作头微调——避免了先前潜在动作流程的多阶段复杂性。在LIBERO、LIBERO-Plus、SimplerEnv和真实世界的操作任务上的实验表明，VLA-JEPA在泛化性和鲁棒性方面实现了优于现有方法的一致性提升。

TLDR: The paper introduces VLA-JEPA, a Vision-Language-Action pretraining framework that uses leakage-free state prediction in latent space to learn robust dynamics abstractions, improving generalization and robustness in robot manipulation tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了VLA-JEPA，一个视觉-语言-动作预训练框架，它在潜在空间中使用无泄漏状态预测来学习鲁棒的动态抽象，从而提高了机器人操作任务中的泛化性和鲁棒性。

Authors: Jingwen Sun, Wenyao Zhang, Zekun Qi, Shaojie Ren, Zezhi Liu, Hanxin Zhu, Guangzhong Sun, Xin Jin, Zhibo Chen

AugVLA-3D: Depth-Driven Feature Augmentation for Vision-Language-Action Models

Abstract (English): Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have recently achieved remarkable progress in robotic perception and control, yet most existing approaches primarily rely on VLM trained using 2D images, which limits their spatial understanding and action grounding in complex 3D environments. To address this limitation, we propose a novel framework that integrates depth estimation into VLA models to enrich 3D feature representations. Specifically, we employ a depth estimation baseline called VGGT to extract geometry-aware 3D cues from standard RGB inputs, enabling efficient utilization of existing large-scale 2D datasets while implicitly recovering 3D structural information. To further enhance the reliability of these depth-derived features, we introduce a new module called action assistant, which constrains the learned 3D representations with action priors and ensures their consistency with downstream control tasks. By fusing the enhanced 3D features with conventional 2D visual tokens, our approach significantly improves the generalization ability and robustness of VLA models. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method not only strengthens perception in geometrically ambiguous scenarios but also leads to superior action prediction accuracy. This work highlights the potential of depth-driven data augmentation and auxiliary expert supervision for bridging the gap between 2D observations and 3D-aware decision-making in robotic systems.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型近来已在机器人感知和控制方面取得了显著进展，然而，大多数现有方法主要依赖于使用2D图像训练的VLM，这限制了它们在复杂3D环境中的空间理解和动作定位。为了解决这个局限性，我们提出了一种新颖的框架，将深度估计集成到VLA模型中，以丰富3D特征表示。具体来说，我们采用了一个名为VGGT的深度估计基线，从标准RGB输入中提取几何感知的3D线索，从而能够有效利用现有的大规模2D数据集，同时隐式地恢复3D结构信息。为了进一步提高这些深度衍生特征的可靠性，我们引入了一个名为动作助手的模块，该模块利用动作先验来约束学习到的3D表示，并确保其与下游控制任务的一致性。通过将增强的3D特征与传统的2D视觉令牌融合，我们的方法显著提高了VLA模型的泛化能力和鲁棒性。实验结果表明，所提出的方法不仅增强了在几何模糊场景中的感知能力，而且还提高了动作预测的准确性。这项工作突出了深度驱动的数据增强和辅助专家监督在弥合机器人系统中2D观测与3D感知决策之间差距的潜力。

TLDR: The paper introduces AugVLA-3D, a framework that integrates depth estimation and action priors into Vision-Language-Action models to improve their spatial understanding and action grounding in 3D environments using 2D datasets.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了AugVLA-3D，一个将深度估计和动作先验知识集成到Vision-Language-Action模型中的框架，旨在利用2D数据集提升模型在3D环境中的空间理解和动作定位能力。

Authors: Zhifeng Rao, Wenlong Chen, Lei Xie, Xia Hua, Dongfu Yin, Zhen Tian, F. Richard Yu

Step 3.5 Flash: Open Frontier-Level Intelligence with 11B Active Parameters

Abstract (English): We introduce Step 3.5 Flash, a sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) model that bridges frontier-level agentic intelligence and computational efficiency. We focus on what matters most when building agents: sharp reasoning and fast, reliable execution. Step 3.5 Flash pairs a 196B-parameter foundation with 11B active parameters for efficient inference. It is optimized with interleaved 3:1 sliding-window/full attention and Multi-Token Prediction (MTP-3) to reduce the latency and cost of multi-round agentic interactions. To reach frontier-level intelligence, we design a scalable reinforcement learning framework that combines verifiable signals with preference feedback, while remaining stable under large-scale off-policy training, enabling consistent self-improvement across mathematics, code, and tool use. Step 3.5 Flash demonstrates strong performance across agent, coding, and math tasks, achieving 85.4% on IMO-AnswerBench, 86.4% on LiveCodeBench-v6 (2024.08-2025.05), 88.2% on tau2-Bench, 69.0% on BrowseComp (with context management), and 51.0% on Terminal-Bench 2.0, comparable to frontier models such as GPT-5.2 xHigh and Gemini 3.0 Pro. By redefining the efficiency frontier, Step 3.5 Flash provides a high-density foundation for deploying sophisticated agents in real-world industrial environments.

摘要（中文）: 我们介绍了 Step 3.5 Flash，一种稀疏的混合专家（MoE）模型，它连接了前沿水平的智能代理和计算效率。 我们专注于构建代理时最重要的因素：敏锐的推理能力和快速、可靠的执行。 Step 3.5 Flash 将一个 196B 参数的基础模型与 11B 的活跃参数配对，以实现高效的推理。 它通过交错的 3:1 滑动窗口/完全注意力机制和多Token预测（MTP-3）进行优化，以减少多轮代理交互的延迟和成本。 为了达到前沿水平的智能，我们设计了一个可扩展的强化学习框架，该框架结合了可验证的信号和偏好反馈，同时在大型离策略训练下保持稳定，从而能够在数学、代码和工具使用方面实现持续的自我改进。 Step 3.5 Flash 在代理、编码和数学任务中表现出强大的性能，在 IMO-AnswerBench 上达到 85.4%，在 LiveCodeBench-v6 (2024.08-2025.05) 上达到 86.4%，在 tau2-Bench 上达到 88.2%，在 BrowseComp 上达到 69.0% （带有上下文管理），在 Terminal-Bench 2.0 上达到 51.0%，与 GPT-5.2 xHigh 和 Gemini 3.0 Pro 等前沿模型相当。 通过重新定义效率边界，Step 3.5 Flash 为在真实世界的工业环境中部署复杂的代理提供了一个高密度基础。

TLDR: Step 3.5 Flash is a sparse MoE model optimized for agentic tasks, balancing frontier-level performance with computational efficiency through interleaved attention, multi-token prediction, and scalable reinforcement learning.

简要说明: Step 3.5 Flash是一个稀疏的MoE模型，针对Agent任务进行了优化，通过交错注意力机制、多token预测和可扩展强化学习，在达到前沿性能的同时保持了计算效率。

Wang

Found-RL: foundation model-enhanced reinforcement learning for autonomous driving

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning (RL) has emerged as a dominant paradigm for end-to-end autonomous driving (AD). However, RL suffers from sample inefficiency and a lack of semantic interpretability in complex scenarios. Foundation Models, particularly Vision-Language Models (VLMs), can mitigate this by offering rich, context-aware knowledge, yet their high inference latency hinders deployment in high-frequency RL training loops. To bridge this gap, we present Found-RL, a platform tailored to efficiently enhance RL for AD using foundation models. A core innovation is the asynchronous batch inference framework, which decouples heavy VLM reasoning from the simulation loop, effectively resolving latency bottlenecks to support real-time learning. We introduce diverse supervision mechanisms: Value-Margin Regularization (VMR) and Advantage-Weighted Action Guidance (AWAG) to effectively distill expert-like VLM action suggestions into the RL policy. Additionally, we adopt high-throughput CLIP for dense reward shaping. We address CLIP's dynamic blindness via Conditional Contrastive Action Alignment, which conditions prompts on discretized speed/command and yields a normalized, margin-based bonus from context-specific action-anchor scoring. Found-RL provides an end-to-end pipeline for fine-tuned VLM integration and shows that a lightweight RL model can achieve near-VLM performance compared with billion-parameter VLMs while sustaining real-time inference (approx. 500 FPS). Code, data, and models will be publicly available at https://github.com/ys-qu/found-rl.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习(RL)已经成为端到端自动驾驶(AD)的主流范式。然而，RL在复杂场景中存在样本效率低下和缺乏语义可解释性的问题。基础模型，特别是视觉-语言模型(VLM)，可以通过提供丰富的、上下文感知的知识来缓解这些问题，但它们的高推理延迟阻碍了在高频率RL训练循环中的部署。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了Found-RL，一个专为使用基础模型有效增强AD的RL而定制的平台。一个核心创新是异步批量推理框架，该框架将繁重的VLM推理与仿真循环解耦，有效地解决了延迟瓶颈，从而支持实时学习。我们引入了多样化的监督机制：价值边际正则化(VMR)和优势加权动作指导(AWAG)，以有效地将类似专家的VLM动作建议提炼到RL策略中。此外，我们采用高吞吐量的CLIP进行密集奖励塑造。我们通过条件对比动作对齐解决了CLIP的动态盲区问题，该方法根据离散化的速度/指令来调节提示，并从上下文相关的动作-锚点评分中产生归一化的、基于边际的奖励。Found-RL提供了一个用于微调VLM集成的端到端流水线，并表明与数十亿参数的VLM相比，一个轻量级的RL模型可以实现接近VLM的性能，同时保持实时推理(约500 FPS)。代码、数据和模型将在https://github.com/ys-qu/found-rl上公开提供。

TLDR: Found-RL enhances reinforcement learning for autonomous driving by efficiently integrating Vision-Language Models using an asynchronous batch inference framework and novel supervision mechanisms, achieving near-VLM performance with real-time inference.

简要说明: Found-RL通过高效地集成视觉语言模型，使用异步批量推理框架和新型监督机制来增强自动驾驶的强化学习，以实现接近 VLM 的性能和实时推理。

Authors: Yansong Qu, Zihao Sheng, Zilin Huang, Jiancong Chen, Yuhao Luo, Tianyi Wang, Yiheng Feng, Samuel Labi, Sikai Chen

SimuScene: Training and Benchmarking Code Generation to Simulate Physical Scenarios

Abstract (English): Large language models (LLMs) have been extensively studied for tasks like math competitions, complex coding, and scientific reasoning, yet their ability to accurately represent and simulate physical scenarios via code remains underexplored. We propose SimuScene, the first systematic study that trains and evaluates LLMs on simulating physical scenarios across five physics domains and 52 physical concepts. We build an automatic pipeline to collect data, with human verification to ensure quality. The final dataset contains 7,659 physical scenarios with 334 human-verified examples as the test set. We evaluated 10 contemporary LLMs and found that even the strongest model achieves only a 21.5% pass rate, demonstrating the difficulty of the task. Finally, we introduce a reinforcement learning pipeline with visual rewards that uses a vision-language model as a judge to train textual models. Experiments show that training with our data improves physical simulation via code while substantially enhancing general code generation performance.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLM）已经在诸如数学竞赛、复杂编程和科学推理等任务中得到广泛研究，然而，它们通过代码准确表示和模拟物理场景的能力仍然未被充分探索。我们提出了SimuScene，首个系统性研究，旨在训练和评估LLM在五个物理领域和52个物理概念中模拟物理场景的能力。我们构建了一个自动化的数据收集流程，并使用人工验证来确保质量。最终数据集包含7659个物理场景，其中334个经过人工验证的示例作为测试集。我们评估了10个当代LLM，发现即使是最强大的模型也仅能达到21.5%的通过率，表明了该任务的难度。最后，我们引入了一个带有视觉奖励的强化学习流程，该流程使用视觉-语言模型作为裁判来训练文本模型。实验表明，使用我们的数据进行训练可以提高通过代码进行的物理模拟能力，同时显著增强通用代码生成性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces SimuScene, a dataset and benchmark for training and evaluating LLMs on simulating physical scenarios via code, finding current models perform poorly and demonstrating improved performance through reinforcement learning with visual rewards.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 SimuScene，一个用于训练和评估 LLM 基于代码模拟物理场景的数据集和基准。研究表明，当前的 LLM 在此任务上表现不佳，并通过使用视觉奖励进行强化学习，实验证明可以提高性能。

Authors: Yanan Wang, Renxi Wang, Yongxin Wang, Xuezhi Liang, Fajri Koto, Timothy Baldwin, Xiaodan Liang, Haonan Li

RePO: Bridging On-Policy Learning and Off-Policy Knowledge through Rephrasing Policy Optimization

Abstract (English): Aligning large language models (LLMs) on domain-specific data remains a fundamental challenge. Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) offers a straightforward way to inject domain knowledge but often degrades the model's generality. In contrast, on-policy reinforcement learning (RL) preserves generality but fails to effectively assimilate hard samples that exceed the model's current reasoning level. Recent off-policy RL attempts improve hard sample utilization, yet they suffer from severe training instability due to the forced distribution shift toward off-policy knowledge. To reconcile effective off-policy knowledge absorption with the stability of on-policy RL, we propose Rephrasing Policy Optimization (RePO). In RePO, the policy model is prompted to first comprehend off-policy knowledge and then rephrase it into trajectories that conform to its own stylistic and parametric distribution. RePO dynamically replaces low-reward rollouts with these rephrased, high-quality trajectories. This strategy guides the model toward correct reasoning paths while strictly preserving on-policy training dynamics. Experiments on several benchmarks demonstrate that RePO improves hard-sample utilization and outperforms existing baselines, achieving state-of-the-art performance.

摘要（中文）: 在领域特定数据上对齐大型语言模型（LLMs）仍然是一项根本性的挑战。监督微调（SFT）提供了一种直接注入领域知识的方法，但常常会降低模型的泛化性。相反，在线强化学习（RL）保留了泛化性，但无法有效吸收超出模型当前推理水平的难样本。 近期离线RL尝试改进了难样本利用，但由于强制将分布转移到离线知识，因此遭受严重的训练不稳定。为了协调有效的离线知识吸收与在线RL的稳定性，我们提出了重述策略优化（RePO）。 在RePO中，策略模型首先被提示理解离线知识，然后将其重述为符合其自身风格和参数分布的轨迹。 RePO动态地将低奖励的rollout替换为这些重述的、高质量的轨迹。这种策略引导模型走向正确的推理路径，同时严格保留了在线训练的动态性。 在几个基准测试上的实验表明，RePO提高了难样本的利用率，并优于现有的基线，实现了最先进的性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces RePO, a novel reinforcement learning method that leverages off-policy knowledge by prompting the policy model to rephrase it into on-policy compatible trajectories, improving hard-sample utilization and stability.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了RePO，一种新的强化学习方法，它通过提示策略模型将离策略知识改写为与在策略兼容的轨迹，从而利用离策略知识，提高了困难样本的利用率和训练稳定性。

Authors: Linxuan Xia, Xiaolong Yang, Yongyuan Chen, Enyue Zhao, Deng Cai, Yasheng Wang, Boxi Wu

Hardware Co-Design Scaling Laws via Roofline Modelling for On-Device LLMs

Abstract (English): Vision-Language-Action Models (VLAs) have emerged as a key paradigm of Physical AI and are increasingly deployed in autonomous vehicles, robots, and smart spaces. In these resource-constrained on-device settings, selecting an appropriate large language model (LLM) backbone is a critical challenge: models must balance accuracy with strict inference latency and hardware efficiency constraints. This makes hardware-software co-design a game-changing requirement for on-device LLM deployment, where each hardware platform demands a tailored architectural solution. We propose a hardware co-design law that jointly captures model accuracy and inference performance. Specifically, we model training loss as an explicit function of architectural hyperparameters and characterise inference latency via roofline modelling. We empirically evaluate 1,942 candidate architectures on NVIDIA Jetson Orin, training 170 selected models for 10B tokens each to fit a scaling law relating architecture to training loss. By coupling this scaling law with latency modelling, we establish a direct accuracy-latency correspondence and identify the Pareto frontier for hardware co-designed LLMs. We further formulate architecture search as a joint optimisation over precision and performance, deriving feasible design regions under industrial hardware and application budgets. Our approach reduces architecture selection from months to days. At the same latency as Qwen2.5-0.5B on the target hardware, our co-designed architecture achieves 19.42% lower perplexity on WikiText-2. To our knowledge, this is the first principled and operational framework for hardware co-design scaling laws in on-device LLM deployment. We will make the code and related checkpoints publicly available.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言-动作模型（VLA）已经成为物理人工智能的关键范式，并越来越多地部署在自动驾驶车辆、机器人和智能空间中。在这些资源受限的设备端环境中，选择合适的LLM骨干网络是一个关键挑战：模型必须在准确性与严格的推理延迟和硬件效率约束之间取得平衡。这使得软硬件协同设计成为设备端LLM部署的一项颠覆性要求，其中每个硬件平台都需要量身定制的架构解决方案。我们提出了一种软硬件协同设计法则，该法则共同捕捉模型准确性和推理性能。具体而言，我们将训练损失建模为架构超参数的显式函数，并通过屋脊线模型描述推理延迟。我们在NVIDIA Jetson Orin上对1942个候选架构进行了实证评估，训练了170个选定的模型，每个模型训练100亿tokens，以拟合一个将架构与训练损失相关联的缩放律。通过将此缩放律与延迟建模相结合，我们建立了直接的准确性-延迟对应关系，并确定了软硬件协同设计LLM的帕累托前沿。我们进一步将架构搜索表述为精度和性能的联合优化，推导出工业硬件和应用预算下的可行设计区域。我们的方法将架构选择的时间从数月缩短到数天。在目标硬件上与Qwen2.5-0.5B相同延迟的情况下，我们协同设计的架构在WikiText-2上实现了19.42%的更低困惑度。据我们所知，这是第一个在设备端LLM部署中用于软硬件协同设计缩放律的原则性且可操作的框架。我们将公开代码和相关检查点。

TLDR: The paper presents a hardware co-design framework for on-device LLMs using roofline modeling and scaling laws to optimize accuracy and latency, achieving significant perplexity reduction compared to existing models like Qwen2.5-0.5B.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一个针对端侧LLM的硬件协同设计框架，利用屋顶线模型和缩放定律优化精度和延迟，与现有模型（如Qwen2.5-0.5B）相比，可显著降低困惑度。

Authors: Luoyang Sun, Jiwen Jiang, Yifeng Ding, Fengfa Li, Yan Song, Haifeng Zhang, Jian Ying, Lei Ren, Kun Zhan, Wei Chen, Yan Xie, Cheng Deng

EgoHumanoid: Unlocking In-the-Wild Loco-Manipulation with Robot-Free Egocentric Demonstration

Abstract (English): Human demonstrations offer rich environmental diversity and scale naturally, making them an appealing alternative to robot teleoperation. While this paradigm has advanced robot-arm manipulation, its potential for the more challenging, data-hungry problem of humanoid loco-manipulation remains largely unexplored. We present EgoHumanoid, the first framework to co-train a vision-language-action policy using abundant egocentric human demonstrations together with a limited amount of robot data, enabling humanoids to perform loco-manipulation across diverse real-world environments. To bridge the embodiment gap between humans and robots, including discrepancies in physical morphology and viewpoint, we introduce a systematic alignment pipeline spanning from hardware design to data processing. A portable system for scalable human data collection is developed, and we establish practical collection protocols to improve transferability. At the core of our human-to-humanoid alignment pipeline lies two key components. The view alignment reduces visual domain discrepancies caused by camera height and perspective variation. The action alignment maps human motions into a unified, kinematically feasible action space for humanoid control. Extensive real-world experiments demonstrate that incorporating robot-free egocentric data significantly outperforms robot-only baselines by 51\%, particularly in unseen environments. Our analysis further reveals which behaviors transfer effectively and the potential for scaling human data.

摘要（中文）: 人类演示提供了丰富的环境多样性并能自然地扩展规模，使其成为机器人遥操作的一个具有吸引力的替代方案。尽管这种模式推动了机械臂操作的发展，但它在人形机器人运动操作这一更具挑战性、更需要大量数据的问题上的潜力仍未得到充分探索。我们提出了EgoHumanoid，这是第一个利用丰富的以自我为中心的人类演示数据以及少量机器人数据来联合训练视觉-语言-动作策略的框架，使人形机器人能够在各种真实世界环境中执行运动操作。为了弥合人类和机器人之间的体现差距，包括物理形态和视角的差异，我们引入了一个系统的对齐流程，涵盖从硬件设计到数据处理的各个方面。我们开发了一个可扩展的人类数据收集的便携式系统，并建立了实用的收集协议以提高可迁移性。我们的人类到人形机器人对齐流程的核心是两个关键组件。视角对齐减少了由相机高度和透视变化引起的视觉域差异。动作对齐将人类运动映射到统一的、运动学上可行的人形机器人控制动作空间中。大量的真实世界实验表明，结合无机器人的以自我为中心的数据显著优于纯机器人基线51％，尤其是在未见过的环境中。我们的分析进一步揭示了哪些行为能够有效地迁移，以及扩展人类数据的潜力。

TLDR: The paper introduces EgoHumanoid, a framework for co-training vision-language-action policies for humanoid loco-manipulation using human egocentric demonstrations and limited robot data, achieving significant improvements over robot-only baselines.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了EgoHumanoid，一个使用人类自我中心演示和有限的机器人数据共同训练类人机器人Loco-Manipulation的视觉-语言-动作策略的框架，与仅使用机器人的baseline相比，实现了显著的改进。

Authors: Modi Shi, Shijia Peng, Jin Chen, Haoran Jiang, Yinghui Li, Di Huang, Ping Luo, Hongyang Li, Li Chen

ContactGaussian-WM: Learning Physics-Grounded World Model from Videos

Abstract (English): Developing world models that understand complex physical interactions is essential for advancing robotic planning and simulation.However, existing methods often struggle to accurately model the environment under conditions of data scarcity and complex contact-rich dynamic motion.To address these challenges, we propose ContactGaussian-WM, a differentiable physics-grounded rigid-body world model capable of learning intricate physical laws directly from sparse and contact-rich video sequences.Our framework consists of two core components: (1) a unified Gaussian representation for both visual appearance and collision geometry, and (2) an end-to-end differentiable learning framework that differentiates through a closed-form physics engine to infer physical properties from sparse visual observations.Extensive simulations and real-world evaluations demonstrate that ContactGaussian-WM outperforms state-of-the-art methods in learning complex scenarios, exhibiting robust generalization capabilities.Furthermore, we showcase the practical utility of our framework in downstream applications, including data synthesis and real-time MPC.

摘要（中文）: 开发能够理解复杂物理交互的世界模型对于推进机器人规划和仿真至关重要。然而，现有方法通常难以在数据匮乏和复杂、富含接触的动态运动条件下准确地建模环境。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了 ContactGaussian-WM，一个可微分的、基于物理刚体世界模型，能够直接从稀疏且富含接触的视频序列中学习复杂的物理定律。我们的框架包含两个核心组件：（1）一个统一的高斯表示，用于视觉外观和碰撞几何，以及（2）一个端到端可微分的学习框架，通过闭式物理引擎进行微分，从而从稀疏的视觉观测中推断物理属性。大量的模拟和真实世界评估表明，ContactGaussian-WM 在学习复杂场景方面优于最先进的方法，并展现出强大的泛化能力。此外，我们展示了我们的框架在下游应用中的实际效用，包括数据合成和实时模型预测控制(MPC)。

TLDR: ContactGaussian-WM introduces a differentiable, physics-grounded world model that learns complex physical interactions from sparse, contact-rich video using a unified Gaussian representation and a closed-form physics engine, outperforming state-of-the-art methods.

简要说明: ContactGaussian-WM 介绍了一种可微分的、基于物理的世界模型，该模型使用统一的高斯表示和闭合形式物理引擎，从稀疏的、富含接触的视频中学习复杂的物理交互，超越了最先进的方法。

Authors: Meizhong Wang, Wanxin Jin, Kun Cao, Lihua Xie, Yiguang Hong

Multi-Task Reinforcement Learning of Drone Aerobatics by Exploiting Geometric Symmetries

Abstract (English): Flight control for autonomous micro aerial vehicles (MAVs) is evolving from steady flight near equilibrium points toward more aggressive aerobatic maneuvers, such as flips, rolls, and Power Loop. Although reinforcement learning (RL) has shown great potential in these tasks, conventional RL methods often suffer from low data efficiency and limited generalization. This challenge becomes more pronounced in multi-task scenarios where a single policy is required to master multiple maneuvers. In this paper, we propose a novel end-to-end multi-task reinforcement learning framework, called GEAR (Geometric Equivariant Aerobatics Reinforcement), which fully exploits the inherent SO(2) rotational symmetry in MAV dynamics and explicitly incorporates this property into the policy network architecture. By integrating an equivariant actor network, FiLM-based task modulation, and a multi-head critic, GEAR achieves both efficiency and flexibility in learning diverse aerobatic maneuvers, enabling a data-efficient, robust, and unified framework for aerobatic control. GEAR attains a 98.85\% success rate across various aerobatic tasks, significantly outperforming baseline methods. In real-world experiments, GEAR demonstrates stable execution of multiple maneuvers and the capability to combine basic motion primitives to complete complex aerobatics.

摘要（中文）: 自主微型飞行器(MAV)的飞行控制正从平衡点附近的稳定飞行演变为更激进的特技飞行，例如翻转、滚转和动力环。尽管强化学习(RL)在这些任务中展现出巨大潜力，但传统的RL方法通常存在数据效率低和泛化能力有限的问题。在需要单个策略来掌握多种机动的多任务场景中，这一挑战变得更加显著。在本文中，我们提出了一种新型的端到端多任务强化学习框架，名为GEAR（几何等变特技强化学习），它充分利用了MAV动力学中固有的SO(2)旋转对称性，并将此性质显式地结合到策略网络架构中。通过集成一个等变演员网络、基于FiLM的任务调制和一个多头评论家，GEAR在学习各种特技机动方面实现了效率和灵活性，从而为特技控制提供了一个数据高效、稳健和统一的框架。GEAR在各种特技任务中达到了 98.85% 的成功率，显著优于基线方法。在真实世界的实验中，GEAR展示了多个机动的稳定执行能力，以及组合基本运动原语来完成复杂特技的能力。

TLDR: The paper introduces GEAR, a multi-task reinforcement learning framework leveraging geometric symmetries (SO(2) rotational symmetry) for efficient and robust drone aerobatic control, demonstrating superior performance in both simulation and real-world experiments.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为GEAR的多任务强化学习框架，它利用几何对称性（SO(2)旋转对称性）实现高效且鲁棒的无人机特技飞行控制，并在仿真和真实世界实验中表现出卓越的性能。

Authors: Zhanyu Guo, Zikang Yin, Guobin Zhu, Shiliang Guo, Shiyu Zhao

Towards Learning a Generalizable 3D Scene Representation from 2D Observations

Abstract (English): We introduce a Generalizable Neural Radiance Field approach for predicting 3D workspace occupancy from egocentric robot observations. Unlike prior methods operating in camera-centric coordinates, our model constructs occupancy representations in a global workspace frame, making it directly applicable to robotic manipulation. The model integrates flexible source views and generalizes to unseen object arrangements without scene-specific finetuning. We demonstrate the approach on a humanoid robot and evaluate predicted geometry against 3D sensor ground truth. Trained on 40 real scenes, our model achieves 26mm reconstruction error, including occluded regions, validating its ability to infer complete 3D occupancy beyond traditional stereo vision methods.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了一种可泛化的神经辐射场方法，用于从以自我为中心的机器人观测中预测3D工作区占用情况。与先前在以相机为中心的坐标系中运行的方法不同，我们的模型在全局工作区坐标系中构建占用情况表示，使其可直接应用于机器人操作。 该模型集成了灵活的源视图，并在未见过的对象排列中进行泛化，而无需针对特定场景进行微调。我们在一个人形机器人上演示了该方法，并根据3D传感器真值评估了预测的几何形状。 我们的模型在40个真实场景上进行训练，实现了26毫米的重建误差，包括遮挡区域，验证了其推断完整3D占用情况的能力，超越了传统的立体视觉方法。

TLDR: This paper introduces a Generalizable Neural Radiance Field approach that predicts 3D workspace occupancy from robot's egocentric vision in a global workspace frame, allowing the model to generalize to unseen object arrangements directly applicable to robotic manipulation.

Authors: Martin Gromniak, Jan-Gerrit Habekost, Sebastian Kamp, Sven Magg, Stefan Wermter

Safe mobility support system using crowd mapping and avoidance route planning using VLM

Abstract (English): Autonomous mobile robots offer promising solutions for labor shortages and increased operational efficiency. However, navigating safely and effectively in dynamic environments, particularly crowded areas, remains challenging. This paper proposes a novel framework that integrates Vision-Language Models (VLM) and Gaussian Process Regression (GPR) to generate dynamic crowd-density maps (``Abstraction Maps'') for autonomous robot navigation. Our approach utilizes VLM's capability to recognize abstract environmental concepts, such as crowd densities, and represents them probabilistically via GPR. Experimental results from real-world trials on a university campus demonstrated that robots successfully generated routes avoiding both static obstacles and dynamic crowds, enhancing navigation safety and adaptability.

Authors: Sena Saito, Kenta Tabata, Renato Miyagusuku, Koichi Ozaki

From Steering to Pedalling: Do Autonomous Driving VLMs Generalize to Cyclist-Assistive Spatial Perception and Planning?

Abstract (English): Cyclists often encounter safety-critical situations in urban traffic, highlighting the need for assistive systems that support safe and informed decision-making. Recently, vision-language models (VLMs) have demonstrated strong performance on autonomous driving benchmarks, suggesting their potential for general traffic understanding and navigation-related reasoning. However, existing evaluations are predominantly vehicle-centric and fail to assess perception and reasoning from a cyclist-centric viewpoint. To address this gap, we introduce CyclingVQA, a diagnostic benchmark designed to probe perception, spatio-temporal understanding, and traffic-rule-to-lane reasoning from a cyclist's perspective. Evaluating 31+ recent VLMs spanning general-purpose, spatially enhanced, and autonomous-driving-specialized models, we find that current models demonstrate encouraging capabilities, while also revealing clear areas for improvement in cyclist-centric perception and reasoning, particularly in interpreting cyclist-specific traffic cues and associating signs with the correct navigational lanes. Notably, several driving-specialized models underperform strong generalist VLMs, indicating limited transfer from vehicle-centric training to cyclist-assistive scenarios. Finally, through systematic error analysis, we identify recurring failure modes to guide the development of more effective cyclist-assistive intelligent systems.

摘要（中文）: 骑行者在城市交通中经常遇到危及安全的状况，这突显了对辅助系统的需求，这些系统能够支持安全且知情的决策。 近年来，视觉-语言模型 (VLMs) 在自动驾驶基准测试中表现出强大的性能，表明它们在通用交通理解和导航相关推理方面的潜力。 然而，现有的评估主要以车辆为中心，未能从骑行者角度评估感知和推理。 为了弥补这一差距，我们推出了 CyclingVQA，这是一种诊断基准，旨在探测骑行者视角的感知、时空理解以及交通规则到车道的推理。 我们评估了 31 多个最新的 VLM，涵盖通用型、空间增强型和自动驾驶专用模型，发现当前的模型表现出令人鼓舞的能力，同时也揭示了以骑行者为中心的感知和推理方面明显的改进空间，特别是在解读骑行者特有的交通信号以及将标志与正确的导航车道相关联方面。值得注意的是，一些驾驶专用模型表现不如强大的通用 VLM，表明从以车辆为中心的训练到骑行者辅助场景的迁移受到限制。 最后，通过系统的误差分析，我们识别出反复出现的失败模式，以指导开发更有效的骑行者辅助智能系统。

TLDR: This paper introduces CyclingVQA, a benchmark designed to evaluate vision-language models (VLMs) from a cyclist's perspective, revealing limitations in existing models trained with a vehicle-centric bias and highlighting areas for improvement in cyclist-assistive systems.

Authors: Krishna Kanth Nakka, Vedasri Nakka

From Representational Complementarity to Dual Systems: Synergizing VLM and Vision-Only Backbones for End-to-End Driving

Abstract (English): Vision-Language-Action (VLA) driving augments end-to-end (E2E) planning with language-enabled backbones, yet it remains unclear what changes beyond the usual accuracy--cost trade-off. We revisit this question with 3--RQ analysis in RecogDrive by instantiating the system with a full VLM and vision-only backbones, all under an identical diffusion Transformer planner. RQ1: At the backbone level, the VLM can introduce additional subspaces upon the vision-only backbones. RQ2: This unique subspace leads to a different behavioral in some long-tail scenario: the VLM tends to be more aggressive whereas ViT is more conservative, and each decisively wins on about 2--3% of test scenarios; With an oracle that selects, per scenario, the better trajectory between the VLM and ViT branches, we obtain an upper bound of 93.58 PDMS. RQ3: To fully harness this observation, we propose HybridDriveVLA, which runs both ViT and VLM branches and selects between their endpoint trajectories using a learned scorer, improving PDMS to 92.10. Finally, DualDriveVLA implements a practical fast--slow policy: it runs ViT by default and invokes the VLM only when the scorer's confidence falls below a threshold; calling the VLM on 15% of scenarios achieves 91.00 PDMS while improving throughput by 3.2x. Code will be released.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言-行动（VLA）驾驶利用语言支持的主干网络增强了端到端（E2E）规划，但其在通常的准确性-成本权衡之外还产生了哪些变化尚不清楚。我们通过在RecogDrive中进行3-RQ分析来重新审视这个问题，其中该系统实例化时配备了完整的VLM和纯视觉主干网络，所有这些都在相同的扩散Transformer规划器下进行。RQ1：在主干网络层面，VLM可以在纯视觉主干网络的基础上引入额外的子空间。RQ2：这种独特的子空间导致在一些长尾场景中产生不同的行为：VLM倾向于更激进，而ViT则更保守，并且各自在约2-3%的测试场景中取得显著优势；通过一个预言机，在每个场景中选择VLM和ViT分支之间更好的轨迹，我们获得了93.58 PDMS的上限。RQ3：为了充分利用这一观察结果，我们提出了HybridDriveVLA，它同时运行ViT和VLM分支，并使用学习的评分器在它们的终点轨迹之间进行选择，将PDMS提升到92.10。最后，DualDriveVLA实现了一种实用的快-慢策略：它默认运行ViT，并且仅当评分器的置信度低于阈值时才调用VLM；在15%的场景调用VLM可以达到91.00 PDMS，同时将吞吐量提高3.2倍。代码即将发布。

TLDR: This paper explores the complementarity of VLM and vision-only backbones in end-to-end driving, proposing a hybrid approach that leverages both for improved performance and efficiency, validated within the RecogDrive framework.

简要说明: 该论文探讨了视觉语言模型（VLM）和纯视觉骨干网络在端到端驾驶中的互补性，提出了一种混合方法，利用两者来提高性能和效率，并在RecogDrive框架中进行了验证。

Say, Dream, and Act: Learning Video World Models for Instruction-Driven Robot Manipulation

Abstract (English): Robotic manipulation requires anticipating how the environment evolves in response to actions, yet most existing systems lack this predictive capability, often resulting in errors and inefficiency. While Vision-Language Models (VLMs) provide high-level guidance, they cannot explicitly forecast future states, and existing world models either predict only short horizons or produce spatially inconsistent frames. To address these challenges, we propose a framework for fast and predictive video-conditioned action. Our approach first selects and adapts a robust video generation model to ensure reliable future predictions, then applies adversarial distillation for fast, few-step video generation, and finally trains an action model that leverages both generated videos and real observations to correct spatial errors. Extensive experiments show that our method produces temporally coherent, spatially accurate video predictions that directly support precise manipulation, achieving significant improvements in embodiment consistency, spatial referring ability, and task completion over existing baselines. Codes & Models will be released.

摘要（中文）: 机器人操作需要预测环境如何响应动作而演变，然而大多数现有系统缺乏这种预测能力，常常导致错误和效率低下。尽管视觉-语言模型（VLMs）提供高层次的指导，它们无法显式地预测未来状态，并且现有的世界模型要么仅预测短时程，要么产生空间不一致的帧。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了一种用于快速和预测性视频条件动作的框架。我们的方法首先选择并调整一个鲁棒的视频生成模型，以确保可靠的未来预测，然后应用对抗蒸馏进行快速、少步视频生成，最后训练一个动作模型，该模型利用生成的视频和真实观测来纠正空间误差。大量实验表明，我们的方法能够产生时间上连贯、空间上准确的视频预测，从而直接支持精确操作，在具身一致性、空间指代能力和任务完成方面，相比现有基线取得了显著的改进。代码和模型将被发布。

TLDR: This paper presents a novel framework that combines video generation and adversarial distillation techniques to enable robots to learn world models for instruction-driven manipulation, achieving improved temporal coherence, spatial accuracy, and task completion.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种新的框架，结合了视频生成和对抗蒸馏技术，使机器人能够学习用于指令驱动操作的世界模型，从而提高时间连贯性、空间准确性和任务完成度。

Authors: Songen Gu, Yunuo Cai, Tianyu Wang, Simo Wu, Yanwei Fu

ReSPEC: A Framework for Online Multispectral Sensor Reconfiguration in Dynamic Environments

Abstract (English): Multi-sensor fusion is central to robust robotic perception, yet most existing systems operate under static sensor configurations, collecting all modalities at fixed rates and fidelity regardless of their situational utility. This rigidity wastes bandwidth, computation, and energy, and prevents systems from prioritizing sensors under challenging conditions such as poor lighting or occlusion. Recent advances in reinforcement learning (RL) and modality-aware fusion suggest the potential for adaptive perception, but prior efforts have largely focused on re-weighting features at inference time, ignoring the physical cost of sensor data collection. We introduce a framework that unifies sensing, learning, and actuation into a closed reconfiguration loop. A task-specific detection backbone extracts multispectral features (e.g. RGB, IR, mmWave, depth) and produces quantitative contribution scores for each modality. These scores are passed to an RL agent, which dynamically adjusts sensor configurations, including sampling frequency, resolution, sensing range, and etc., in real time. Less informative sensors are down-sampled or deactivated, while critical sensors are sampled at higher fidelity as environmental conditions evolve. We implement and evaluate this framework on a mobile rover, showing that adaptive control reduces GPU load by 29.3\% with only a 5.3\% accuracy drop compared to a heuristic baseline. These results highlight the potential of resource-aware adaptive sensing for embedded robotic platforms.

摘要（中文）: 多传感器融合是实现鲁棒机器人感知的核心，然而，现有的大多数系统都在静态传感器配置下运行，以固定的速率和保真度采集所有模态数据，而不管它们在特定情境下的效用。这种刚性方法浪费了带宽、计算和能源，并阻碍了系统在诸如光照不良或遮挡等具有挑战性的条件下对传感器进行优先级排序。强化学习（RL）和模态感知融合的最新进展表明了自适应感知的潜力，但先前的研究主要集中在推理时对特征进行重新加权，忽略了传感器数据收集的物理成本。我们提出一个框架，将感知、学习和执行统一到一个闭环重配置中。一个特定任务的检测骨干网络提取多光谱特征（例如，RGB、IR、毫米波、深度），并为每个模态生成量化的贡献分数。这些分数被传递给一个RL智能体，该智能体实时动态调整传感器配置，包括采样频率、分辨率、感知范围等。不太有信息的传感器被降采样或停用，而关键传感器则以更高的保真度进行采样，随着环境条件的变化而变化。我们在移动漫游车上实现并评估了这个框架，结果表明，与启发式基线相比，自适应控制可以将GPU负载降低29.3%，而精度仅下降5.3%。这些结果突出了资源感知的自适应感知对于嵌入式机器人平台的潜力。

TLDR: This paper presents a reinforcement learning framework called ReSPEC for dynamically reconfiguring multispectral sensors on a mobile robot based on modality contribution scores. It demonstrates resource savings with minimal accuracy loss.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种名为 ReSPEC 的强化学习框架，该框架基于模态贡献分数动态地重新配置移动机器人上的多光谱传感器。它展示了资源节省，同时精度损失最小。

Authors: Yanchen Liu, Yuang Fan, Minghui Zhao, Xiaofan Jiang

Co-jump: Cooperative Jumping with Quadrupedal Robots via Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): While single-agent legged locomotion has witnessed remarkable progress, individual robots remain fundamentally constrained by physical actuation limits. To transcend these boundaries, we introduce Co-jump, a cooperative task where two quadrupedal robots synchronize to execute jumps far beyond their solo capabilities. We tackle the high-impulse contact dynamics of this task under a decentralized setting, achieving synchronization without explicit communication or pre-specified motion primitives. Our framework leverages Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (MAPPO) enhanced by a progressive curriculum strategy, which effectively overcomes the sparse-reward exploration challenges inherent in mechanically coupled systems. We demonstrate robust performance in simulation and successful transfer to physical hardware, executing multi-directional jumps onto platforms up to 1.5 m in height. Specifically, one of the robots achieves a foot-end elevation of 1.1 m, which represents a 144% improvement over the 0.45 m jump height of a standalone quadrupedal robot, demonstrating superior vertical performance. Notably, this precise coordination is achieved solely through proprioceptive feedback, establishing a foundation for communication-free collaborative locomotion in constrained environments.

摘要（中文）: 本文介绍了一种合作任务Co-jump，旨在突破单智能体腿式运动固有的物理驱动限制。在该任务中，两只四足机器人同步执行跳跃，其性能远超单只机器人的能力。我们处理了该任务中高冲击的接触动力学，并在去中心化环境下实现了同步，无需显式通信或预先指定的运动原语。我们的框架利用多智能体近端策略优化（MAPPO），并辅以渐进式课程学习策略，有效克服了机械耦合系统中固有的稀疏奖励探索挑战。我们展示了在仿真中的稳健性能，并成功迁移到实体硬件上，实现了向高达1.5米的平台进行多方向跳跃。特别地，其中一台机器人的足端高度达到了1.1米，相比于单只四足机器人0.45米的跳跃高度，提升了144%，展现了卓越的垂直性能。值得注意的是，这种精确的协调仅通过本体感受反馈实现，为受限环境中无需通信的协作运动奠定了基础。

TLDR: The paper presents Co-jump, a multi-agent reinforcement learning framework for two quadrupedal robots to perform cooperative jumps exceeding individual capabilities, achieving synchronization without communication, and demonstrating successful transfer to physical hardware.

简要说明: 该论文提出了Co-jump，一种多智能体强化学习框架，使两个四足机器人能够进行超出个体能力的协同跳跃，无需通信即可实现同步，并成功迁移到物理硬件。

Authors: Shihao Dong, Yeke Chen, Zeren Luo, Jiahui Zhang, Bowen Xu, Jinghan Lin, Yimin Han, Ji Ma, Zhiyou Yu, Yudong Zhao, Peng Lu

Towards Long-Lived Robots: Continual Learning VLA Models via Reinforcement Fine-Tuning

Abstract (English): Pretrained on large-scale and diverse datasets, VLA models demonstrate strong generalization and adaptability as general-purpose robotic policies. However, Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT), which serves as the primary mechanism for adapting VLAs to downstream domains, requires substantial amounts of task-specific data and is prone to catastrophic forgetting. To address these limitations, we propose LifeLong-RFT, a simple yet effective Reinforcement Fine-Tuning (RFT) strategy for VLA models independent of online environmental feedback and pre-trained reward models. By integrating chunking-level on-policy reinforcement learning with the proposed Multi-Dimensional Process Reward (MDPR) mechanism, LifeLong-RFT quantifies the heterogeneous contributions of intermediate action chunks across three dimensions to facilitate policy optimization. Specifically, (1) the Quantized Action Consistency Reward (QACR) ensures accurate action prediction within the discrete action space; (2) the Continuous Trajectory Alignment Reward (CTAR) aligns decoded continuous action chunks with reference trajectories to ensure precise control; (3) the Format Compliance Reward (FCR) guarantees the structural validity of outputs. Comprehensive experiments across SimplerEnv, LIBERO, and real-world tasks demonstrate that LifeLong-RFT exhibits strong performance in multi-task learning. Furthermore, for continual learning on the LIBERO benchmark, our method achieves a 22% gain in average success rate over SFT, while effectively adapting to new tasks using only 20% of the training data. Overall, our method provides a promising post-training paradigm for VLAs.

摘要（中文）: 大规模多样化数据集上预训练的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型展现出了强大的泛化性和适应性，可作为通用型机器人策略。然而，作为将VLA模型适配到下游领域的主要机制的监督微调（SFT）需要大量的特定任务数据，并且容易发生灾难性遗忘。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了一种简单而有效的强化微调（RFT）策略LifeLong-RFT，用于VLA模型，该策略独立于在线环境反馈和预训练的奖励模型。通过将块级别（chunking-level）的在策略强化学习与我们提出的多维度过程奖励（MDPR）机制相结合，LifeLong-RFT可以量化中间动作块在三个维度上的异构贡献，从而促进策略优化。具体来说，(1) 量化动作一致性奖励（QACR）确保在离散动作空间内准确的动作预测；(2) 连续轨迹对齐奖励（CTAR）将解码的连续动作块与参考轨迹对齐，以确保精准控制；(3) 格式兼容性奖励（FCR）保证输出的结构有效性。在SimplerEnv、LIBERO和真实世界任务上的综合实验表明，LifeLong-RFT在多任务学习中表现出强大的性能。此外，在LIBERO基准上的持续学习中，我们的方法相比于SFT，平均成功率提高了22%，同时仅使用20%的训练数据就能有效地适应新任务。总而言之，我们的方法为VLA模型提供了一种有前景的后训练范式。

TLDR: This paper introduces LifeLong-RFT, a Reinforcement Fine-Tuning strategy for VLA models that overcomes catastrophic forgetting and data inefficiency associated with Supervised Fine-Tuning by using a multi-dimensional process reward mechanism. Experiments show significant improvement in continual learning settings.

简要说明: 本文介绍了LifeLong-RFT，一种用于VLA模型的强化微调策略，通过多维过程奖励机制克服了监督微调相关的灾难性遗忘和数据效率低下的问题。实验表明，该方法在持续学习环境中取得了显著改进。

Authors: Yuan Liu, Haoran Li, Shuai Tian, Yuxing Qin, Yuhui Chen, Yupeng Zheng, Yongzhen Huang, Dongbin Zhao

LocoVLM: Grounding Vision and Language for Adapting Versatile Legged Locomotion Policies

Abstract (English): Recent advances in legged locomotion learning are still dominated by the utilization of geometric representations of the environment, limiting the robot's capability to respond to higher-level semantics such as human instructions. To address this limitation, we propose a novel approach that integrates high-level commonsense reasoning from foundation models into the process of legged locomotion adaptation. Specifically, our method utilizes a pre-trained large language model to synthesize an instruction-grounded skill database tailored for legged robots. A pre-trained vision-language model is employed to extract high-level environmental semantics and ground them within the skill database, enabling real-time skill advisories for the robot. To facilitate versatile skill control, we train a style-conditioned policy capable of generating diverse and robust locomotion skills with high fidelity to specified styles. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first work to demonstrate real-time adaptation of legged locomotion using high-level reasoning from environmental semantics and instructions with instruction-following accuracy of up to 87% without the need for online query to on-the-cloud foundation models.

摘要（中文）: 在足式运动学习方面的最新进展仍然主要依赖于环境的几何表示，这限制了机器人对诸如人类指令等更高层语义的响应能力。为了解决这一局限性，我们提出了一种新颖的方法，将来自基础模型的高层常识推理整合到足式运动适应过程中。具体而言，我们的方法利用预训练的大型语言模型来合成一个针对足式机器人量身定制的、以指令为基础的技能数据库。我们采用预训练的视觉-语言模型来提取高层环境语义，并将它们嵌入到该技能数据库中，从而为机器人实现实时的技能建议。为了促进多功能技能控制，我们训练了一个风格条件策略，该策略能够生成多样且鲁棒的运动技能，并以高保真度匹配指定的风格。据我们所知，这是首个展示如何利用来自环境语义和指令的高层推理，对足式运动进行实时适应的工作，指令遵循准确率高达 87%，且无需在线查询云端基础模型。

TLDR: LocoVLM uses vision-language models to extract environmental semantics and LLMs to create instruction-grounded skill databases, enabling real-time adaptation of legged locomotion policies based on high-level instructions.

Authors: I Made Aswin Nahrendra, Seunghyun Lee, Dongkyu Lee, Hyun Myung

Confounding Robust Continuous Control via Automatic Reward Shaping

Abstract (English): Reward shaping has been applied widely to accelerate Reinforcement Learning (RL) agents' training. However, a principled way of designing effective reward shaping functions, especially for complex continuous control problems, remains largely under-explained. In this work, we propose to automatically learn a reward shaping function for continuous control problems from offline datasets, potentially contaminated by unobserved confounding variables. Specifically, our method builds upon the recently proposed causal Bellman equation to learn a tight upper bound on the optimal state values, which is then used as the potentials in the Potential-Based Reward Shaping (PBRS) framework. Our proposed reward shaping algorithm is tested with Soft-Actor-Critic (SAC) on multiple commonly used continuous control benchmarks and exhibits strong performance guarantees under unobserved confounders. More broadly, our work marks a solid first step towards confounding robust continuous control from a causal perspective. Code for training our reward shaping functions can be found at https://github.com/mateojuliani/confounding_robust_cont_control.

摘要（中文）: 奖励塑造已被广泛应用于加速强化学习 (RL) 智能体的训练。然而，一种设计有效奖励塑造函数的原则性方法，尤其是针对复杂的连续控制问题，仍然很大程度上未得到充分解释。在这项工作中，我们提出从离线数据集中自动学习一个用于连续控制问题的奖励塑造函数，这些数据集可能受到未观察到的混淆变量的污染。具体而言，我们的方法建立在最近提出的因果贝尔曼方程的基础上，以学习最优状态值的紧上限，然后将其用作基于势函数的奖励塑造 (PBRS) 框架中的势函数。我们提出的奖励塑造算法使用软演员-评论家 (SAC) 在多个常用的连续控制基准上进行了测试，并在未观察到的混淆因素下表现出强大的性能保证。更广泛地说，我们的工作标志着朝着从因果角度进行混淆鲁棒的连续控制的坚实第一步。训练我们的奖励塑造函数的代码可在 https://github.com/mateojuliani/confounding_robust_cont_control 找到。

TLDR: This paper proposes a method for automatically learning reward shaping functions for continuous control in reinforcement learning from offline datasets, addressing the challenge of unobserved confounding variables using a causal Bellman equation approach and achieving strong performance on continuous control benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种自动学习连续控制强化学习中奖励塑造函数的方法，该方法从离线数据集中学习，通过因果贝尔曼方程解决未观察到的混淆变量的挑战，并在连续控制基准测试中实现了强大的性能。

Authors: Mateo Juliani, Mingxuan Li, Elias Bareinboim

A Human-in-the-Loop Confidence-Aware Failure Recovery Framework for Modular Robot Policies

Abstract (English): Robots operating in unstructured human environments inevitably encounter failures, especially in robot caregiving scenarios. While humans can often help robots recover, excessive or poorly targeted queries impose unnecessary cognitive and physical workload on the human partner. We present a human-in-the-loop failure-recovery framework for modular robotic policies, where a policy is composed of distinct modules such as perception, planning, and control, any of which may fail and often require different forms of human feedback. Our framework integrates calibrated estimates of module-level uncertainty with models of human intervention cost to decide which module to query and when to query the human. It separates these two decisions: a module selector identifies the module most likely responsible for failure, and a querying algorithm determines whether to solicit human input or act autonomously. We evaluate several module-selection strategies and querying algorithms in controlled synthetic experiments, revealing trade-offs between recovery efficiency, robustness to system and user variables, and user workload. Finally, we deploy the framework on a robot-assisted bite acquisition system and demonstrate, in studies involving individuals with both emulated and real mobility limitations, that it improves recovery success while reducing the workload imposed on users. Our results highlight how explicitly reasoning about both robot uncertainty and human effort can enable more efficient and user-centered failure recovery in collaborative robots. Supplementary materials and videos can be found at: http://emprise.cs.cornell.edu/modularhil

摘要（中文）: 在非结构化的人类环境中运行的机器人不可避免地会遇到故障，尤其是在机器人照护场景中。虽然人类通常可以帮助机器人恢复，但过度或目标性不强的查询会对人类伙伴造成不必要的认知和体力负担。我们提出了一种用于模块化机器人策略的人在环故障恢复框架，其中策略由不同的模块组成，例如感知、规划和控制，这些模块中的任何一个都可能发生故障，并且通常需要不同形式的人工反馈。我们的框架集成了校准后的模块级不确定性估计和人类干预成本模型，以决定查询哪个模块以及何时查询人类。它分离了这两个决策：一个模块选择器识别最有可能导致故障的模块，一个查询算法确定是征求人工输入还是自主行动。我们在受控的合成实验中评估了几种模块选择策略和查询算法，揭示了恢复效率、对系统和用户变量的鲁棒性以及用户工作量之间的权衡。最后，我们将该框架部署在一个机器人辅助咬合获取系统上，并在涉及模拟和真实行动不便个体参与的研究中证明，该框架提高了恢复成功率，同时降低了用户的劳动强度。我们的结果强调，显式地推理机器人不确定性和人类努力可以使协作机器人实现更有效和以用户为中心的故障恢复。补充材料和视频可在以下网址找到：http://emprise.cs.cornell.edu/modularhil

TLDR: This paper presents a human-in-the-loop failure recovery framework for modular robotic policies, integrating robot's uncertainty and human intervention cost to improve recovery success and reduce human workload, validated on a robot-assisted bite acquisition system.

简要说明: 本文提出了一个用于模块化机器人策略的人在环路中的故障恢复框架，该框架结合了机器人的不确定性和人为干预成本，以提高恢复成功率并减少人为工作量，并在机器人辅助的咬合采集系统上进行了验证。

Authors: Rohan Banerjee, Krishna Palempalli, Bohan Yang, Jiaying Fang, Alif Abdullah, Tom Silver, Sarah Dean, Tapomayukh Bhattacharjee

Adaptive Time Step Flow Matching for Autonomous Driving Motion Planning

Abstract (English): Autonomous driving requires reasoning about interactions with surrounding traffic. A prevailing approach is large-scale imitation learning on expert driving datasets, aimed at generalizing across diverse real-world scenarios. For online trajectory generation, such methods must operate at real-time rates. Diffusion models require hundreds of denoising steps at inference, resulting in high latency. Consistency models mitigate this issue but rely on carefully tuned noise schedules to capture the multimodal action distributions common in autonomous driving. Adapting the schedule, typically requires expensive retraining. To address these limitations, we propose a framework based on conditional flow matching that jointly predicts future motions of surrounding agents and plans the ego trajectory in real time. We train a lightweight variance estimator that selects the number of inference steps online, removing the need for retraining to balance runtime and imitation learning performance. To further enhance ride quality, we introduce a trajectory post-processing step cast as a convex quadratic program, with negligible computational overhead. Trained on the Waymo Open Motion Dataset, the framework performs maneuvers such as lane changes, cruise control, and navigating unprotected left turns without requiring scenario-specific tuning. Our method maintains a 20 Hz update rate on an NVIDIA RTX 3070 GPU, making it suitable for online deployment. Compared to transformer, diffusion, and consistency model baselines, we achieve improved trajectory smoothness and better adherence to dynamic constraints. Experiment videos and code implementations can be found at https://flow-matching-self-driving.github.io/.

摘要（中文）: 自动驾驶需要推理与周围交通的交互行为。一种主流方法是在专家驾驶数据集上进行大规模模仿学习，旨在推广到各种真实世界的场景。对于在线轨迹生成，此类方法必须以实时速率运行。扩散模型在推理时需要数百个去噪步骤，导致高延迟。一致性模型缓解了这个问题，但依赖于精心调整的噪声计划来捕捉自动驾驶中常见的多模态动作分布。调整计划通常需要昂贵的重新训练。为了解决这些限制，我们提出了一种基于条件流匹配的框架，该框架可以实时联合预测周围智能体的未来运动并规划自车轨迹。我们训练了一个轻量级的方差估计器，可以在线上选择推理步骤的数量，从而无需重新训练即可平衡运行时间和模仿学习性能。为了进一步提高乘坐舒适性，我们引入了一个轨迹后处理步骤，将其建模为一个凸二次规划问题，且计算开销可忽略不计。该框架在 Waymo Open Motion Dataset 上训练，可以执行诸如变道、巡航控制以及导航无保护左转等操作，而无需针对特定场景进行调整。我们的方法在 NVIDIA RTX 3070 GPU 上保持 20 Hz 的更新速率，使其适合在线部署。与 Transformer、扩散模型和一致性模型基线相比，我们实现了更好的轨迹平滑度和对动态约束的更好遵守。实验视频和代码实现可在 https://flow-matching-self-driving.github.io/ 找到。

TLDR: This paper introduces an adaptive time step flow matching framework for autonomous driving motion planning that achieves real-time performance by jointly predicting agent motions and planning ego trajectories, offering improved smoothness and constraint adherence compared to existing methods.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种自适应时间步长的流匹配框架，用于自动驾驶运动规划，通过联合预测智能体运动和规划自我轨迹，实现了实时性能，并相比现有方法提供了更好的平滑度和约束依从性。

Authors: Ananya Trivedi, Anjian Li, Mohamed Elnoor, Yusuf Umut Ciftci, Avinash Singh, Jovin D'sa, Sangjae Bae, David Isele, Taskin Padir, Faizan M. Tariq

Robo3R: Enhancing Robotic Manipulation with Accurate Feed-Forward 3D Reconstruction

Abstract (English): 3D spatial perception is fundamental to generalizable robotic manipulation, yet obtaining reliable, high-quality 3D geometry remains challenging. Depth sensors suffer from noise and material sensitivity, while existing reconstruction models lack the precision and metric consistency required for physical interaction. We introduce Robo3R, a feed-forward, manipulation-ready 3D reconstruction model that predicts accurate, metric-scale scene geometry directly from RGB images and robot states in real time. Robo3R jointly infers scale-invariant local geometry and relative camera poses, which are unified into the scene representation in the canonical robot frame via a learned global similarity transformation. To meet the precision demands of manipulation, Robo3R employs a masked point head for sharp, fine-grained point clouds, and a keypoint-based Perspective-n-Point (PnP) formulation to refine camera extrinsics and global alignment. Trained on Robo3R-4M, a curated large-scale synthetic dataset with four million high-fidelity annotated frames, Robo3R consistently outperforms state-of-the-art reconstruction methods and depth sensors. Across downstream tasks including imitation learning, sim-to-real transfer, grasp synthesis, and collision-free motion planning, we observe consistent gains in performance, suggesting the promise of this alternative 3D sensing module for robotic manipulation.

摘要（中文）: 3D空间感知是实现通用机器人操作的基础，但获得可靠、高质量的3D几何信息仍然面临挑战。深度传感器存在噪声和对材料敏感的问题，而现有的重建模型缺乏物理交互所需的精度和度量一致性。我们提出了Robo3R，一种前馈的、可直接应用于操作的3D重建模型，可以从RGB图像和机器人状态实时预测精确、度量尺度的场景几何信息。Robo3R联合推断尺度不变的局部几何信息和相对相机姿态，并通过学习到的全局相似变换将其统一到规范机器人坐标系中的场景表示中。为了满足操作的精度要求，Robo3R采用掩码点头生成清晰、细粒度的点云，并采用基于关键点的透视N点(PnP)公式来优化相机外参和全局对齐。Robo3R在Robo3R-4M数据集上进行了训练，该数据集是一个精心策划的大规模合成数据集，包含400万个高保真度注释帧，Robo3R始终优于最先进的重建方法和深度传感器。在包括模仿学习、模拟到真实迁移、抓取合成和无碰撞运动规划等下游任务中，我们观察到性能的持续提升，这表明这种替代的3D感知模块在机器人操作领域具有良好的前景。

TLDR: Robo3R is a feed-forward 3D reconstruction model that leverages RGB images and robot states to predict accurate metric-scale scene geometry for robotic manipulation, outperforming existing methods in downstream tasks like imitation learning and sim-to-real transfer.

简要说明: Robo3R是一个前馈3D重建模型，它利用RGB图像和机器人状态来预测精确的度量尺度场景几何，用于机器人操作。在模仿学习和sim-to-real迁移等下游任务中，Robo3R的性能优于现有方法。

Authors: Sizhe Yang, Linning Xu, Hao Li, Juncheng Mu, Jia Zeng, Dahua Lin, Jiangmiao Pang

UniVTAC: A Unified Simulation Platform for Visuo-Tactile Manipulation Data Generation, Learning, and Benchmarking

Abstract (English): Robotic manipulation has seen rapid progress with vision-language-action (VLA) policies. However, visuo-tactile perception is critical for contact-rich manipulation, as tasks such as insertion are difficult to complete robustly using vision alone. At the same time, acquiring large-scale and reliable tactile data in the physical world remains costly and challenging, and the lack of a unified evaluation platform further limits policy learning and systematic analysis. To address these challenges, we propose UniVTAC, a simulation-based visuo-tactile data synthesis platform that supports three commonly used visuo-tactile sensors and enables scalable and controllable generation of informative contact interactions. Based on this platform, we introduce the UniVTAC Encoder, a visuo-tactile encoder trained on large-scale simulation-synthesized data with designed supervisory signals, providing tactile-centric visuo-tactile representations for downstream manipulation tasks. In addition, we present the UniVTAC Benchmark, which consists of eight representative visuo-tactile manipulation tasks for evaluating tactile-driven policies. Experimental results show that integrating the UniVTAC Encoder improves average success rates by 17.1% on the UniVTAC Benchmark, while real-world robotic experiments further demonstrate a 25% improvement in task success. Our webpage is available at https://univtac.github.io/.

摘要（中文）: 机器人操作在视觉-语言-动作 (VLA) 策略上取得了快速进展。然而，视觉-触觉感知对于富接触操作至关重要，因为诸如插入之类的任务仅依靠视觉很难稳健地完成。同时，在物理世界中获取大规模且可靠的触觉数据仍然成本高昂且具有挑战性，缺乏统一的评估平台进一步限制了策略学习和系统分析。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了 UniVTAC，一个基于仿真的视觉-触觉数据合成平台，它支持三种常用的视觉-触觉传感器，并能够可扩展地、可控地生成信息丰富的接触交互。基于该平台，我们引入了 UniVTAC 编码器，一个在设计监督信号的大规模仿真合成数据上训练的视觉-触觉编码器，为下游操作任务提供以触觉为中心的视觉-触觉表示。此外，我们提出了 UniVTAC 基准测试，它由八个具有代表性的视觉-触觉操作任务组成，用于评估触觉驱动的策略。实验结果表明，集成 UniVTAC 编码器在 UniVTAC 基准测试上平均成功率提高了 17.1%，而真实世界的机器人实验进一步证明了任务成功率提高了 25%。我们的网页地址是 https://univtac.github.io/。

TLDR: The paper introduces UniVTAC, a simulation platform for visuo-tactile manipulation, along with a pre-trained encoder, and a benchmark, demonstrating improved performance in both simulation and real-world robotic tasks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了 UniVTAC，一个用于视觉触觉操作的仿真平台，以及一个预训练的编码器和一个基准测试，展示了在仿真和现实世界机器人任务中性能的提升。

Authors: Baijun Chen, Weijie Wan, Tianxing Chen, Xianda Guo, Congsheng Xu, Yuanyang Qi, Haojie Zhang, Longyan Wu, Tianling Xu, Zixuan Li, Yizhe Wu, Rui Li, Xiaokang Yang, Ping Luo, Wei Sui, Yao Mu

Chatting with Images for Introspective Visual Thinking

Abstract (English): Current large vision-language models (LVLMs) typically rely on text-only reasoning based on a single-pass visual encoding, which often leads to loss of fine-grained visual information. Recently the proposal of ''thinking with images'' attempts to alleviate this limitation by manipulating images via external tools or code; however, the resulting visual states are often insufficiently grounded in linguistic semantics, impairing effective cross-modal alignment - particularly when visual semantics or geometric relationships must be reasoned over across distant regions or multiple images. To address these challenges, we propose ''chatting with images'', a new framework that reframes visual manipulation as language-guided feature modulation. Under the guidance of expressive language prompts, the model dynamically performs joint re-encoding over multiple image regions, enabling tighter coupling between linguistic reasoning and visual state updates. We instantiate this paradigm in ViLaVT, a novel LVLM equipped with a dynamic vision encoder explicitly designed for such interactive visual reasoning, and trained it with a two-stage curriculum combining supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning to promote effective reasoning behaviors. Extensive experiments across eight benchmarks demonstrate that ViLaVT achieves strong and consistent improvements, with particularly pronounced gains on complex multi-image and video-based spatial reasoning tasks.

摘要（中文）: 当前大型视觉-语言模型（LVLMs）通常依赖于基于单次视觉编码的纯文本推理，这常常导致细粒度视觉信息的丢失。最近提出的“用图像思考”尝试通过外部工具或代码来操作图像，以缓解这一局限；然而，由此产生的视觉状态往往在语言语义上的扎根不足，从而损害了有效的跨模态对齐——尤其是在必须跨越遥远区域或多个图像进行视觉语义或几何关系推理时。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了“与图像聊天”，一种将视觉操作重构为语言引导的特征调制的全新框架。在富有表达性的语言提示的指导下，模型动态地对多个图像区域执行联合重新编码，从而实现语言推理和视觉状态更新之间更紧密的耦合。我们将这一范式实例化到ViLaVT中，这是一种配备了专为这种交互式视觉推理设计的动态视觉编码器的新型LVLM，并利用结合了监督微调和强化学习的两阶段课程对其进行训练，以促进有效的推理行为。在八个基准测试中进行的大量实验表明，ViLaVT取得了强大且一致的改进，尤其是在复杂的多图像和基于视频的空间推理任务上获得了显著提升。

TLDR: The paper introduces ViLaVT, a novel LVLM framework that uses language-guided feature modulation for improved visual reasoning and cross-modal alignment, achieving better performance on multi-image and video-based spatial reasoning tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种新型的 LVLM 框架 ViLaVT，它使用语言引导的特征调制来改进视觉推理和跨模态对齐，从而在多图像和基于视频的空间推理任务中取得更好的性能。
