Authors: Junfei Wu, Jian Guan, Qiang Liu, Shu Wu, Liang Wang, Wei Wu, Tieniu Tan

FeatureBench: Benchmarking Agentic Coding for Complex Feature Development

Abstract (English): Agents powered by large language models (LLMs) are increasingly adopted in the software industry, contributing code as collaborators or even autonomous developers. As their presence grows, it becomes important to assess the current boundaries of their coding abilities. Existing agentic coding benchmarks, however, cover a limited task scope, e.g., bug fixing within a single pull request (PR), and often rely on non-executable evaluations or lack an automated approach for continually updating the evaluation coverage. To address such issues, we propose FeatureBench, a benchmark designed to evaluate agentic coding performance in end-to-end, feature-oriented software development. FeatureBench incorporates an execution-based evaluation protocol and a scalable test-driven method that automatically derives tasks from code repositories with minimal human effort. By tracing from unit tests along a dependency graph, our approach can identify feature-level coding tasks spanning multiple commits and PRs scattered across the development timeline, while ensuring the proper functioning of other features after the separation. Using this framework, we curated 200 challenging evaluation tasks and 3825 executable environments from 24 open-source repositories in the first version of our benchmark. Empirical evaluation reveals that the state-of-the-art agentic model, such as Claude 4.5 Opus, which achieves a 74.4% resolved rate on SWE-bench, succeeds on only 11.0% of tasks, opening new opportunities for advancing agentic coding. Moreover, benefiting from our automated task collection toolkit, FeatureBench can be easily scaled and updated over time to mitigate data leakage. The inherent verifiability of constructed environments also makes our method potentially valuable for agent training.

摘要（中文）: 由大型语言模型 (LLM) 驱动的智能体在软件行业中日益普及，它们以协作者的身份甚至作为自主开发者参与代码贡献。随着它们的出现频率增加，评估其当前编码能力的边界变得至关重要。然而，现有的基于智能体的编码基准测试覆盖的任务范围有限，例如，仅关注单个拉取请求 (PR) 中的错误修复，并且通常依赖于不可执行的评估方法，或者缺乏一种可自动更新评估覆盖率的方法。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了 FeatureBench，一个旨在评估基于智能体的编码在端到端、以特性为导向的软件开发中的性能的基准测试。FeatureBench 结合了基于执行的评估协议和可扩展的测试驱动方法，该方法能够以最小的人工干预，从代码仓库中自动派生任务。通过沿着依赖关系图追踪单元测试，我们的方法可以识别跨越多个提交和 PR、分散在开发时间轴上的特性级编码任务，同时确保分离后其他特性的正常运行。利用该框架，我们在基准测试的第一个版本中整理了来自 24 个开源仓库的 200 个具有挑战性的评估任务和 3825 个可执行环境。实证评估表明，最先进的基于智能体的模型，例如 Claude 4.5 Opus，虽然在 SWE-bench 上达到了 74.4% 的解决率，但在我们的任务中仅成功解决了 11.0% 的任务，这为推进基于智能体的编码提供了新的机会。此外，受益于我们的自动化任务收集工具包，FeatureBench 可以随着时间的推移轻松扩展和更新，以减轻数据泄露。构建环境固有的可验证性也使我们的方法对智能体训练具有潜在价值。

TLDR: The paper introduces FeatureBench, a new benchmark for evaluating agentic coding performance in end-to-end feature development, highlighting limitations of current LLM agents on complex tasks and offering a scalable, automated approach to task generation.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了FeatureBench，一个新的用于评估端到端特性开发中智能体编码性能的基准，突出了当前LLM智能体在复杂任务上的局限性，并提供了一种可扩展的、自动化的任务生成方法。

Authors: Qixing Zhou, Jiacheng Zhang, Haiyang Wang, Rui Hao, Jiahe Wang, Minghao Han, Yuxue Yang, Shuzhe Wu, Feiyang Pan, Lue Fan, Dandan Tu, Zhaoxiang Zhang

Blind Gods and Broken Screens: Architecting a Secure, Intent-Centric Mobile Agent Operating System

Abstract (English): The evolution of Large Language Models (LLMs) has shifted mobile computing from App-centric interactions to system-level autonomous agents. Current implementations predominantly rely on a "Screen-as-Interface" paradigm, which inherits structural vulnerabilities and conflicts with the mobile ecosystem's economic foundations. In this paper, we conduct a systematic security analysis of state-of-the-art mobile agents using Doubao Mobile Assistant as a representative case. We decompose the threat landscape into four dimensions - Agent Identity, External Interface, Internal Reasoning, and Action Execution - revealing critical flaws such as fake App identity, visual spoofing, indirect prompt injection, and unauthorized privilege escalation stemming from a reliance on unstructured visual data. To address these challenges, we propose Aura, an Agent Universal Runtime Architecture for a clean-slate secure agent OS. Aura replaces brittle GUI scraping with a structured, agent-native interaction model. It adopts a Hub-and-Spoke topology where a privileged System Agent orchestrates intent, sandboxed App Agents execute domain-specific tasks, and the Agent Kernel mediates all communication. The Agent Kernel enforces four defense pillars: (i) cryptographic identity binding via a Global Agent Registry; (ii) semantic input sanitization through a multilayer Semantic Firewall; (iii) cognitive integrity via taint-aware memory and plan-trajectory alignment; and (iv) granular access control with non-deniable auditing. Evaluation on MobileSafetyBench shows that, compared to Doubao, Aura improves low-risk Task Success Rate from roughly 75% to 94.3%, reduces high-risk Attack Success Rate from roughly 40% to 4.4%, and achieves near-order-of-magnitude latency gains. These results demonstrate Aura as a viable, secure alternative to the "Screen-as-Interface" paradigm.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLMs）的演进已将移动计算从以应用为中心的交互转变为系统级的自主代理。当前的实现主要依赖于“屏幕即接口”范式，该范式继承了结构性漏洞，并与移动生态系统的经济基础产生冲突。在本文中，我们以豆包移动助手为代表案例，对目前最先进的移动代理进行了系统的安全分析。我们将威胁态势分解为代理身份、外部接口、内部推理和动作执行四个维度，揭示了关键缺陷，例如虚假应用身份、视觉欺骗、间接提示注入以及源于对非结构化视觉数据依赖的未经授权的权限提升。 为应对这些挑战，我们提出了Aura，一种用于全新安全代理操作系统的代理通用运行时架构。Aura 用结构化的、代理原生交互模型取代了脆弱的GUI抓取。它采用中心辐射型拓扑结构，其中特权系统代理协调意图，沙箱化的应用代理执行特定领域的任务，代理内核调解所有通信。代理内核强制执行四个防御支柱：（i）通过全局代理注册表进行加密身份绑定；（ii）通过多层语义防火墙进行语义输入清理；（iii）通过污点感知的内存和计划轨迹对齐实现认知完整性；（iv）通过不可否认的审计实现细粒度的访问控制。在MobileSafetyBench上的评估表明，与豆包相比，Aura将低风险任务成功率从大约75%提高到94.3%，将高风险攻击成功率从大约40%降低到4.4%，并实现了接近数量级的延迟增益。这些结果表明，Aura是“屏幕即接口”范式的一个可行且安全的替代方案。

TLDR: The paper proposes Aura, a secure agent operating system to address vulnerabilities of current mobile agents that rely on screen scraping, presenting a new architecture with improved security and performance.

简要说明: 该论文提出了Aura，一个安全的代理操作系统，旨在解决当前依赖屏幕抓取的移动代理的漏洞，并提出了一种具有改进的安全性和性能的新架构。

Authors: Zhenhua Zou, Sheng Guo, Qiuyang Zhan, Lepeng Zhao, Shuo Li, Qi Li, Ke Xu, Mingwei Xu, Zhuotao Liu

Interactive LLM-assisted Curriculum Learning for Multi-Task Evolutionary Policy Search

Abstract (English): Multi-task policy search is a challenging problem because policies are required to generalize beyond training cases. Curriculum learning has proven to be effective in this setting, as it introduces complexity progressively. However, designing effective curricula is labor-intensive and requires extensive domain expertise. LLM-based curriculum generation has only recently emerged as a potential solution, but was limited to operate in static, offline modes without leveraging real-time feedback from the optimizer. Here we propose an interactive LLM-assisted framework for online curriculum generation, where the LLM adaptively designs training cases based on real-time feedback from the evolutionary optimization process. We investigate how different feedback modalities, ranging from numeric metrics alone to combinations with plots and behavior visualizations, influence the LLM ability to generate meaningful curricula. Through a 2D robot navigation case study, tackled with genetic programming as optimizer, we evaluate our approach against static LLM-generated curricula and expert-designed baselines. We show that interactive curriculum generation outperforms static approaches, with multimodal feedback incorporating both progression plots and behavior visualizations yielding performance competitive with expert-designed curricula. This work contributes to understanding how LLMs can serve as interactive curriculum designers for embodied AI systems, with potential extensions to broader evolutionary robotics applications.

摘要（中文）: 多任务策略搜索是一个具有挑战性的问题，因为策略需要泛化到训练案例之外。课程学习已被证明在这种情况下是有效的，因为它逐步引入复杂性。然而，设计有效的课程是劳动密集型的，并且需要广泛的领域专业知识。基于LLM的课程生成最近才作为一种潜在的解决方案出现，但仅限于静态、离线模式运行，而没有利用来自优化器的实时反馈。在这里，我们提出了一种交互式的、LLM辅助的在线课程生成框架，其中LLM根据进化优化过程中的实时反馈自适应地设计训练案例。我们研究了不同的反馈模式，从仅使用数字指标到与图表和行为可视化相结合，如何影响LLM生成有意义课程的能力。通过一个2D机器人导航案例研究，使用遗传编程作为优化器，我们针对静态的LLM生成课程和专家设计的基线评估了我们的方法。我们表明，交互式课程生成优于静态方法，其中包含进度图和行为可视化的多模态反馈产生了与专家设计的课程具有竞争力的性能。这项工作有助于理解LLM如何作为具身AI系统的交互式课程设计师，并具有扩展到更广泛的进化机器人应用的潜力。

TLDR: This paper proposes an interactive LLM-assisted curriculum learning framework for multi-task evolutionary policy search in embodied AI, demonstrating that real-time feedback (especially multimodal) to the LLM can generate curricula competitive with expert-designed ones.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种交互式的LLM辅助课程学习框架，用于具身人工智能中的多任务进化策略搜索。实验表明，向LLM提供实时反馈（特别是多模态反馈）可以生成与专家设计的课程相媲美的课程。

Authors: Berfin Sakallioglu, Giorgia Nadizar, Eric Medvet

ICA: Information-Aware Credit Assignment for Visually Grounded Long-Horizon Information-Seeking Agents

Abstract (English): Despite the strong performance achieved by reinforcement learning-trained information-seeking agents, learning in open-ended web environments remains severely constrained by low signal-to-noise feedback. Text-based parsers often discard layout semantics and introduce unstructured noise, while long-horizon training typically relies on sparse outcome rewards that obscure which retrieval actions actually matter. We propose a visual-native search framework that represents webpages as visual snapshots, allowing agents to leverage layout cues to quickly localize salient evidence and suppress distractors. To learn effectively from these high-dimensional observations, we introduce Information-Aware Credit Assignment (ICA), a post-hoc method that estimates each retrieved snapshot's contribution to the final outcome via posterior analysis and propagates dense learning signals back to key search turns. Integrated with a GRPO-based training pipeline, our approach consistently outperforms text-based baselines on diverse information-seeking benchmarks, providing evidence that visual snapshot grounding with information-level credit assignment alleviates the credit-assignment bottleneck in open-ended web environments. The code and datasets will be released in https://github.com/pc-inno/ICA_MM_deepsearch.git.

摘要（中文）: 尽管强化学习训练的信息检索代理取得了显著的性能，但在开放式网络环境中学习仍然受到低信噪比反馈的严重制约。基于文本的解析器通常会丢弃布局语义并引入非结构化噪声，而长程训练通常依赖于稀疏的结果奖励，这掩盖了哪些检索行为真正重要。我们提出了一种视觉原生搜索框架，该框架将网页表示为视觉快照，使代理能够利用布局线索快速定位显著证据并抑制干扰。为了从这些高维观测中有效地学习，我们引入了信息感知信用分配 (ICA)，这是一种后验方法，通过后验分析估计每个检索快照对最终结果的贡献，并将密集的学习信号传播回关键搜索回合。与基于 GRPO 的训练流程集成后，我们的方法在各种信息检索基准测试中始终优于基于文本的基线，这证明了带有信息级别信用分配的视觉快照接地可以缓解开放式网络环境中的信用分配瓶颈。代码和数据集将在 https://github.com/pc-inno/ICA_MM_deepsearch.git 上发布。

TLDR: This paper introduces Information-Aware Credit Assignment (ICA) for visually grounded information-seeking agents, enabling them to effectively learn in open-ended web environments by leveraging visual layout cues and dense reward signals. It outperforms text-based baselines.

简要说明: 本文介绍了信息感知信用分配 (ICA)，用于视觉接地的寻信智能体，通过利用视觉布局线索和密集奖励信号，使其能够在开放式网络环境中有效学习。结果表明ICA方案优于基于文本的基线。

Authors: Cong Pang, Xuyu Feng, Yujie Yi, Zixuan Chen, Jiawei Hong, Tiankuo Yao, Nang Yuan, Jiapeng Luo, Lewei Lu, Xin Lou

VESPO: Variational Sequence-Level Soft Policy Optimization for Stable Off-Policy LLM Training

Abstract (English): Training stability remains a central challenge in reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models (LLMs). Policy staleness, asynchronous training, and mismatches between training and inference engines all cause the behavior policy to diverge from the current policy, risking training collapse. Importance sampling provides a principled correction for this distribution shift but suffers from high variance; existing remedies such as token-level clipping and sequence-level normalization lack a unified theoretical foundation. We propose Variational sEquence-level Soft Policy Optimization (VESPO). By incorporating variance reduction into a variational formulation over proposal distributions, VESPO derives a closed-form reshaping kernel that operates directly on sequence-level importance weights without length normalization. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that VESPO maintains stable training under staleness ratios up to 64x and fully asynchronous execution, and delivers consistent gains across both dense and Mixture-of-Experts models. Code is available at https://github.com/FloyedShen/VESPO

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLM）强化学习（RL）中的训练稳定性仍然是一个核心挑战。策略陈旧性、异步训练以及训练与推理引擎之间的不匹配，都会导致行为策略与当前策略发散，从而带来训练崩溃的风险。重要性采样为这种分布偏移提供了一个原则性的修正方法，但其方差较高；现有的解决方案，如 token 级裁剪和序列级规范化，缺乏统一的理论基础。我们提出变分序列级软策略优化（VESPO）。通过将方差缩减纳入提案分布的变分公式中，VESPO 推导出一个闭式重塑核，可以直接对序列级重要性权重进行操作，无需长度归一化。在数学推理基准测试上的实验表明，VESPO 在高达 64 倍的陈旧率和完全异步执行下，仍能保持训练稳定性，并在稠密模型和混合专家模型上均能提供一致的收益。代码位于：https://github.com/FloyedShen/VESPO

TLDR: The paper introduces VESPO, a novel sequence-level policy optimization method for stable off-policy LLM training using a variational formulation to reduce variance in importance sampling, showing improvements on mathematical reasoning benchmarks with high staleness and asynchronous execution.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了VESPO，一种新的序列级别策略优化方法，用于稳定大型语言模型的离线策略训练。该方法采用变分公式来减少重要性采样的方差，并在数学推理基准测试中展示了在高延迟和异步执行下的改进。

Authors: Guobin Shen, Chenxiao Zhao, Xiang Cheng, Lei Huang, Xing Yu

TwiFF (Think With Future Frames): A Large-Scale Dataset for Dynamic Visual Reasoning

Abstract (English): Visual Chain-of-Thought (VCoT) has emerged as a promising paradigm for enhancing multimodal reasoning by integrating visual perception into intermediate reasoning steps. However, existing VCoT approaches are largely confined to static scenarios and struggle to capture the temporal dynamics essential for tasks such as instruction, prediction, and camera motion. To bridge this gap, we propose TwiFF-2.7M, the first large-scale, temporally grounded VCoT dataset derived from $2.7$ million video clips, explicitly designed for dynamic visual question and answer. Accompanying this, we introduce TwiFF-Bench, a high-quality evaluation benchmark of $1,078$ samples that assesses both the plausibility of reasoning trajectories and the correctness of final answers in open-ended dynamic settings. Building on these foundations, we propose the TwiFF model, a unified modal that synergistically leverages pre-trained video generation and image comprehension capabilities to produce temporally coherent visual reasoning cues-iteratively generating future action frames and textual reasoning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that TwiFF significantly outperforms existing VCoT methods and Textual Chain-of-Thought baselines on dynamic reasoning tasks, which fully validates the effectiveness for visual question answering in dynamic scenarios. Our code and data is available at https://github.com/LiuJunhua02/TwiFF.

摘要（中文）: 视觉思维链 (VCoT) 已经成为一种很有前景的范式，它通过将视觉感知整合到中间推理步骤中来增强多模态推理。然而，现有的 VCoT 方法大多局限于静态场景，难以捕捉指令、预测和相机运动等任务所必需的时序动态。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了 TwiFF-2.7M，这是第一个大规模、时序对齐的 VCoT 数据集，来源于 270 万个视频片段，专门为动态视觉问答而设计。与此同时，我们推出了 TwiFF-Bench，一个包含 1078 个样本的高质量评估基准，用于评估开放式动态环境中推理轨迹的合理性和最终答案的正确性。在此基础上，我们提出了 TwiFF 模型，这是一个统一的模态，它协同利用预训练的视频生成和图像理解能力，生成时序连贯的视觉推理提示——迭代生成未来的动作帧和文本推理。大量实验表明，TwiFF 在动态推理任务上显著优于现有的 VCoT 方法和文本思维链基线，充分验证了其在动态场景中进行视觉问答的有效性。我们的代码和数据可在 https://github.com/LiuJunhua02/TwiFF 获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces TwiFF-2.7M, a large-scale, temporally grounded VCoT dataset for dynamic visual reasoning, along with a benchmark and a novel model (TwiFF) that leverages video generation and image comprehension for enhanced performance in dynamic visual question answering.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了TwiFF-2.7M，一个大规模、时序对齐的VCoT数据集，用于动态视觉推理。同时提出了一个基准和新模型（TwiFF），该模型利用视频生成和图像理解来增强动态视觉问答的性能。

Authors: Junhua Liu, Zhangcheng Wang, Zhike Han, Ningli Wang, Guotao Liang, Kun Kuang

OmniSapiens: A Foundation Model for Social Behavior Processing via Heterogeneity-Aware Relative Policy Optimization

Abstract (English): To develop socially intelligent AI, existing approaches typically model human behavioral dimensions (e.g., affective, cognitive, or social attributes) in isolation. Although useful, task-specific modeling often increases training costs and limits generalization across behavioral settings. Recent reasoning RL methods facilitate training a single unified model across multiple behavioral tasks, but do not explicitly address learning across different heterogeneous behavioral data. To address this gap, we introduce Heterogeneity-Aware Relative Policy Optimization (HARPO), an RL method that balances leaning across heterogeneous tasks and samples. This is achieved by modulating advantages to ensure that no single task or sample carries disproportionate influence during policy optimization. Using HARPO, we develop and release Omnisapiens-7B 2.0, a foundation model for social behavior processing. Relative to existing behavioral foundation models, Omnisapiens-7B 2.0 achieves the strongest performance across behavioral tasks, with gains of up to +16.85% and +9.37% on multitask and held-out settings respectively, while producing more explicit and robust reasoning traces. We also validate HARPO against recent RL methods, where it achieves the most consistently strong performance across behavioral tasks.

摘要（中文）: 为了开发具有社会智能的AI，现有方法通常孤立地对人类行为维度（例如，情感、认知或社会属性）进行建模。尽管这些方法很有用，但特定于任务的建模往往会增加训练成本，并限制在不同行为环境中的泛化能力。最近的推理强化学习（RL）方法促进了跨多个行为任务的单一统一模型的训练，但没有明确解决跨不同异构行为数据的学习问题。为了弥补这一差距，我们引入了异构感知相对策略优化（HARPO），这是一种RL方法，它平衡跨异构任务和样本的学习。这通过调节优势函数来实现，以确保没有单个任务或样本在策略优化过程中产生不成比例的影响。使用HARPO，我们开发并发布了Omnisapiens-7B 2.0，一个用于社会行为处理的基础模型。相对于现有的行为基础模型，Omnisapiens-7B 2.0在各种行为任务中取得了最强的性能，在多任务和预留设置中分别获得了高达+16.85%和+9.37%的收益，同时产生了更明确和更稳健的推理轨迹。我们还针对最近的RL方法验证了HARPO，结果表明它在各种行为任务中都取得了最稳定和最强的性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces Heterogeneity-Aware Relative Policy Optimization (HARPO), an RL method for training a social behavior processing foundation model, Omnisapiens-7B 2.0, achieving state-of-the-art performance across various behavioral tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了异质性感知相对策略优化（HARPO），一种用于训练社会行为处理基础模型的强化学习方法，Omnisapiens-7B 2.0，在各种行为任务中实现了最先进的性能。

Authors: Keane Ong, Sabri Boughorbel, Luwei Xiao, Chanakya Ekbote, Wei Dai, Ao Qu, Jingyao Wu, Rui Mao, Ehsan Hoque, Erik Cambria, Gianmarco Mengaldo, Paul Pu Liang

Neuro-symbolic Action Masking for Deep Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Deep reinforcement learning (DRL) may explore infeasible actions during training and execution. Existing approaches assume a symbol grounding function that maps high-dimensional states to consistent symbolic representations and a manually specified action masking techniques to constrain actions. In this paper, we propose Neuro-symbolic Action Masking (NSAM), a novel framework that automatically learn symbolic models, which are consistent with given domain constraints of high-dimensional states, in a minimally supervised manner during the DRL process. Based on the learned symbolic model of states, NSAM learns action masks that rules out infeasible actions. NSAM enables end-to-end integration of symbolic reasoning and deep policy optimization, where improvements in symbolic grounding and policy learning mutually reinforce each other. We evaluate NSAM on multiple domains with constraints, and experimental results demonstrate that NSAM significantly improves sample efficiency of DRL agent while substantially reducing constraint violations.

摘要（中文）: 深度强化学习（DRL）在训练和执行过程中可能会探索不可行的动作。现有方法通常假设存在一个符号接地函数，该函数将高维状态映射到一致的符号表示，并依赖于手动指定的动作掩码技术来约束动作。在本文中，我们提出了一种神经符号动作掩码（NSAM）框架，该框架能够在DRL过程中，以最小监督的方式自动学习符号模型，该模型与高维状态的给定领域约束保持一致。基于学习到的状态符号模型，NSAM学习动作掩码来排除不可行的动作。NSAM实现了符号推理和深度策略优化的端到端集成，其中符号接地的改进和策略学习相互增强。我们在多个具有约束的领域中评估了NSAM，实验结果表明，NSAM显著提高了DRL代理的样本效率，同时大幅减少了约束违反。

TLDR: The paper introduces Neuro-symbolic Action Masking (NSAM), a framework that automatically learns symbolic models from high-dimensional states to create action masks, improving sample efficiency and reducing constraint violations in DRL.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了神经符号动作掩码（NSAM），该框架自动从高维状态中学习符号模型以创建动作掩码，从而提高 DRL 中的样本效率并减少约束违规。

Authors: Shuai Han, Mehdi Dastani, Shihan Wang

LLM-Based Scientific Equation Discovery via Physics-Informed Token-Regularized Policy Optimization

Abstract (English): Symbolic regression aims to distill mathematical equations from observational data. Recent approaches have successfully leveraged Large Language Models (LLMs) to generate equation hypotheses, capitalizing on their vast pre-trained scientific priors. However, existing frameworks predominantly treat the LLM as a static generator, relying on prompt-level guidance to steer exploration. This paradigm fails to update the model's internal representations based on search feedback, often yielding physically inconsistent or mathematically redundant expressions. In this work, we propose PiT-PO (Physics-informed Token-regularized Policy Optimization), a unified framework that evolves the LLM into an adaptive generator via reinforcement learning. Central to PiT-PO is a dual-constraint mechanism that rigorously enforces hierarchical physical validity while simultaneously applying fine-grained, token-level penalties to suppress redundant structures. Consequently, PiT-PO aligns LLM to produce equations that are both scientifically consistent and structurally parsimonious. Empirically, PiT-PO achieves state-of-the-art performance on standard benchmarks and successfully discovers novel turbulence models for challenging fluid dynamics problems. We also demonstrate that PiT-PO empowers small-scale models to outperform closed-source giants, democratizing access to high-performance scientific discovery.

摘要（中文）: 符号回归旨在从观测数据中提炼数学方程。最近的方法成功地利用大型语言模型 (LLM) 生成方程假设，并充分利用其预训练的大量科学先验知识。然而，现有的框架主要将 LLM 视为静态生成器，依靠提示级别的指导来引导探索。这种范式无法基于搜索反馈更新模型的内部表示，经常产生物理上不一致或数学上冗余的表达式。在这项工作中，我们提出 PiT-PO（物理信息令牌正则化策略优化），这是一个统一的框架，通过强化学习将 LLM 演化为自适应生成器。 PiT-PO 的核心是双重约束机制，该机制严格地执行分层物理有效性，同时应用细粒度的代币级别惩罚来抑制冗余结构。因此，PiT-PO 使 LLM 能够产生在科学上一致且结构上简约的方程。在标准基准测试中，PiT-PO 在经验上实现了最先进的性能，并成功地为具有挑战性的流体动力学问题发现了新的湍流模型。我们还证明了 PiT-PO 使小型模型能够胜过闭源大型模型，从而普及了对高性能科学发现的访问。

TLDR: The paper introduces PiT-PO, a reinforcement learning framework that fine-tunes LLMs for scientific equation discovery by enforcing physical validity and suppressing redundant structures, achieving state-of-the-art performance and discovering novel turbulence models.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为PiT-PO的强化学习框架，该框架通过强化物理有效性并抑制冗余结构来微调LLM，以用于科学方程发现，从而实现了最先进的性能并发现了新的湍流模型。

Authors: Boxiao Wang, Kai Li, Tianyi Liu, Chen Li, Junzhe Wang, Yifan Zhang, Jian Cheng

MetaphorStar: Image Metaphor Understanding and Reasoning with End-to-End Visual Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Metaphorical comprehension in images remains a critical challenge for Nowadays AI systems. While Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) excel at basic Visual Question Answering (VQA), they consistently struggle to grasp the nuanced cultural, emotional, and contextual implications embedded in visual content. This difficulty stems from the task's demand for sophisticated multi-hop reasoning, cultural context, and Theory of Mind (ToM) capabilities, which current models lack. To fill this gap, we propose MetaphorStar, the first end-to-end visual reinforcement learning (RL) framework for image implication tasks. Our framework includes three core components: the fine-grained dataset TFQ-Data, the visual RL method TFQ-GRPO, and the well-structured benchmark TFQ-Bench. Our fully open-source MetaphorStar family, trained using TFQ-GRPO on TFQ-Data, significantly improves performance by an average of 82.6% on the image implication benchmarks. Compared with 20+ mainstream MLLMs, MetaphorStar-32B achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) on Multiple-Choice Question and Open-Style Question, significantly outperforms the top closed-source model Gemini-3.0-pro on True-False Question. Crucially, our experiments reveal that learning image implication tasks improves the general understanding ability, especially the complex visual reasoning ability. We further provide a systematic analysis of model parameter scaling, training data scaling, and the impact of different model architectures and training strategies, demonstrating the broad applicability of our method. We open-sourced all model weights, datasets, and method code at https://metaphorstar.github.io.

摘要（中文）: 图像中的隐喻理解仍然是当前人工智能系统面临的一个关键挑战。尽管多模态大型语言模型(MLLMs)在基础视觉问答(VQA)方面表现出色，但它们始终难以掌握视觉内容中蕴含的微妙的文化、情感和语境含义。这种困难源于该任务需要复杂的多步推理、文化背景知识和心理理论(ToM)能力，而当前的模型缺乏这些能力。为了弥补这一差距，我们提出了MetaphorStar，它是首个用于图像隐喻任务的端到端视觉强化学习(RL)框架。我们的框架包括三个核心组成部分：细粒度数据集TFQ-Data、视觉强化学习方法TFQ-GRPO，以及结构良好的基准测试TFQ-Bench。 我们的完全开源MetaphorStar系列，使用TFQ-GRPO在TFQ-Data上进行训练，在图像隐喻基准测试上平均提高了82.6%的性能。与20多个主流MLLM相比，MetaphorStar-32B在多项选择题和开放式问题上实现了最先进(SOTA)的性能，并在判断题上显著优于顶级的闭源模型Gemini-3.0-pro。至关重要的是，我们的实验表明，学习图像隐喻任务能提高通用理解能力，尤其是复杂的视觉推理能力。我们进一步提供了模型参数规模、训练数据规模以及不同模型架构和训练策略影响的系统分析，证明了我们方法的广泛适用性。我们已在https://metaphorstar.github.io开源了所有模型权重、数据集和方法代码。

TLDR: The paper introduces MetaphorStar, an end-to-end visual reinforcement learning framework for image metaphor understanding, featuring a dataset, RL method, and benchmark, achieving state-of-the-art results compared to MLLMs and improving general visual reasoning ability.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了MetaphorStar，一个端到端的视觉强化学习框架，用于图像隐喻理解。它包含数据集、强化学习方法和基准，并在与多模态大型语言模型相比取得了最先进的结果，并提高了通用视觉推理能力。

Authors: Chenhao Zhang, Yazhe Niu, Hongsheng Li

LHAW: Controllable Underspecification for Long-Horizon Tasks

Abstract (English): Long-horizon workflow agents that operate effectively over extended periods are essential for truly autonomous systems. Their reliable execution critically depends on the ability to reason through ambiguous situations in which clarification seeking is necessary to ensure correct task execution. However, progress is limited by the lack of scalable, task-agnostic frameworks for systematically curating and measuring the impact of ambiguity across custom workflows. We address this gap by introducing LHAW (Long-Horizon Augmented Workflows), a modular, dataset-agnostic synthetic pipeline that transforms any well-specified task into controllable underspecified variants by systematically removing information across four dimensions - Goals, Constraints, Inputs, and Context - at configurable severity levels. Unlike approaches that rely on LLM predictions of ambiguity, LHAW validates variants through empirical agent trials, classifying them as outcome-critical, divergent, or benign based on observed terminal state divergence. We release 285 task variants from TheAgentCompany, SWE-Bench Pro and MCP-Atlas according to our taxonomy alongside formal analysis measuring how current agents detect, reason about, and resolve underspecification across ambiguous settings. LHAW provides the first systematic framework for cost-sensitive evaluation of agent clarification behavior in long-horizon settings, enabling development of reliable autonomous systems.

摘要（中文）: 为实现真正自主的系统，长时间跨度工作流agent在扩展的时间周期内有效运作至关重要。它们可靠的执行严重依赖于在模糊情境中进行推理的能力，其中寻求澄清对于确保正确的任务执行是必要的。然而，由于缺乏可扩展的、任务无关的框架来系统地管理和衡量模糊性对自定义工作流的影响，进展受到了限制。我们通过引入LHAW（长时程增强工作流）来解决这一差距，LHAW是一个模块化的、数据集无关的合成流水线，它通过在四个维度——目标、约束、输入和上下文——以可配置的严重程度系统地删除信息，将任何明确指定的任务转换为可控的不完全指定变体。与依赖于LLM预测模糊性的方法不同，LHAW通过经验性的agent试验来验证变体，根据观察到的终态差异将它们分类为结果关键型、发散型或良性。我们根据我们的分类法发布了来自TheAgentCompany、SWE-Bench Pro和MCP-Atlas的285个任务变体，并进行了正式分析，以衡量当前agent如何在模糊环境中检测、推理和解决不完全指定问题。LHAW提供了第一个系统性的框架，用于在长时间跨度环境中对agent澄清行为进行成本敏感型评估，从而实现可靠的自主系统的开发。

TLDR: The paper introduces LHAW, a framework for generating controllable underspecified task variants to evaluate the reliability of long-horizon agents in ambiguous situations, enabling systematic benchmarking of clarification behavior.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了LHAW，一个用于生成可控的不完备任务变体的框架，旨在评估长程智能体在模糊情况下的可靠性，从而系统地评估澄清行为。

Authors: George Pu, Michael S. Lee, Udari Madhushani Sehwag, David J. Lee, Bryan Zhu, Yash Maurya, Mohit Raghavendra, Yuan Xue, Samuel Marc Denton

AudioRouter: Data Efficient Audio Understanding via RL based Dual Reasoning

Abstract (English): Large Audio Language Models (LALMs) have demonstrated strong capabilities in audio understanding and reasoning. However, their performance on fine grained auditory perception remains unreliable, and existing approaches largely rely on data intensive training to internalize perceptual abilities. We propose AudioRouter, a reinforcement learning framework that enables LALMs to improve audio understanding by learning when and how to use external audio tools. Rather than tightly coupling tool usage with audio reasoning, AudioRouter formulates tool use as an explicit decision making problem and optimizes a lightweight routing policy while keeping the underlying reasoning model frozen. Experimental results show that AudioRouter achieves substantial improvements on standard audio understanding benchmarks while requiring up to 600x less training data to learn tool usage compared with conventional training paradigms. These findings suggest that learning effective tool usage offers a data efficient and scalable alternative to internalizing perceptual abilities in LALMs.

摘要（中文）: 大型音频语言模型（LALM）在音频理解和推理方面表现出强大的能力。然而，它们在细粒度听觉感知方面的性能仍然不可靠，并且现有的方法在很大程度上依赖于数据密集型训练来内化感知能力。我们提出了AudioRouter，一种强化学习框架，它使LALM能够通过学习何时以及如何使用外部音频工具来提高音频理解能力。与将工具使用与音频推理紧密耦合不同，AudioRouter 将工具使用形式化为一个显式的决策问题，并在保持底层推理模型冻结的同时优化一个轻量级的路由策略。实验结果表明，与传统的训练范式相比，AudioRouter 在标准音频理解基准测试上取得了显著的改进，同时学习工具使用所需的训练数据减少了高达 600 倍。这些发现表明，学习有效的工具使用为在 LALM 中内化感知能力提供了一种数据高效且可扩展的替代方案。

TLDR: AudioRouter is a reinforcement learning framework that enables Large Audio Language Models (LALMs) to improve audio understanding by learning to use external audio tools efficiently, requiring significantly less training data compared to conventional methods.

简要说明: AudioRouter是一个强化学习框架，它使大型音频语言模型（LALMs）能够通过学习如何有效地使用外部音频工具来提高音频理解能力，与传统方法相比，所需的训练数据大大减少。

Authors: Liyang Chen, Hongkai Chen, Yujun Cai, Sifan Li, Qingwen Ye, Yiwei Wang

Affordances Enable Partial World Modeling with LLMs

Abstract (English): Full models of the world require complex knowledge of immense detail. While pre-trained large models have been hypothesized to contain similar knowledge due to extensive pre-training on vast amounts of internet scale data, using them directly in a search procedure is inefficient and inaccurate. Conversely, partial models focus on making high quality predictions for a subset of state and actions: those linked through affordances that achieve user intents~\citep{khetarpal2020can}. Can we posit large models as partial world models? We provide a formal answer to this question, proving that agents achieving task-agnostic, language-conditioned intents necessarily possess predictive partial-world models informed by affordances. In the multi-task setting, we introduce distribution-robust affordances and show that partial models can be extracted to significantly improve search efficiency. Empirical evaluations in tabletop robotics tasks demonstrate that our affordance-aware partial models reduce the search branching factor and achieve higher rewards compared to full world models.

摘要（中文）: 以下是该英文论文摘要的中文翻译： 世界的完整模型需要对海量细节的复杂知识。虽然预训练的大型模型由于在海量互联网规模的数据上进行广泛的预训练，已被假设包含类似知识，但在搜索过程中直接使用它们是低效且不准确的。相反，部分模型专注于对状态和动作的子集做出高质量的预测：这些状态和动作通过实现用户意图的可供性（affordances）连接起来。我们能否假设大型模型是世界的部分模型？我们对这个问题给出了正式的答案，证明了实现任务无关的、语言调节意图的智能体必然拥有由可供性驱动的预测性部分世界模型。在多任务设置中，我们引入了分布鲁棒的可供性，并表明可以提取部分模型以显著提高搜索效率。在桌面机器人任务中的实证评估表明，与完整世界模型相比，我们基于可供性的部分模型降低了搜索分支因子并实现了更高的奖励。

TLDR: This paper argues that LLMs can be viewed as partial world models informed by affordances, and demonstrates that using affordance-aware partial models improves search efficiency and reward in tabletop robotics tasks compared to full world models.

简要说明: 该论文认为大型语言模型可以被视为由可供性（affordance）所引导的局部世界模型，并展示了与完整世界模型相比，使用感知可供性的局部模型可以提高桌面机器人任务的搜索效率和奖励。

Authors: Khimya Khetarpal, Gheorghe Comanici, Jonathan Richens, Jeremy Shar, Fei Xia, Laurent Orseau, Aleksandra Faust, Doina Precup

Olaf-World: Orienting Latent Actions for Video World Modeling

Abstract (English): Scaling action-controllable world models is limited by the scarcity of action labels. While latent action learning promises to extract control interfaces from unlabeled video, learned latents often fail to transfer across contexts: they entangle scene-specific cues and lack a shared coordinate system. This occurs because standard objectives operate only within each clip, providing no mechanism to align action semantics across contexts. Our key insight is that although actions are unobserved, their semantic effects are observable and can serve as a shared reference. We introduce Seq$Δ$-REPA, a sequence-level control-effect alignment objective that anchors integrated latent action to temporal feature differences from a frozen, self-supervised video encoder. Building on this, we present Olaf-World, a pipeline that pretrains action-conditioned video world models from large-scale passive video. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method learns a more structured latent action space, leading to stronger zero-shot action transfer and more data-efficient adaptation to new control interfaces than state-of-the-art baselines.

摘要（中文）: 扩展具备动作可控性的世界模型受到动作标签稀缺的限制。尽管隐变量动作学习有望从无标签视频中提取控制接口，但学习到的隐变量通常无法跨环境迁移：它们混杂了特定于场景的线索并且缺乏共享的坐标系。这是因为标准目标函数仅在每个片段内操作，无法提供跨环境对齐动作语义的机制。我们的关键洞察是，尽管动作是不可观察的，但它们的语义效果是可观察的，并且可以作为共享的参考。我们引入了 Seq$Δ$-REPA，一种序列级别的控制-效果对齐目标函数，它将整合的隐变量动作锚定到来自冻结的自监督视频编码器的时间特征差异。在此基础上，我们提出了 Olaf-World，一种从大规模被动视频预训练动作条件视频世界模型的流程。大量的实验表明，我们的方法学习了一种更结构化的隐变量动作空间，与最先进的基线相比，它能够在零样本动作迁移中表现更强，并且能够以更高的数据效率适应新的控制接口。

TLDR: Olaf-World presents a method for pretraining action-conditioned video world models from unlabeled video by aligning latent actions with observed effects, improving zero-shot transfer and data efficiency compared to baselines.

简要说明: Olaf-World提出了一种从无标签视频中预训练动作条件视频世界模型的方法，通过将潜在动作与观察到的效果对齐，从而提高了零样本迁移和数据效率，优于基线方法。

Authors: Yuxin Jiang, Yuchao Gu, Ivor W. Tsang, Mike Zheng Shou

Agent World Model: Infinity Synthetic Environments for Agentic Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Recent advances in large language model (LLM) have empowered autonomous agents to perform complex tasks that require multi-turn interactions with tools and environments. However, scaling such agent training is limited by the lack of diverse and reliable environments. In this paper, we propose Agent World Model (AWM), a fully synthetic environment generation pipeline. Using this pipeline, we scale to 1,000 environments covering everyday scenarios, in which agents can interact with rich toolsets (35 tools per environment on average) and obtain high-quality observations. Notably, these environments are code-driven and backed by databases, providing more reliable and consistent state transitions than environments simulated by LLMs. Moreover, they enable more efficient agent interaction compared with collecting trajectories from realistic environments. To demonstrate the effectiveness of this resource, we perform large-scale reinforcement learning for multi-turn tool-use agents. Thanks to the fully executable environments and accessible database states, we can also design reliable reward functions. Experiments on three benchmarks show that training exclusively in synthetic environments, rather than benchmark-specific ones, yields strong out-of-distribution generalization. The code is available at https://github.com/Snowflake-Labs/agent-world-model.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLM）的最新进展已经赋能自主智能体执行需要与工具和环境进行多轮交互的复杂任务。然而，缺乏多样化和可靠的环境限制了此类智能体训练的扩展。在本文中，我们提出了一种完全合成的环境生成流程，即智能体世界模型（AWM）。利用该流程，我们将环境扩展到1000个，涵盖日常场景，其中智能体可以与丰富的工具集（平均每个环境35个工具）交互，并获得高质量的观测。值得注意的是，这些环境由代码驱动并由数据库支持，与由LLM模拟的环境相比，提供了更可靠和一致的状态转换。此外，与从真实环境中收集轨迹相比，它们使智能体交互更有效率。为了证明这种资源的有效性，我们对多轮工具使用智能体进行了大规模强化学习。得益于完全可执行的环境和可访问的数据库状态，我们还可以设计可靠的奖励函数。在三个基准测试上的实验表明，完全在合成环境中进行训练，而不是在特定于基准测试的环境中进行训练，能够产生强大的分布外泛化能力。代码可在https://github.com/Snowflake-Labs/agent-world-model获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces Agent World Model (AWM), a fully synthetic, code-driven environment generation pipeline for scaling agent training with diverse scenarios, rich toolsets, and reliable state transitions, leading to improved out-of-distribution generalization in tool-use agents.

简要说明: 本文介绍了Agent World Model (AWM)，一个完全合成的、代码驱动的环境生成管道，用于扩展智能体训练，该管道具有多样化的场景、丰富的工具集和可靠的状态转换，从而提高了工具使用智能体的分布外泛化能力。

Authors: Zhaoyang Wang, Canwen Xu, Boyi Liu, Yite Wang, Siwei Han, Zhewei Yao, Huaxiu Yao, Yuxiong He

CODE-SHARP: Continuous Open-ended Discovery and Evolution of Skills as Hierarchical Reward Programs

Abstract (English): Developing agents capable of open-endedly discovering and learning novel skills is a grand challenge in Artificial Intelligence. While reinforcement learning offers a powerful framework for training agents to master complex skills, it typically relies on hand-designed reward functions. This is infeasible for open-ended skill discovery, where the set of meaningful skills is not known a priori. While recent methods have shown promising results towards automating reward function design, they remain limited to refining rewards for pre-defined tasks. To address this limitation, we introduce Continuous Open-ended Discovery and Evolution of Skills as Hierarchical Reward Programs (CODE-SHARP), a novel framework leveraging Foundation Models (FM) to open-endedly expand and refine a hierarchical skill archive, structured as a directed graph of executable reward functions in code. We show that a goal-conditioned agent trained exclusively on the rewards generated by the discovered SHARP skills learns to solve increasingly long-horizon goals in the Craftax environment. When composed by a high-level FM-based planner, the discovered skills enable a single goal-conditioned agent to solve complex, long-horizon tasks, outperforming both pretrained agents and task-specific expert policies by over $134$% on average. We will open-source our code and provide additional videos at https://sites.google.com/view/code-sharp/homepage.

摘要（中文）: 能够开放式地发现和学习新技能的智能体是人工智能领域的一项宏伟挑战。虽然强化学习为训练智能体掌握复杂技能提供了一个强大的框架，但通常依赖于手工设计的奖励函数。这对于开放式技能发现是不可行的，因为有意义的技能集合是先验未知的。尽管最近的方法在自动化奖励函数设计方面显示出有希望的结果，但它们仍然仅限于为预定义的任务优化奖励。为了解决这个局限性，我们提出了一种新颖的框架：基于分层奖励程序的技能持续开放式发现与进化（CODE-SHARP），该框架利用基础模型（FM）来开放式地扩展和优化一个分层技能档案，该档案被组织成代码中可执行奖励函数的有向图。我们表明，一个仅基于由已发现的SHARP技能生成的奖励训练的目标条件智能体，能够学会解决Craftax环境中越来越长期的目标。当由基于高级FM的规划器组合时，所发现的技能使单个目标条件智能体能够解决复杂的、长期的任务，平均优于预训练的智能体和特定于任务的专家策略超过$134$％。我们将开源我们的代码，并在https://sites.google.com/view/code-sharp/homepage提供更多视频。

TLDR: The paper introduces CODE-SHARP, a framework for open-ended skill discovery using foundation models to generate hierarchical reward programs, enabling agents to solve complex, long-horizon tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了CODE-SHARP，一个使用基础模型生成分层奖励程序的开放式技能发现框架，使智能体能够解决复杂的、长期的任务。

Authors: Richard Bornemann, Pierluigi Vito Amadori, Antoine Cully

Optimistic World Models: Efficient Exploration in Model-Based Deep Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Efficient exploration remains a central challenge in reinforcement learning (RL), particularly in sparse-reward environments. We introduce Optimistic World Models (OWMs), a principled and scalable framework for optimistic exploration that brings classical reward-biased maximum likelihood estimation (RBMLE) from adaptive control into deep RL. In contrast to upper confidence bound (UCB)-style exploration methods, OWMs incorporate optimism directly into model learning by augmentation with an optimistic dynamics loss that biases imagined transitions toward higher-reward outcomes. This fully gradient-based loss requires neither uncertainty estimates nor constrained optimization. Our approach is plug-and-play with existing world model frameworks, preserving scalability while requiring only minimal modifications to standard training procedures. We instantiate OWMs within two state-of-the-art world model architectures, leading to Optimistic DreamerV3 and Optimistic STORM, which demonstrate significant improvements in sample efficiency and cumulative return compared to their baseline counterparts.

摘要（中文）: 高效探索是强化学习（RL）中一个核心挑战，尤其是在稀疏奖励环境中。我们提出了乐观世界模型（OWMs），一个有原则的和可扩展的乐观探索框架，将自适应控制中经典的带有奖励偏差的最大似然估计（RBMLE）引入到深度强化学习中。与基于置信上限（UCB）的探索方法不同，OWMs通过增加一个乐观的动力学损失，将乐观性直接融入到模型学习中，该损失将想象中的转移偏向于更高奖励的结果。这种完全基于梯度的损失既不需要不确定性估计，也不需要约束优化。我们的方法可以即插即用，与现有的世界模型框架结合，保持可扩展性的同时，只需要对标准训练程序进行最小的修改。我们在两个最先进的世界模型架构中实例化了OWMs，从而产生了乐观DreamerV3和乐观STORM，与它们的基线对应物相比，它们在样本效率和累积回报方面表现出显著的改进。

TLDR: The paper introduces Optimistic World Models (OWMs), a novel exploration technique for deep RL that incorporates optimism into model learning through an optimistic dynamics loss, achieving improved sample efficiency in sparse-reward environments.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了乐观世界模型 (OWMs)，一种新的深度强化学习探索技术，通过乐观动态损失将乐观性融入模型学习中，从而在稀疏奖励环境中提高样本效率。

Authors: Akshay Mete, Shahid Aamir Sheikh, Tzu-Hsiang Lin, Dileep Kalathil, P. R. Kumar

Active Zero: Self-Evolving Vision-Language Models through Active Environment Exploration

Abstract (English): Self-play has enabled large language models to autonomously improve through self-generated challenges. However, existing self-play methods for vision-language models rely on passive interaction with static image collections, resulting in strong dependence on initial datasets and inefficient learning. Without the ability to actively seek visual data tailored to their evolving capabilities, agents waste computational effort on samples that are either trivial or beyond their current skill level. To address these limitations, we propose Active-Zero, a framework that shifts from passive interaction to active exploration of visual environments. Active-Zero employs three co-evolving agents: a Searcher that retrieves images from open-world repositories based on the model's capability frontier, a Questioner that synthesizes calibrated reasoning tasks, and a Solver refined through accuracy rewards. This closed loop enables self-scaffolding auto-curricula where the model autonomously constructs its learning trajectory. On Qwen2.5-VL-7B-Instruct across 12 benchmarks, Active-Zero achieves 53.97 average accuracy on reasoning tasks (5.7% improvement) and 59.77 on general understanding (3.9% improvement), consistently outperforming existing self-play baselines. These results highlight active exploration as a key ingredient for scalable and adaptive self-evolving vision-language systems.

摘要（中文）: 自博弈使得大型语言模型能够通过自我生成的挑战自主提升能力。然而，现有的视觉-语言模型自博弈方法依赖于与静态图像集合的被动交互，导致对初始数据集的强烈依赖和低效学习。由于缺乏主动寻求针对其不断发展的能力量身定制的视觉数据的能力，智能体会在要么过于简单，要么超出其当前技能水平的样本上浪费计算资源。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了 Active-Zero，一个将被动交互转变为主动探索视觉环境的框架。Active-Zero 采用三个协同演化的智能体：一个搜索者（Searcher），基于模型的能力前沿从开放世界存储库中检索图像；一个提问者（Questioner），合成校准的推理任务；以及一个求解者（Solver），通过准确性奖励进行优化。这种闭环使得模型能够自主构建其学习轨迹，从而实现自我构建的自动课程。在 Qwen2.5-VL-7B-Instruct 模型上，Active-Zero 在 12 个基准测试中的推理任务上达到了 53.97 的平均准确率（提升 5.7%），在通用理解上达到了 59.77 的平均准确率（提升 3.9%），始终优于现有的自博弈基线。这些结果表明，主动探索是可扩展和自适应的自进化视觉-语言系统的关键要素。

TLDR: The paper introduces Active-Zero, a novel self-evolving vision-language model framework that uses active exploration of visual environments to improve its reasoning and general understanding abilities, outperforming existing self-play baselines.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Active-Zero，一种新型的自进化视觉-语言模型框架，它使用主动探索视觉环境来提高其推理和一般理解能力，优于现有的自博弈基线。

Authors: Jinghan He, Junfeng Fang, Feng Xiong, Zijun Yao, Fei Shen, Haiyun Guo, Jinqiao Wang, Tat-Seng Chua

ResWorld: Temporal Residual World Model for End-to-End Autonomous Driving

Abstract (English): The comprehensive understanding capabilities of world models for driving scenarios have significantly improved the planning accuracy of end-to-end autonomous driving frameworks. However, the redundant modeling of static regions and the lack of deep interaction with trajectories hinder world models from exerting their full effectiveness. In this paper, we propose Temporal Residual World Model (TR-World), which focuses on dynamic object modeling. By calculating the temporal residuals of scene representations, the information of dynamic objects can be extracted without relying on detection and tracking. TR-World takes only temporal residuals as input, thus predicting the future spatial distribution of dynamic objects more precisely. By combining the prediction with the static object information contained in the current BEV features, accurate future BEV features can be obtained. Furthermore, we propose Future-Guided Trajectory Refinement (FGTR) module, which conducts interaction between prior trajectories (predicted from the current scene representation) and the future BEV features. This module can not only utilize future road conditions to refine trajectories, but also provides sparse spatial-temporal supervision on future BEV features to prevent world model collapse. Comprehensive experiments conducted on the nuScenes and NAVSIM datasets demonstrate that our method, namely ResWorld, achieves state-of-the-art planning performance. The code is available at https://github.com/mengtan00/ResWorld.git.

摘要（中文）: 世界模型对驾驶场景的全面理解能力已显著提升端到端自动驾驶框架的规划精度。然而，对静态区域的冗余建模以及与轨迹缺乏深度交互，阻碍了世界模型充分发挥其效力。本文提出了一种时间残差世界模型（TR-World），专注于动态对象建模。通过计算场景表示的时间残差，可以在不依赖于检测和跟踪的情况下提取动态对象的信息。TR-World仅将时间残差作为输入，从而可以更精确地预测动态对象的未来空间分布。通过将预测结果与当前BEV特征中包含的静态对象信息相结合，可以获得准确的未来BEV特征。此外，我们提出了未来引导的轨迹精炼（FGTR）模块，该模块在（通过当前场景表示预测得到的）先验轨迹和未来BEV特征之间进行交互。该模块不仅可以利用未来的道路状况来精炼轨迹，还可以对未来的BEV特征提供稀疏的时空监督，以防止世界模型崩溃。在nuScenes和NAVSIM数据集上进行的大量实验表明，我们的方法ResWorld实现了最先进的规划性能。代码可在 https://github.com/mengtan00/ResWorld.git 获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces ResWorld, a Temporal Residual World Model for autonomous driving that improves planning accuracy by focusing on dynamic object modeling and using a Future-Guided Trajectory Refinement module. It achieves state-of-the-art performance on nuScenes and NAVSIM datasets.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ResWorld，一种用于自动驾驶的时间残差世界模型，通过关注动态对象建模以及使用未来引导的轨迹优化模块来提高规划精度。该方法在nuScenes和NAVSIM数据集上取得了最先进的性能。

Authors: Jinqing Zhang, Zehua Fu, Zelin Xu, Wenying Dai, Qingjie Liu, Yunhong Wang

Why Does RL Generalize Better Than SFT? A Data-Centric Perspective on VLM Post-Training

Abstract (English): The adaptation of large-scale Vision-Language Models (VLMs) through post-training reveals a pronounced generalization gap: models fine-tuned with Reinforcement Learning (RL) consistently achieve superior out-of-distribution (OOD) performance compared to those trained with Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT). This paper posits a data-centric explanation for this phenomenon, contending that RL's generalization advantage arises from an implicit data filtering mechanism that inherently prioritizes medium-difficulty training samples. To test this hypothesis, we systematically evaluate the OOD generalization of SFT models across training datasets of varying difficulty levels. Our results confirm that data difficulty is a critical factor, revealing that training on hard samples significantly degrades OOD performance. Motivated by this finding, we introduce Difficulty-Curated SFT (DC-SFT), a straightforward method that explicitly filters the training set based on sample difficulty. Experiments show that DC-SFT not only substantially enhances OOD generalization over standard SFT, but also surpasses the performance of RL-based training, all while providing greater stability and computational efficiency. This work offers a data-centric account of the OOD generalization gap in VLMs and establishes a more efficient pathway to achieving robust generalization. Code is available at https://github.com/byyx666/DC-SFT.

摘要（中文）: 大规模视觉-语言模型（VLMs）通过后训练进行适配时，揭示了一个显著的泛化差距：与使用监督式微调（SFT）训练的模型相比，使用强化学习（RL）进行微调的模型始终能获得更优的分布外（OOD）性能。本文针对这种现象提出了一个以数据为中心的解释，认为RL的泛化优势源于一种隐式的数据过滤机制，该机制本质上优先选择中等难度的训练样本。为了验证这一假设，我们系统性地评估了SFT模型在不同难度级别的训练数据集上的OOD泛化性能。我们的结果证实了数据难度是一个关键因素，表明在困难样本上训练会显著降低OOD性能。受此发现的启发，我们引入了难度分级SFT（DC-SFT），这是一种直接基于样本难度对训练集进行显式过滤的方法。实验表明，DC-SFT不仅大幅提高了相对于标准SFT的OOD泛化性能，而且超越了基于RL的训练的性能，同时提供了更高的稳定性和计算效率。这项工作为VLMs中的OOD泛化差距提供了一个以数据为中心的解释，并建立了一条更有效的实现稳健泛化的途径。代码可在https://github.com/byyx666/DC-SFT上获取。

TLDR: This paper investigates why RL outperforms SFT for VLM generalization, attributing it to RL's implicit data filtering that prioritizes medium-difficulty samples. It introduces Difficulty-Curated SFT (DC-SFT), which surpasses RL in OOD generalization with improved efficiency and stability.

简要说明: 本文研究了为什么强化学习 (RL) 在视觉语言模型 (VLM) 泛化方面优于监督微调 (SFT)，认为这归因于 RL 隐式数据过滤，该过滤优先考虑中等难度的样本。文章提出了一种难度管理型 SFT (DC-SFT) 方法，该方法在超出分布 (OOD) 泛化方面超越了 RL，并具有更高的效率和稳定性。

Authors: Aojun Lu, Tao Feng, Hangjie Yuan, Wei Li, Yanan Sun

DeepImageSearch: Benchmarking Multimodal Agents for Context-Aware Image Retrieval in Visual Histories

Abstract (English): Existing multimodal retrieval systems excel at semantic matching but implicitly assume that query-image relevance can be measured in isolation. This paradigm overlooks the rich dependencies inherent in realistic visual streams, where information is distributed across temporal sequences rather than confined to single snapshots. To bridge this gap, we introduce DeepImageSearch, a novel agentic paradigm that reformulates image retrieval as an autonomous exploration task. Models must plan and perform multi-step reasoning over raw visual histories to locate targets based on implicit contextual cues. We construct DISBench, a challenging benchmark built on interconnected visual data. To address the scalability challenge of creating context-dependent queries, we propose a human-model collaborative pipeline that employs vision-language models to mine latent spatiotemporal associations, effectively offloading intensive context discovery before human verification. Furthermore, we build a robust baseline using a modular agent framework equipped with fine-grained tools and a dual-memory system for long-horizon navigation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DISBench poses significant challenges to state-of-the-art models, highlighting the necessity of incorporating agentic reasoning into next-generation retrieval systems.

摘要（中文）: 现有的多模态检索系统擅长语义匹配，但隐式地假设查询-图像相关性可以孤立地衡量。这种范式忽略了现实视觉流中固有的丰富依赖关系，在视觉流中信息分布在时间序列中，而不是局限于单个快照。为了弥合这一差距，我们引入了 DeepImageSearch，一种新颖的 Agentic 范式，它将图像检索重新定义为自主探索任务。模型必须规划并基于原始视觉历史执行多步推理，以根据隐式上下文线索定位目标。我们构建了 DISBench，一个建立在互连视觉数据上的具有挑战性的基准。为了应对创建上下文相关查询的可扩展性挑战，我们提出了一种人-模型协作流程，该流程利用视觉-语言模型来挖掘潜在的时空关联，从而在人工验证之前有效地卸载密集的上下文发现。此外，我们构建了一个强大的基线，该基线使用配备了细粒度工具和用于长程导航的双重记忆系统的模块化 Agent 框架。广泛的实验表明，DISBench 对最先进的模型提出了重大挑战，突显了将 Agentic 推理纳入下一代检索系统的必要性。

TLDR: The paper introduces DeepImageSearch (DIS), a new agentic paradigm and benchmark (DISBench) for context-aware image retrieval in visual histories. It highlights the limitations of existing retrieval systems and emphasizes the need for agentic reasoning in realistic visual streams.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了DeepImageSearch (DIS), 一种新的基于智能体的图像检索范式和基准测试 (DISBench)，用于在视觉历史中实现上下文感知的图像检索。论文强调了现有检索系统的局限性，并强调了在现实视觉流中引入智能体推理的必要性。

Authors: Chenlong Deng, Mengjie Deng, Junjie Wu, Dun Zeng, Teng Wang, Qingsong Xie, Jiadeng Huang, Shengjie Ma, Changwang Zhang, Zhaoxiang Wang, Jun Wang, Yutao Zhu, Zhicheng Dou

Multimodal Priors-Augmented Text-Driven 3D Human-Object Interaction Generation

Abstract (English): We address the challenging task of text-driven 3D human-object interaction (HOI) motion generation. Existing methods primarily rely on a direct text-to-HOI mapping, which suffers from three key limitations due to the significant cross-modality gap: (Q1) sub-optimal human motion, (Q2) unnatural object motion, and (Q3) weak interaction between humans and objects. To address these challenges, we propose MP-HOI, a novel framework grounded in four core insights: (1) Multimodal Data Priors: We leverage multimodal data (text, image, pose/object) from large multimodal models as priors to guide HOI generation, which tackles Q1 and Q2 in data modeling. (2) Enhanced Object Representation: We improve existing object representations by incorporating geometric keypoints, contact features, and dynamic properties, enabling expressive object representations, which tackles Q2 in data representation. (3) Multimodal-Aware Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) Model: We propose a modality-aware MoE model for effective multimodal feature fusion paradigm, which tackles Q1 and Q2 in feature fusion. (4) Cascaded Diffusion with Interaction Supervision: We design a cascaded diffusion framework that progressively refines human-object interaction features under dedicated supervision, which tackles Q3 in interaction refinement. Comprehensive experiments demonstrate that MP-HOI outperforms existing approaches in generating high-fidelity and fine-grained HOI motions.

摘要（中文）: 我们致力于解决文本驱动的3D人-物交互 (HOI) 运动生成这一具有挑战性的任务。现有方法主要依赖于直接的文本到HOI映射，但由于显著的跨模态差距，存在三个主要局限：（Q1）次优的人体运动、（Q2）不自然的物体运动、（Q3）人与物体之间的弱交互。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了MP-HOI，一个基于四个核心洞见的新型框架：（1）多模态数据先验：我们利用来自大型多模态模型的多模态数据（文本、图像、姿势/物体）作为先验来指导HOI生成，从而在数据建模中解决Q1和Q2。（2）增强的物体表示：我们通过结合几何关键点、接触特征和动态属性来改进现有的物体表示，从而实现富有表现力的物体表示，从而在数据表示中解决Q2。（3）多模态感知的专家混合 (MoE)模型：我们提出了一种模态感知的MoE模型，用于有效进行多模态特征融合，从而在特征融合中解决Q1和Q2。（4）具有交互监督的级联扩散：我们设计了一个级联扩散框架，该框架在专用监督下逐步细化人物交互特征，从而在交互细化中解决Q3。综合实验表明，MP-HOI在生成高保真和精细的HOI运动方面优于现有方法。

TLDR: This paper introduces MP-HOI, a novel framework using multimodal priors and a cascaded diffusion model to generate high-fidelity 3D human-object interaction motions from text, addressing limitations in existing text-to-HOI mapping approaches.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种名为MP-HOI的新框架，该框架利用多模态先验知识和一个级联扩散模型，从文本生成高保真度的3D人和物体交互动作，从而解决现有文本到HOI映射方法的局限性。

Authors: Yin Wang, Ziyao Zhang, Zhiying Leng, Haitian Liu, Frederick W. B. Li, Mu Li, Xiaohui Liang

VideoWorld 2: Learning Transferable Knowledge from Real-world Videos

Abstract (English): Learning transferable knowledge from unlabeled video data and applying it in new environments is a fundamental capability of intelligent agents. This work presents VideoWorld 2, which extends VideoWorld and offers the first investigation into learning transferable knowledge directly from raw real-world videos. At its core, VideoWorld 2 introduces a dynamic-enhanced Latent Dynamics Model (dLDM) that decouples action dynamics from visual appearance: a pretrained video diffusion model handles visual appearance modeling, enabling the dLDM to learn latent codes that focus on compact and meaningful task-related dynamics. These latent codes are then modeled autoregressively to learn task policies and support long-horizon reasoning. We evaluate VideoWorld 2 on challenging real-world handcraft making tasks, where prior video generation and latent-dynamics models struggle to operate reliably. Remarkably, VideoWorld 2 achieves up to 70% improvement in task success rate and produces coherent long execution videos. In robotics, we show that VideoWorld 2 can acquire effective manipulation knowledge from the Open-X dataset, which substantially improves task performance on CALVIN. This study reveals the potential of learning transferable world knowledge directly from raw videos, with all code, data, and models to be open-sourced for further research.

摘要（中文）: 从无标签视频数据中学习可迁移的知识并将其应用于新环境，是智能体的一项基本能力。本研究提出了 VideoWorld 2，它是 VideoWorld 的扩展，并首次研究了直接从原始真实世界视频中学习可迁移知识的问题。VideoWorld 2 的核心在于引入了一种动态增强的潜在动态模型 (dLDM)，它将动作动态与视觉表征解耦：预训练的视频扩散模型负责视觉表征建模，从而使 dLDM 能够学习专注于紧凑且有意义的任务相关动态的潜在编码。然后对这些潜在编码进行自回归建模，以学习任务策略并支持长时程推理。我们在具有挑战性的真实世界手工制作任务上评估了 VideoWorld 2，在这些任务中，先前的视频生成和潜在动态模型难以可靠地运行。值得注意的是，VideoWorld 2 将任务成功率提高了高达 70%，并生成了连贯的长时执行视频。在机器人领域，我们展示了 VideoWorld 2 可以从 Open-X 数据集中获得有效的操作知识，从而大幅提高在 CALVIN 上的任务性能。这项研究揭示了直接从原始视频中学习可迁移世界知识的潜力，所有代码、数据和模型都将开源，以供进一步研究。

TLDR: The paper introduces VideoWorld 2, a framework for learning transferable knowledge from real-world videos using a dynamic-enhanced Latent Dynamics Model (dLDM). It attains improvements in real-world handcrafting and robotics tasks demonstrating potential for learning from raw video.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了VideoWorld 2，一个利用动态增强潜在动力学模型(dLDM)从真实世界视频中学习可迁移知识的框架。 它在现实世界的手工艺和机器人任务中取得了改进，证明了从原始视频中学习的潜力。

Authors: Zhongwei Ren, Yunchao Wei, Xiao Yu, Guixun Luo, Yao Zhao, Bingyi Kang, Jiashi Feng, Xiaojie Jin

Spatio-Temporal Attention for Consistent Video Semantic Segmentation in Automated Driving

Abstract (English): Deep neural networks, especially transformer-based architectures, have achieved remarkable success in semantic segmentation for environmental perception. However, existing models process video frames independently, thus failing to leverage temporal consistency, which could significantly improve both accuracy and stability in dynamic scenes. In this work, we propose a Spatio-Temporal Attention (STA) mechanism that extends transformer attention blocks to incorporate multi-frame context, enabling robust temporal feature representations for video semantic segmentation. Our approach modifies standard self-attention to process spatio-temporal feature sequences while maintaining computational efficiency and requiring minimal changes to existing architectures. STA demonstrates broad applicability across diverse transformer architectures and remains effective across both lightweight and larger-scale models. A comprehensive evaluation on the Cityscapes and BDD100k datasets shows substantial improvements of 9.20 percentage points in temporal consistency metrics and up to 1.76 percentage points in mean intersection over union compared to single-frame baselines. These results demonstrate STA as an effective architectural enhancement for video-based semantic segmentation applications.

摘要（中文）: 深度神经网络，特别是基于Transformer的架构，在环境感知的语义分割领域取得了显著的成功。然而，现有的模型独立处理视频帧，因此未能利用时间一致性，而时间一致性可以显著提高动态场景中的准确性和稳定性。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种时空注意力（STA）机制，该机制扩展了Transformer的注意力模块以整合多帧上下文，从而为视频语义分割实现鲁棒的时间特征表示。我们的方法修改了标准的自注意力机制来处理时空特征序列，同时保持计算效率，并且只需要对现有架构进行最小的修改。STA展示了跨不同Transformer架构的广泛适用性，并且在轻量级和更大规模的模型中都保持有效性。在Cityscapes和BDD100k数据集上的全面评估显示，与单帧基线相比，时间一致性指标有了9.20个百分点的显著提高，平均交并比（mIoU）提高了高达1.76个百分点。这些结果表明，STA是基于视频的语义分割应用的一种有效的架构增强。

TLDR: This paper introduces a Spatio-Temporal Attention (STA) mechanism to improve the temporal consistency and accuracy of video semantic segmentation, particularly for automated driving applications, demonstrating significant improvements on Cityscapes and BDD100k datasets.

Authors: Serin Varghese, Kevin Ross, Fabian Hueger, Kira Maag

TVCACHE: A Stateful Tool-Value Cache for Post-Training LLM Agents

Abstract (English): In RL post-training of LLM agents, calls to external tools take several seconds or even minutes, leaving allocated GPUs idle and inflating post-training time and cost. While many tool invocations repeat across parallel rollouts and could in principle be cached, naively caching their outputs for reuse is incorrect since tool outputs depend on the environment state induced by prior agent interactions. We present TVCACHE, a stateful tool-value cache for LLM agent post-training. TVCACHE maintains a tree of observed tool-call sequences and performs longest-prefix matching for cache lookups: a hit occurs only when the agent's full tool history matches a previously executed sequence, guaranteeing identical environment state. On three diverse workloads-terminal-based tasks, SQL generation, and video understanding. TVCACHE achieves cache hit rates of up to 70% and reduces median tool call execution time by up to 6.9X, with no degradation in post-training reward accumulation.

摘要（中文）: 在LLM智能体的RL后训练中，对外部工具的调用需要几秒甚至几分钟，导致已分配的GPU处于空闲状态，并增加了后训练的时间和成本。虽然许多工具调用在并行展开中重复出现，原则上可以被缓存，但简单地缓存其输出以供重用是不正确的，因为工具的输出取决于先前智能体交互所引发的环境状态。我们提出了TVCACHE，一种用于LLM智能体后训练的有状态工具值缓存。TVCACHE维护一个观察到的工具调用序列树，并执行最长前缀匹配来进行缓存查找：只有当智能体的完整工具历史记录与之前执行的序列相匹配时，才会发生命中，保证相同的环境状态。在三个不同的工作负载中——基于终端的任务、SQL生成和视频理解——TVCACHE的缓存命中率高达70%，并将工具调用执行时间中位数降低高达6.9倍，并且后训练的奖励积累没有任何下降。

TLDR: The paper introduces TVCACHE, a stateful tool-value cache for LLM agents that caches tool call outputs based on the agent's tool-call history, significantly reducing post-training time and cost without sacrificing performance.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为TVCACHE的有状态工具值缓存，用于LLM代理，该缓存根据代理的工具调用历史记录缓存工具调用输出，从而在不牺牲性能的情况下显著减少后训练时间和成本。

Authors: Abhishek Vijaya Kumar, Bhaskar Kataria, Byungsoo Oh, Emaad Manzoor, Rachee Singh

Near-Constant Strong Violation and Last-Iterate Convergence for Online CMDPs via Decaying Safety Margins

Abstract (English): We study safe online reinforcement learning in Constrained Markov Decision Processes (CMDPs) under strong regret and violation metrics, which forbid error cancellation over time. Existing primal-dual methods that achieve sublinear strong reward regret inevitably incur growing strong constraint violation or are restricted to average-iterate convergence due to inherent oscillations. To address these limitations, we propose the Flexible safety Domain Optimization via Margin-regularized Exploration (FlexDOME) algorithm, the first to provably achieve near-constant $\tilde{O}(1)$ strong constraint violation alongside sublinear strong regret and non-asymptotic last-iterate convergence. FlexDOME incorporates time-varying safety margins and regularization terms into the primal-dual framework. Our theoretical analysis relies on a novel term-wise asymptotic dominance strategy, where the safety margin is rigorously scheduled to asymptotically majorize the functional decay rates of the optimization and statistical errors, thereby clamping cumulative violations to a near-constant level. Furthermore, we establish non-asymptotic last-iterate convergence guarantees via a policy-dual Lyapunov argument. Experiments corroborate our theoretical findings.

摘要（中文）: 我们研究在约束马尔可夫决策过程(CMDP)中，针对强化学习的强遗憾和违背度量下的安全在线强化学习，其中强遗憾和违背度量禁止误差随时间抵消。 现有实现亚线性强奖励遗憾的原-对偶方法，不可避免地会产生增长的强约束违背，或者由于固有的振荡而局限于平均迭代收敛。 为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了通过边际正则化探索的柔性安全域优化(FlexDOME)算法，该算法是首个能证明在实现亚线性强遗憾的同时，还能实现近乎常数级别$\tilde{O}(1)$的强约束违背以及非渐近最后迭代收敛的算法。 FlexDOME将时变的安全边际和正则化项纳入原-对偶框架。 我们的理论分析依赖于一种新型的逐项渐近支配策略，其中安全边际被严格调度，以渐近地主导优化和统计误差的函数衰减率，从而将累积违背限制在一个近乎常数的水平。 此外，我们通过策略-对偶 Lyapunov 论证建立了非渐近最后迭代收敛保证。 实验结果证实了我们的理论发现。

TLDR: This paper introduces FlexDOME, a novel algorithm for safe online reinforcement learning in CMDPs that achieves near-constant strong constraint violation, sublinear strong regret, and non-asymptotic last-iterate convergence, a challenging combination not previously demonstrated.

简要说明: 这篇论文介绍了一种名为FlexDOME的新算法，用于CMDPs中的安全在线强化学习，该算法实现了近乎恒定的强约束违背、次线性强遗憾和非渐近最后迭代收敛，这是一个以前没有展示过的具有挑战性的组合。

Authors: Qian Zuo, Zhiyong Wang, Fengxiang He

Patch the Distribution Mismatch: RL Rewriting Agent for Stable Off-Policy SFT

Abstract (English): Large language models (LLMs) have made rapid progress, yet adapting them to downstream scenarios still commonly relies on supervised fine-tuning (SFT). When downstream data exhibit a substantial distribution shift from the model's prior training distribution, SFT can induce catastrophic forgetting. To narrow this gap, data rewriting has been proposed as a data-centric approach that rewrites downstream training data prior to SFT. However, existing methods typically sample rewrites from a prompt-induced conditional distribution, so the resulting targets are not necessarily aligned with the model's natural QA-style generation distribution. Moreover, reliance on fixed templates can lead to diversity collapse. To address these issues, we cast data rewriting as a policy learning problem and learn a rewriting policy that better matches the backbone's QA-style generation distribution while preserving diversity. Since distributional alignment, diversity and task consistency are automatically evaluable but difficult to optimize end-to-end with differentiable objectives, we leverage reinforcement learning to optimize the rewrite distribution under reward feedback and propose an RL-based data-rewriting agent. The agent jointly optimizes QA-style distributional alignment and diversity under a hard task-consistency gate, thereby constructing a higher-quality rewritten dataset for downstream SFT. Extensive experiments show that our method achieves downstream gains comparable to standard SFT while reducing forgetting on non-downstream benchmarks by 12.34% on average. Our code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Patch-the-Prompt-Gap-4112 .

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLM）取得了快速进展，但将它们适配到下游场景通常仍依赖于监督式微调（SFT）。当下游数据与模型先前的训练分布存在显著的分布偏移时，SFT可能会导致灾难性遗忘。为了缩小这种差距，数据重写已被提出作为一种以数据为中心的方法，它在SFT之前重写下游训练数据。然而，现有方法通常从提示诱导的条件分布中采样重写内容，因此生成的目标不一定与模型自然的问答式生成分布对齐。此外，对固定模板的依赖可能导致多样性崩溃。为了解决这些问题，我们将数据重写视为策略学习问题，并学习一种重写策略，该策略更好地匹配主干模型的问答式生成分布，同时保持多样性。由于分布对齐、多样性和任务一致性是自动可评估的，但难以通过可微目标进行端到端优化，因此我们利用强化学习来优化奖励反馈下的重写分布，并提出了一种基于强化学习的数据重写代理。该代理联合优化问答式分布对齐和多样性，并实施一个硬性任务一致性门控，从而构建一个更高质量的重写数据集用于下游SFT。大量实验表明，我们的方法在实现与标准SFT相当的下游收益的同时，在非下游基准测试上的遗忘程度平均降低了12.34%。我们的代码可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Patch-the-Prompt-Gap-4112 获取。

TLDR: This paper introduces an RL-based data-rewriting agent that optimizes the downstream fine-tuning of LLMs by aligning the data distribution with the model's QA-style generation distribution, reducing catastrophic forgetting.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种基于强化学习的数据重写代理，通过将数据分布与模型的QA风格生成分布对齐来优化LLM的下游微调过程，从而减少灾难性遗忘。

Authors: Jiacheng Wang, Ping Jian, Zhen Yang, Zirong Chen, Keren Liao, Zhongbin Guo

Prioritize the Process, Not Just the Outcome: Rewarding Latent Thought Trajectories Improves Reasoning in Looped Language Models

Abstract (English): Looped Language Models (LoopLMs) perform multi-step latent reasoning prior to token generation and outperform conventional LLMs on reasoning benchmarks at smaller parameter budgets. However, attempts to further improve LoopLM reasoning with reinforcement learning have failed - standard objectives such as Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) only assign credit to the final latent state, creating a fundamental mismatch with the model's internal computation. To resolve this, we introduce RLTT (Reward Latent Thought Trajectories), a reinforcement learning framework which distributes reward across the full latent reasoning trajectory. RLTT provides dense, trajectory-level credit assignment without relying on external verifiers and can directly replace GRPO with negligible overhead. Across extensive experiments with Ouro-2.6B-Thinking under identical training and inference conditions, RLTT yields substantial improvements over GRPO on challenging mathematical reasoning benchmarks, improving accuracy by +14.4% on MATH-500, +16.6% on AIME24, and +10.0% on BeyondAIME. Despite being trained exclusively on mathematics, RLTT also transfers effectively to non-mathematical reasoning benchmarks, demonstrating the effectiveness of trajectory-level credit assignment for reinforcement learning in LoopLMs.

摘要（中文）: 循环语言模型(LoopLM)在生成token之前执行多步潜在推理，并在较小的参数预算下优于传统的LLM在推理基准测试上的表现。然而，进一步利用强化学习来改进LoopLM推理的尝试已经失败——诸如组相对策略优化(GRPO)等标准目标仅将信用分配给最终潜在状态，从而与模型的内部计算产生根本性的不匹配。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了RLTT(奖励潜在思维轨迹)，一个强化学习框架，它将奖励分配到整个潜在推理轨迹。RLTT提供密集的、轨迹级别的信用分配，而无需依赖外部验证器，并且可以直接替换GRPO，只需极小的开销。在使用Ouro-2.6B-Thinking进行的大量实验中，在相同的训练和推理条件下，RLTT在具有挑战性的数学推理基准测试上比GRPO产生了显著的改进，在MATH-500上的准确率提高了+14.4%，在AIME24上提高了+16.6%，在BeyondAIME上提高了+10.0%。尽管仅在数学上进行训练，RLTT也能有效地迁移到非数学推理基准测试，证明了轨迹级别信用分配对于LoopLM中强化学习的有效性。

TLDR: This paper introduces RLTT, a reinforcement learning framework that improves reasoning in Looped Language Models by distributing reward across the latent reasoning trajectory, leading to substantial gains on mathematical reasoning benchmarks and transfer to non-mathematical tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个强化学习框架RLTT，通过在潜在推理轨迹中分配奖励，改进了循环语言模型的推理能力，从而在数学推理基准测试中取得了显著的收益，并迁移到了非数学任务。

Authors: Jonathan Williams, Esin Tureci

Features as Rewards: Scalable Supervision for Open-Ended Tasks via Interpretability

Abstract (English): Language models trained on large-scale datasets have been shown to learn features that encode abstract concepts such as factuality or intent. Such features are traditionally used for test-time monitoring or steering. We present an alternative affordance: features as scalable supervision for open-ended tasks. We consider the case of hallucination-reduction as a desirable, yet open-ended behavior and design a reinforcement learning (RL) pipeline, titled RLFR (Reinforcement Learning from Feature Rewards), that uses features as reward functions. Grounded in a novel probing framework that identifies candidate hallucinated claims, our pipeline teaches a model to intervene and correct its completions when it is uncertain of their factuality. Furthermore, the pipeline enables scalable test-time compute, guided once more by our reward features. This end-to-end process operationalized on Gemma-3-12B-IT results in a policy that is 58% less likely to hallucinate compared to the original model (when run in tandem with our probing harness), while preserving performance on standard benchmarks. Taken together, by grounding supervision in the language of features, this paper introduces a novel paradigm in the use of interpretability for learning open-ended tasks.

摘要（中文）: 基于大规模数据集训练的语言模型已被证明能够学习编码抽象概念的特征，如事实性或意图。这些特征传统上用于测试时监控或引导。我们提出了一种替代用途：将特征作为开放式任务的可扩展监督。我们将幻觉减少视为一种理想但开放式的行为，并设计了一个名为 RLFR (基于特征奖励的强化学习) 的强化学习 (RL) 流程，该流程使用特征作为奖励函数。我们的流程基于一个新颖的探测框架，该框架识别候选幻觉声明，并教导模型在不确定其事实性的情况下介入并纠正其补全。此外，该流程能够实现可扩展的测试时计算，并再次由我们的奖励特征引导。这个在 Gemma-3-12B-IT 上实现的端到端流程产生了一个策略，与原始模型相比，该策略产生幻觉的可能性降低了 58%（与我们的探测工具同时运行），同时保留了在标准基准测试中的性能。总而言之，通过将监督建立在特征语言的基础上，本文引入了一种利用可解释性学习开放式任务的新范式。

TLDR: This paper introduces RLFR, a reinforcement learning pipeline that utilizes language model features as reward functions to reduce hallucinations in language models, achieving a 58% reduction in hallucinations on Gemma-3-12B-IT.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为 RLFR 的强化学习流程，它利用语言模型的特征作为奖励函数来减少语言模型中的幻觉，在 Gemma-3-12B-IT 上实现了 58% 的幻觉减少。

Authors: Aaditya Vikram Prasad, Connor Watts, Jack Merullo, Dhruvil Gala, Owen Lewis, Thomas McGrath, Ekdeep Singh Lubana

SQ-CBF: Signed Distance Functions for Numerically Stable Superquadric-Based Safety Filtering

Abstract (English): Ensuring safe robot operation in cluttered and dynamic environments remains a fundamental challenge. While control barrier functions provide an effective framework for real-time safety filtering, their performance critically depends on the underlying geometric representation, which is often simplified, leading to either overly conservative behavior or insufficient collision coverage. Superquadrics offer an expressive way to model complex shapes using a few primitives and are increasingly used for robot safety. To integrate this representation into collision avoidance, most existing approaches directly use their implicit functions as barrier candidates. However, we identify a critical but overlooked issue in this practice: the gradients of the implicit SQ function can become severely ill-conditioned, potentially rendering the optimization infeasible and undermining reliable real-time safety filtering. To address this issue, we formulate an SQ-based safety filtering framework that uses signed distance functions as barrier candidates. Since analytical SDFs are unavailable for general SQs, we compute distances using the efficient Gilbert-Johnson-Keerthi algorithm and obtain gradients via randomized smoothing. Extensive simulation and real-world experiments demonstrate consistent collision-free manipulation in cluttered and unstructured scenes, showing robustness to challenging geometries, sensing noise, and dynamic disturbances, while improving task efficiency in teleoperation tasks. These results highlight a pathway toward safety filters that remain precise and reliable under the geometric complexity of real-world environments.

摘要（中文）: 在杂乱和动态环境中确保机器人的安全运行仍然是一个根本性的挑战。虽然控制屏障函数为实时安全滤波提供了一个有效的框架，但其性能关键依赖于底层的几何表示，而几何表示通常被简化，导致过于保守的行为或不足的碰撞覆盖。超二次曲面提供了一种使用少量基本形状来建模复杂形状的表达性方法，并越来越多地用于机器人安全。为了将这种表示集成到避撞中，大多数现有方法直接使用其隐式函数作为屏障候选。然而，我们发现这种做法中一个关键但被忽视的问题：隐式 SQ 函数的梯度可能变得严重病态，从而可能使优化变得不可行并破坏可靠的实时安全滤波。为了解决这个问题，我们构建了一个基于 SQ 的安全滤波框架，该框架使用有符号距离函数作为屏障候选。由于通用 SQ 没有解析 SDF，我们使用高效的 Gilbert-Johnson-Keerthi 算法计算距离，并通过随机平滑获得梯度。大量的仿真和真实世界实验表明，在杂乱和非结构化场景中，一致地实现了无碰撞操作，对具有挑战性的几何形状、传感噪声和动态扰动具有鲁棒性，同时提高了遥操作任务的任务效率。这些结果突出了在真实世界环境的几何复杂性下，保持精确和可靠的安全滤波器的可行途径。

TLDR: This paper introduces SQ-CBF, a signed distance function-based control barrier function framework using superquadrics for robot safety filtering, addressing the ill-conditioning issue of superquadric implicit function gradients. The method achieves robust collision avoidance in complex environments through efficient distance computation and gradient estimation.

简要说明: 本文介绍了SQ-CBF，一个基于有符号距离函数的控制障碍函数框架，使用超二次曲面进行机器人安全过滤，解决了超二次曲面隐函数梯度病态的问题。该方法通过高效的距离计算和梯度估计，在复杂的环境中实现了稳健的避碰。

Authors: Haocheng Zhao, Lukas Brunke, Oliver Lagerquist, Siqi Zhou, Angela P. Schoellig

Enhancing Predictability of Multi-Tenant DNN Inference for Autonomous Vehicles' Perception

Abstract (English): Autonomous vehicles (AVs) rely on sensors and deep neural networks (DNNs) to perceive their surrounding environment and make maneuver decisions in real time. However, achieving real-time DNN inference in the AV's perception pipeline is challenging due to the large gap between the computation requirement and the AV's limited resources. Most, if not all, of existing studies focus on optimizing the DNN inference time to achieve faster perception by compressing the DNN model with pruning and quantization. In contrast, we present a Predictable Perception system with DNNs (PP-DNN) that reduce the amount of image data to be processed while maintaining the same level of accuracy for multi-tenant DNNs by dynamically selecting critical frames and regions of interest (ROIs). PP-DNN is based on our key insight that critical frames and ROIs for AVs vary with the AV's surrounding environment. However, it is challenging to identify and use critical frames and ROIs in multi-tenant DNNs for predictable inference. Given image-frame streams, PP-DNN leverages an ROI generator to identify critical frames and ROIs based on the similarities of consecutive frames and traffic scenarios. PP-DNN then leverages a FLOPs predictor to predict multiply-accumulate operations (MACs) from the dynamic critical frames and ROIs. The ROI scheduler coordinates the processing of critical frames and ROIs with multiple DNN models. Finally, we design a detection predictor for the perception of non-critical frames. We have implemented PP-DNN in an ROS-based AV pipeline and evaluated it with the BDD100K and the nuScenes dataset. PP-DNN is observed to significantly enhance perception predictability, increasing the number of fusion frames by up to 7.3x, reducing the fusion delay by >2.6x and fusion-delay variations by >2.3x, improving detection completeness by 75.4% and the cost-effectiveness by up to 98% over the baseline.

摘要（中文）: 自动驾驶车辆（AVs）依赖于传感器和深度神经网络（DNNs）来感知周围环境并实时做出操控决策。然而，由于计算需求与自动驾驶车辆有限资源之间的巨大差距，在自动驾驶车辆的感知流水线中实现实时DNN推理极具挑战性。大部分（如果不是全部）现有研究都侧重于优化DNN推理时间，以通过剪枝和量化压缩DNN模型来加速感知。与此相反，我们提出了一种具有DNNs的可预测感知系统（PP-DNN），该系统通过动态选择关键帧和感兴趣区域（ROIs）来减少需要处理的图像数据量，同时为多租户DNN保持相同的精度水平。PP-DNN基于我们的关键洞见，即自动驾驶车辆的关键帧和ROIs随着自动驾驶车辆周围环境的变化而变化。然而，在多租户DNN中识别和使用关键帧和ROIs以实现可预测推断仍然具有挑战性。对于图像帧流，PP-DNN利用ROIs生成器，根据连续帧和交通场景的相似性来识别关键帧和ROIs。然后，PP-DNN利用一个FLOPs预测器，从动态关键帧和ROIs中预测乘加运算（MACs）。ROI调度器协调关键帧和ROIs与多个DNN模型的处理。最后，我们设计了一个检测预测器，用于非关键帧的感知。我们已在基于ROS的自动驾驶车辆流水线中实现了PP-DNN，并使用BDD100K和nuScenes数据集对其进行了评估。观察到 PP-DNN 显著提高了感知可预测性，融合帧数量最多增加了 7.3 倍，融合延迟降低了>2.6 倍，融合延迟变化降低了>2.3 倍，检测完整性提高了 75.4%，且成本效益比基线提高了高达 98%。

TLDR: This paper proposes a system (PP-DNN) that enhances the predictability of multi-tenant DNN inference for autonomous vehicles by dynamically selecting critical frames and ROIs to reduce the amount of image data processed while maintaining accuracy, resulting in significant performance improvements.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种系统(PP-DNN)，通过动态选择关键帧和感兴趣区域来减少处理的图像数据量，同时保持准确性，从而增强自动驾驶汽车多租户DNN推理的可预测性，并带来显著的性能提升。

Authors: Liangkai Liu, Kang G. Shin, Jinkyu Lee, Chengmo Yang, Weisong Shi

Developing Neural Network-Based Gaze Control Systems for Social Robots

Abstract (English): During multi-party interactions, gaze direction is a key indicator of interest and intent, making it essential for social robots to direct their attention appropriately. Understanding the social context is crucial for robots to engage effectively, predict human intentions, and navigate interactions smoothly. This study aims to develop an empirical motion-time pattern for human gaze behavior in various social situations (e.g., entering, leaving, waving, talking, and pointing) using deep neural networks based on participants' data. We created two video clips-one for a computer screen and another for a virtual reality headset-depicting different social scenarios. Data were collected from 30 participants: 15 using an eye-tracker and 15 using an Oculus Quest 1 headset. Deep learning models, specifically Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) and Transformers, were used to analyze and predict gaze patterns. Our models achieved 60% accuracy in predicting gaze direction in a 2D animation and 65% accuracy in a 3D animation. Then, the best model was implemented onto the Nao robot; and 36 new participants evaluated its performance. The feedback indicated overall satisfaction, with those experienced in robotics rating the models more favorably.

摘要（中文）: 在多人交互中，视线方向是兴趣和意图的关键指标，因此对社交机器人而言，适当地引导其注意力至关重要。理解社会情境对于机器人有效参与、预测人类意图以及流畅地进行交互至关重要。本研究旨在使用基于参与者数据的深度神经网络，为各种社会情境（例如，进入、离开、挥手、谈话和指点）中人类视线行为开发一种经验性的运动-时间模式。我们创建了两个视频片段——一个用于计算机屏幕，另一个用于虚拟现实头显——描绘不同的社交场景。数据从30名参与者收集：15名使用眼动追踪器，15名使用Oculus Quest 1 头显。深度学习模型，特别是长短期记忆（LSTM）和Transformer，被用于分析和预测视线模式。我们的模型在预测2D动画中的视线方向的准确率达到60%，在3D动画中的准确率达到65%。然后，最佳模型被部署到Nao机器人上；并由36名新参与者评估其性能。反馈表明总体满意，具有机器人技术经验的参与者对模型的评价更高。

TLDR: This paper explores using LSTM and Transformer models to predict human gaze patterns in social interactions for implementation on a Nao robot, achieving moderate accuracy and positive initial user feedback.

简要说明: 本文探讨了使用LSTM和Transformer模型预测社交互动中人类的视线模式，以便在Nao机器人上实现，获得了中等的准确率和初步的积极用户反馈。

Authors: Ramtin Tabatabaei, Alireza Taheri

Semi-Supervised Cross-Domain Imitation Learning

Abstract (English): Cross-domain imitation learning (CDIL) accelerates policy learning by transferring expert knowledge across domains, which is valuable in applications where the collection of expert data is costly. Existing methods are either supervised, relying on proxy tasks and explicit alignment, or unsupervised, aligning distributions without paired data, but often unstable. We introduce the Semi-Supervised CDIL (SS-CDIL) setting and propose the first algorithm for SS-CDIL with theoretical justification. Our method uses only offline data, including a small number of target expert demonstrations and some unlabeled imperfect trajectories. To handle domain discrepancy, we propose a novel cross-domain loss function for learning inter-domain state-action mappings and design an adaptive weight function to balance the source and target knowledge. Experiments on MuJoCo and Robosuite show consistent gains over the baselines, demonstrating that our approach achieves stable and data-efficient policy learning with minimal supervision. Our code is available at~ https://github.com/NYCU-RL-Bandits-Lab/CDIL.

摘要（中文）: 跨领域模仿学习（CDIL）通过跨领域迁移专家知识来加速策略学习，这在收集专家数据成本高昂的应用中具有重要价值。现有方法要么是有监督的，依赖于代理任务和显式对齐，要么是无监督的，在没有配对数据的情况下对齐分布，但通常不稳定。我们引入了半监督跨领域模仿学习（SS-CDIL）设置，并提出了第一个具有理论依据的SS-CDIL算法。我们的方法仅使用离线数据，包括少量目标专家演示和一些未标记的不完美轨迹。为了处理领域差异，我们提出了一种新的跨领域损失函数，用于学习领域间的状态-动作映射，并设计了一个自适应权重函数来平衡源领域和目标领域的知识。在MuJoCo和Robosuite上的实验表明，相比于基线方法，我们的方法能够获得一致的提升，证明了我们的方法能够在极少监督的情况下实现稳定且数据高效的策略学习。我们的代码已在https://github.com/NYCU-RL-Bandits-Lab/CDIL上提供。

TLDR: This paper introduces a semi-supervised cross-domain imitation learning (SS-CDIL) algorithm that leverages a few expert target demonstrations and unlabeled imperfect trajectories to transfer knowledge across domains, validated on MuJoCo and Robosuite.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种半监督跨域模仿学习 (SS-CDIL) 算法，该算法利用少量的专家目标演示和未标记的不完美轨迹，实现跨领域的知识迁移，并在 MuJoCo 和 Robosuite 上进行了验证。
