Authors: Li-Min Chu, Kai-Siang Ma, Ming-Hong Chen, Ping-Chun Hsieh

(MGS)$^2$-Net: Unifying Micro-Geometric Scale and Macro-Geometric Structure for Cross-View Geo-Localization

Abstract (English): Cross-view geo-localization (CVGL) is pivotal for GNSS-denied UAV navigation but remains brittle under the drastic geometric misalignment between oblique aerial views and orthographic satellite references. Existing methods predominantly operate within a 2D manifold, neglecting the underlying 3D geometry where view-dependent vertical facades (macro-structure) and scale variations (micro-scale) severely corrupt feature alignment. To bridge this gap, we propose (MGS)$^2$, a geometry-grounded framework. The core of our innovation is the Macro-Geometric Structure Filtering (MGSF) module. Unlike pixel-wise matching sensitive to noise, MGSF leverages dilated geometric gradients to physically filter out high-frequency facade artifacts while enhancing the view-invariant horizontal plane, directly addressing the domain shift. To guarantee robust input for this structural filtering, we explicitly incorporate a Micro-Geometric Scale Adaptation (MGSA) module. MGSA utilizes depth priors to dynamically rectify scale discrepancies via multi-branch feature fusion. Furthermore, a Geometric-Appearance Contrastive Distillation (GACD) loss is designed to strictly discriminate against oblique occlusions. Extensive experiments demonstrate that (MGS)$^2$ achieves state-of-the-art performance, recording a Recall@1 of 97.5\% on University-1652 and 97.02\% on SUES-200. Furthermore, the framework exhibits superior cross-dataset generalization against geometric ambiguity. The code is available at: \href{https://github.com/GabrielLi1473/MGS-Net}{https://github.com/GabrielLi1473/MGS-Net}.

摘要（中文）: **中文翻译：** 跨视角地理定位（CVGL）对于GNSS拒止环境下的无人机导航至关重要，但由于倾斜航拍图像与正射卫星参考图像之间存在剧烈的几何错位，其鲁棒性仍然较差。现有方法主要在二维流形中运行，忽略了底层三维几何结构，而视角相关的垂直立面（宏观结构）和尺度变化（微观尺度）严重破坏了特征对齐。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了(MGS)$^2$，一个基于几何的框架。我们创新的核心是宏观几何结构滤波（MGSF）模块。与对噪声敏感的逐像素匹配不同，MGSF利用扩张的几何梯度来物理地滤除高频立面伪影，同时增强视角不变的水平面，从而直接解决领域偏移。为了保证该结构滤波的鲁棒输入，我们显式地引入了微观几何尺度自适应（MGSA）模块。MGSA利用深度先验，通过多分支特征融合来动态地校正尺度差异。此外，我们设计了一种几何-外观对比蒸馏（GACD）损失，以严格区分倾斜遮挡。大量实验表明，(MGS)$^2$达到了最先进的性能，在University-1652数据集上获得了97.5%的Recall@1，在SUES-200数据集上获得了97.02%的Recall@1。此外，该框架在几何模糊性方面表现出卓越的跨数据集泛化能力。代码可在以下网址获取：\href{https://github.com/GabrielLi1473/MGS-Net}{https://github.com/GabrielLi1473/MGS-Net}。

TLDR: The paper introduces (MGS)$^2$-Net, a novel geometry-grounded framework for cross-view geo-localization that addresses geometric misalignment issues between aerial and satellite views by filtering out facade artifacts and adapting to scale discrepancies using depth priors and contrastive distillation.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了(MGS)$^2$-Net，一种用于跨视角地理定位的新型几何框架，通过过滤立面伪影并使用深度先验和对比蒸馏来适应尺度差异，从而解决航拍图像和卫星图像之间几何错位问题。

Authors: Minglei Li, Mengfan He, Chao Chen, Ziyang Meng

A Unified Experimental Architecture for Informative Path Planning: from Simulation to Deployment with GuadalPlanner

Abstract (English): The evaluation of informative path planning algorithms for autonomous vehicles is often hindered by fragmented execution pipelines and limited transferability between simulation and real-world deployment. This paper introduces a unified architecture that decouples high-level decision-making from vehicle-specific control, enabling algorithms to be evaluated consistently across different abstraction levels without modification. The proposed architecture is realized through GuadalPlanner, which defines standardized interfaces between planning, sensing, and vehicle execution. It is an open and extensible research tool that supports discrete graph-based environments and interchangeable planning strategies, and is built upon widely adopted robotics technologies, including ROS2, MAVLink, and MQTT. Its design allows the same algorithmic logic to be deployed in fully simulated environments, software-in-the-loop configurations, and physical autonomous vehicles using an identical execution pipeline. The approach is validated through a set of experiments, including real-world deployment on an autonomous surface vehicle performing water quality monitoring with real-time sensor feedback.

摘要（中文）: 用于评估自动驾驶汽车的信息化路径规划算法通常受阻于零散的执行流程以及在仿真和真实部署之间有限的迁移性。本文介绍了一种统一架构，该架构将高层决策与车辆特定控制解耦，从而无需修改即可在不同抽象级别上一致地评估算法。所提出的架构通过GuadalPlanner实现，它定义了规划、感知和车辆执行之间的标准化接口。它是一个开放且可扩展的研究工具，支持离散的基于图的环境和可互换的规划策略，并建立在广泛采用的机器人技术之上，包括ROS2、MAVLink和MQTT。其设计允许使用相同的执行流程将相同的算法逻辑部署在完全仿真的环境中、软件在环配置中以及物理自动驾驶汽车中。该方法通过一系列实验得到验证，包括在自主水面舰艇上执行水质监测的真实部署，并使用实时传感器反馈。

TLDR: The paper presents GuadalPlanner, a ROS2-based unified architecture for informative path planning that enables consistent evaluation of algorithms across simulation and real-world deployment, validated on an autonomous surface vehicle.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一个名为GuadalPlanner的统一架构，该架构基于ROS2，用于信息路径规划，能够在仿真和实际部署中一致地评估算法，并在自主水面车辆上进行了验证。

Authors: Alejandro Mendoza Barrionuevo, Dame Seck Diop, Alejandro Casado Pérez, Daniel Gutiérrez Reina, Sergio L. Toral Marín, Samuel Yanes Luis

Assessing Vision-Language Models for Perception in Autonomous Underwater Robotic Software

Abstract (English): Autonomous Underwater Robots (AURs) operate in challenging underwater environments, including low visibility and harsh water conditions. Such conditions present challenges for software engineers developing perception modules for the AUR software. To successfully carry out these tasks, deep learning has been incorporated into the AUR software to support its operations. However, the unique challenges of underwater environments pose difficulties for deep learning models, which often rely on labeled data that is scarce and noisy. This may undermine the trustworthiness of AUR software that relies on perception modules. Vision-Language Models (VLMs) offer promising solutions for AUR software as they generalize to unseen objects and remain robust in noisy conditions by inferring information from contextual cues. Despite this potential, their performance and uncertainty in underwater environments remain understudied from a software engineering perspective. Motivated by the needs of an industrial partner in assurance and risk management for maritime systems to assess the potential use of VLMs in this context, we present an empirical evaluation of VLM-based perception modules within the AUR software. We assess their ability to detect underwater trash by computing performance, uncertainty, and their relationship, to enable software engineers to select appropriate VLMs for their AUR software.

摘要（中文）: 自动水下机器人（AURs）在充满挑战性的水下环境中运行，包括低能见度和恶劣的水况。这些条件对开发AUR软件感知模块的软件工程师提出了挑战。为了成功执行这些任务，深度学习已被纳入AUR软件以支持其运行。然而，水下环境的独特挑战给深度学习模型带来了困难，这些模型通常依赖于稀缺且嘈杂的已标注数据。这可能会削弱依赖于感知模块的AUR软件的可信度。视觉-语言模型（VLMs）为AUR软件提供了有前景的解决方案，因为它们可以推广到未见过的物体，并通过从上下文线索中推断信息，在嘈杂的环境中保持稳健性。尽管存在这种潜力，但从软件工程的角度来看，它们在水下环境中的性能和不确定性仍然研究不足。受到海事系统保障和风险管理领域工业合作伙伴的需求驱动，为了评估在此背景下VLMs的潜在用途，我们对基于VLMs的AUR软件感知模块进行了实证评估。我们通过计算性能、不确定性及其关系来评估它们检测水下垃圾的能力，从而使软件工程师能够为其AUR软件选择合适的VLMs。

TLDR: This paper empirically evaluates vision-language models (VLMs) for underwater trash detection in autonomous underwater robots (AURs), focusing on performance, uncertainty, and their relationship to aid software engineers in VLM selection.

简要说明: 本文对视觉-语言模型(VLMs)在自主水下机器人(AURs)中用于水下垃圾检测进行了实证评估，重点关注性能、不确定性及其关系，以帮助软件工程师选择合适的VLM。

Authors: Muhammad Yousaf, Aitor Arrieta, Shaukat Ali, Paolo Arcaini, Shuai Wang

DD-MDN: Human Trajectory Forecasting with Diffusion-Based Dual Mixture Density Networks and Uncertainty Self-Calibration

Abstract (English): Human Trajectory Forecasting (HTF) predicts future human movements from past trajectories and environmental context, with applications in Autonomous Driving, Smart Surveillance, and Human-Robot Interaction. While prior work has focused on accuracy, social interaction modeling, and diversity, little attention has been paid to uncertainty modeling, calibration, and forecasts from short observation periods, which are crucial for downstream tasks such as path planning and collision avoidance. We propose DD-MDN, an end-to-end probabilistic HTF model that combines high positional accuracy, calibrated uncertainty, and robustness to short observations. Using a few-shot denoising diffusion backbone and a dual mixture density network, our method learns self-calibrated residence areas and probability-ranked anchor paths, from which diverse trajectory hypotheses are derived, without predefined anchors or endpoints. Experiments on the ETH/UCY, SDD, inD, and IMPTC datasets demonstrate state-of-the-art accuracy, robustness at short observation intervals, and reliable uncertainty modeling. The code is available at: https://github.com/kav-institute/ddmdn.

摘要（中文）: 人类轨迹预测 (HTF) 旨在根据过往轨迹和环境背景预测未来的人类移动，在自动驾驶、智能监控和人机交互等领域有着广泛应用。 虽然先前的工作主要集中在精度、社交互动建模和多样性上，但对不确定性建模、校准以及从短观测期进行的预测关注较少，而这些对于下游任务（例如路径规划和避撞）至关重要。 我们提出了 DD-MDN，这是一个端到端概率 HTF 模型，它结合了高位置精度、校准后的不确定性以及对短观测的鲁棒性。 通过使用小样本去噪扩散骨干网络和双混合密度网络，我们的方法学习自校准的驻留区域和概率排序的锚点路径，从中可以导出多样化的轨迹假设，而无需预定义的锚点或终点。 在 ETH/UCY、SDD、inD 和 IMPTC 数据集上的实验证明了最先进的精度、在短观测间隔下的鲁棒性和可靠的不确定性建模。 代码可在以下网址获取：https://github.com/kav-institute/ddmdn。

TLDR: This paper introduces DD-MDN, a diffusion-based model for human trajectory forecasting that focuses on improved accuracy, calibrated uncertainty, and robustness to short observation periods, outperforming existing methods on standard datasets.

简要说明: 本文介绍了DD-MDN，一种基于扩散的人类轨迹预测模型，专注于提高准确性、校准不确定性和对短观测周期的鲁棒性，并在标准数据集上优于现有方法。

Authors: Manuel Hetzel, Kerim Turacan, Hannes Reichert, Konrad Doll, Bernhard Sick

Flow-Enabled Generalization to Human Demonstrations in Few-Shot Imitation Learning

Abstract (English): Imitation Learning (IL) enables robots to learn complex skills from demonstrations without explicit task modeling, but it typically requires large amounts of demonstrations, creating significant collection costs. Prior work has investigated using flow as an intermediate representation to enable the use of human videos as a substitute, thereby reducing the amount of required robot demonstrations. However, most prior work has focused on the flow, either on the object or on specific points of the robot/hand, which cannot describe the motion of interaction. Meanwhile, relying on flow to achieve generalization to scenarios observed only in human videos remains limited, as flow alone cannot capture precise motion details. Furthermore, conditioning on scene observation to produce precise actions may cause the flow-conditioned policy to overfit to training tasks and weaken the generalization indicated by the flow. To address these gaps, we propose SFCrP, which includes a Scene Flow prediction model for Cross-embodiment learning (SFCr) and a Flow and Cropped point cloud conditioned Policy (FCrP). SFCr learns from both robot and human videos and predicts any point trajectories. FCrP follows the general flow motion and adjusts the action based on observations for precision tasks. Our method outperforms SOTA baselines across various real-world task settings, while also exhibiting strong spatial and instance generalization to scenarios seen only in human videos.

摘要（中文）: 以下是翻译结果： 模仿学习(IL)使得机器人能够通过示教学习复杂的技能，而无需显式的任务建模，但它通常需要大量的示教，从而产生显著的收集成本。先前的工作已经研究了使用光流作为中间表示，以利用人类视频作为替代，从而减少所需的机器人示教数量。然而，大多数先前的工作都集中在光流上，或者是物体上的光流，或者是机器人/手的特定点上的光流，这无法描述交互的运动。同时，仅依靠光流来实现对仅在人类视频中观察到的场景的泛化仍然有限，因为光流本身无法捕捉精确的运动细节。此外，以场景观测为条件来产生精确动作可能会导致以光流为条件的策略过度拟合训练任务，并削弱光流所指示的泛化能力。为了解决这些差距，我们提出了SFCrP，它包括一个用于跨具身学习的场景光流预测模型(SFCr)和一个光流和裁剪点云条件策略(FCrP)。SFCr从机器人和人类视频中学习，并预测任何点轨迹。FCrP遵循通用光流运动，并根据观测调整动作以进行精确任务。我们的方法在各种真实世界任务设置中优于最先进的基线，同时还表现出对仅在人类视频中看到的场景的强大的空间和实例泛化能力。

Authors: Runze Tang, Penny Sweetser

Morphogenetic Assembly and Adaptive Control for Heterogeneous Modular Robots

Abstract (English): This paper presents a closed-loop automation framework for heterogeneous modular robots, covering the full pipeline from morphological construction to adaptive control. In this framework, a mobile manipulator handles heterogeneous functional modules including structural, joint, and wheeled modules to dynamically assemble diverse robot configurations and provide them with immediate locomotion capability. To address the state-space explosion in large-scale heterogeneous reconfiguration, we propose a hierarchical planner: the high-level planner uses a bidirectional heuristic search with type-penalty terms to generate module-handling sequences, while the low level planner employs A* search to compute optimal execution trajectories. This design effectively decouples discrete configuration planning from continuous motion execution. For adaptive motion generation of unknown assembled configurations, we introduce a GPU accelerated Annealing-Variance Model Predictive Path Integral (MPPI) controller. By incorporating a multi stage variance annealing strategy to balance global exploration and local convergence, the controller enables configuration-agnostic, real-time motion control. Large scale simulations show that the type-penalty term is critical for planning robustness in heterogeneous scenarios. Moreover, the greedy heuristic produces plans with lower physical execution costs than the Hungarian heuristic. The proposed annealing-variance MPPI significantly outperforms standard MPPI in both velocity tracking accuracy and control frequency, achieving real time control at 50 Hz. The framework validates the full-cycle process, including module assembly, robot merging and splitting, and dynamic motion generation.

摘要（中文）: 本文提出了一种用于异构模块化机器人的闭环自动化框架，涵盖了从形态构建到自适应控制的完整流程。在该框架中，移动机械臂操控包括结构模块、关节模块和轮式模块在内的异构功能模块，以动态组装各种机器人构型，并为其提供即时移动能力。为了解决大规模异构重构中的状态空间爆炸问题，我们提出了一种分层规划器：高层规划器采用带类型惩罚项的双向启发式搜索来生成模块操控序列，而低层规划器采用A*搜索来计算最优执行轨迹。这种设计有效地将离散构型规划与连续运动执行解耦。对于未知组装构型的自适应运动生成，我们引入了一种GPU加速的退火方差模型预测路径积分（MPPI）控制器。通过结合多阶段方差退火策略来平衡全局探索和局部收敛，该控制器能够实现构型无关的实时运动控制。大规模仿真表明，类型惩罚项对于异构场景中的规划鲁棒性至关重要。此外，贪婪启发式算法产生的规划比匈牙利启发式算法具有更低的物理执行成本。所提出的退火方差MPPI在速度跟踪精度和控制频率方面均显著优于标准MPPI，实现了50 Hz的实时控制。该框架验证了包括模块组装、机器人合并和拆分以及动态运动生成在内的完整周期过程。

TLDR: This paper introduces a closed-loop automation framework for heterogeneous modular robots, enabling dynamic assembly, adaptive control, and real-time motion generation via a hierarchical planner and an annealing-variance MPPI controller.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一个用于异构模块化机器人的闭环自动化框架，该框架通过分层规划器和退火方差MPPI控制器实现动态组装、自适应控制和实时运动生成。

Authors: Chongxi Meng, Da Zhao, Yifei Zhao, Minghao Zeng, Yanmin Zhou, Zhipeng Wang, Bin He

End-to-End LiDAR optimization for 3D point cloud registration

Abstract (English): LiDAR sensors are a key modality for 3D perception, yet they are typically designed independently of downstream tasks such as point cloud registration. Conventional registration operates on pre-acquired datasets with fixed LiDAR configurations, leading to suboptimal data collection and significant computational overhead for sampling, noise filtering, and parameter tuning. In this work, we propose an adaptive LiDAR sensing framework that dynamically adjusts sensor parameters, jointly optimizing LiDAR acquisition and registration hyperparameters. By integrating registration feedback into the sensing loop, our approach optimally balances point density, noise, and sparsity, improving registration accuracy and efficiency. Evaluations in the CARLA simulation demonstrate that our method outperforms fixed-parameter baselines while retaining generalization abilities, highlighting the potential of adaptive LiDAR for autonomous perception and robotic applications.

摘要（中文）: 激光雷达传感器是3D感知的一种关键模式，但通常其设计与点云配准等下游任务是独立进行的。传统的配准操作采用具有固定激光雷达配置的预先采集的数据集，导致次优的数据采集以及在采样、噪声滤波和参数调整方面产生显著的计算开销。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种自适应激光雷达感知框架，它动态地调整传感器参数，联合优化激光雷达采集和配准超参数。通过将配准反馈集成到感知循环中，我们的方法能够优化平衡点密度、噪声和稀疏性，从而提高配准精度和效率。在CARLA模拟环境中的评估表明，我们的方法优于固定参数的基线方法，同时保留了泛化能力，突出了自适应激光雷达在自主感知和机器人应用中的潜力。

Authors: Siddhant Katyan, Marc-André Gardner, Jean-François Lalonde

Decoupled MPPI-Based Multi-Arm Motion Planning

Abstract (English): Recent advances in sampling-based motion planning algorithms for high DOF arms leverage GPUs to provide SOTA performance. These algorithms can be used to control multiple arms jointly, but this approach scales poorly. To address this, we extend STORM, a sampling-based model-predictive-control (MPC) motion planning algorithm, to handle multiple robots in a distributed fashion. First, we modify STORM to handle dynamic obstacles. Then, we let each arm compute its own motion plan prefix, which it shares with the other arms, which treat it as a dynamic obstacle. Finally, we add a dynamic priority scheme. The new algorithm, MR-STORM, demonstrates clear empirical advantages over SOTA algorithms when operating with both static and dynamic obstacles.

摘要（中文）: 针对高自由度机械臂的基于采样的运动规划算法的最新进展利用 GPU 实现了最先进的性能。这些算法可以用于联合控制多个机械臂，但这种方法的可扩展性很差。为了解决这个问题，我们扩展了 STORM，一种基于采样的模型预测控制 (MPC) 运动规划算法，使其能够以分布式的方式处理多个机器人。首先，我们修改 STORM 以处理动态障碍物。然后，我们让每个机械臂计算其自身运动计划的前缀，并与其他机械臂共享，其他机械臂将其视为动态障碍物。最后，我们添加了一种动态优先级方案。新的算法 MR-STORM 在存在静态和动态障碍物时，与最先进的算法相比，表现出明显的经验优势。

TLDR: The paper introduces MR-STORM, a distributed, sampling-based MPC motion planning algorithm that efficiently controls multiple arms with dynamic obstacles, demonstrating advantages over existing methods.

Authors: Dan Evron, Elias Goldsztejn, Ronen I. Brafman

Learning Agile Quadrotor Flight in the Real World

Abstract (English): Learning-based controllers have achieved impressive performance in agile quadrotor flight but typically rely on massive training in simulation, necessitating accurate system identification for effective Sim2Real transfer. However, even with precise modeling, fixed policies remain susceptible to out-of-distribution scenarios, ranging from external aerodynamic disturbances to internal hardware degradation. To ensure safety under these evolving uncertainties, such controllers are forced to operate with conservative safety margins, inherently constraining their agility outside of controlled settings. While online adaptation offers a potential remedy, safely exploring physical limits remains a critical bottleneck due to data scarcity and safety risks. To bridge this gap, we propose a self-adaptive framework that eliminates the need for precise system identification or offline Sim2Real transfer. We introduce Adaptive Temporal Scaling (ATS) to actively explore platform physical limits, and employ online residual learning to augment a simple nominal model. {Based on the learned hybrid model, we further propose Real-world Anchored Short-horizon Backpropagation Through Time (RASH-BPTT) to achieve efficient and robust in-flight policy updates. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our quadrotor reliably executes agile maneuvers near actuator saturation limits. The system evolves a conservative base policy with a peak speed of 1.9 m/s to 7.3 m/s within approximately 100 seconds of flight time. These findings underscore that real-world adaptation serves not merely to compensate for modeling errors, but as a practical mechanism for sustained performance improvement in aggressive flight regimes.

摘要（中文）: 基于学习的控制器在敏捷四旋翼飞行中取得了令人印象深刻的性能，但通常依赖于大规模的仿真训练，因此需要精确的系统辨识来实现有效的Sim2Real迁移。然而，即使使用精确的建模，固定的策略仍然容易受到分布外场景的影响，例如外部空气动力干扰或内部硬件退化。为了在这些不断演变的不确定性下确保安全，此类控制器被迫采用保守的安全裕度，从而固有地限制了它们在受控环境之外的敏捷性。虽然在线自适应提供了一种可能的补救方法，但由于数据稀缺和安全风险，安全地探索物理极限仍然是一个关键瓶颈。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了一种自适应框架，该框架消除了对精确系统辨识或离线Sim2Real迁移的需求。我们引入了自适应时间尺度调整(ATS)来主动探索平台的物理极限，并采用在线残差学习来增强一个简单的标称模型。基于学习到的混合模型，我们进一步提出了真实世界锚定的短时回溯时间反向传播(RASH-BPTT)，以实现高效和鲁棒的飞行中策略更新。大量的实验表明，我们的四旋翼可靠地执行接近执行器饱和极限的敏捷动作。该系统在大约100秒的飞行时间内，将具有1.9米/秒峰值速度的保守基础策略演进到7.3米/秒。这些发现强调，真实世界的自适应不仅仅是用于补偿建模误差，而且还是在激进飞行状态下持续提高性能的实用机制。

TLDR: This paper presents a self-adaptive framework for agile quadrotor flight that eliminates the need for precise system identification or offline Sim2Real transfer using Adaptive Temporal Scaling (ATS) and Real-world Anchored Short-horizon Backpropagation Through Time (RASH-BPTT), achieving significant performance improvements in real-world experiments.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种用于敏捷四旋翼飞行的自适应框架，无需精确的系统辨识或离线Sim2Real迁移，通过自适应时间缩放 (ATS) 和实物锚定的短时反向传播 (RASH-BPTT)，在真实世界的实验中实现了显著的性能提升。

Authors: Yunfan Ren, Zhiyuan Zhu, Jiaxu Xing, Davide Scaramuzza

Humanoid Factors: Design Principles for AI Humanoids in Human Worlds

Abstract (English): Human factors research has long focused on optimizing environments, tools, and systems to account for human performance. Yet, as humanoid robots begin to share our workplaces, homes, and public spaces, the design challenge expands. We must now consider not only factors for humans but also factors for humanoids, since both will coexist and interact within the same environments. Unlike conventional machines, humanoids introduce expectations of human-like behavior, communication, and social presence, which reshape usability, trust, and safety considerations. In this article, we introduce the concept of humanoid factors as a framework structured around four pillars - physical, cognitive, social, and ethical - that shape the development of humanoids to help them effectively coexist and collaborate with humans. This framework characterizes the overlap and divergence between human capabilities and those of general-purpose humanoids powered by AI foundation models. To demonstrate our framework's practical utility, we then apply the framework to evaluate a real-world humanoid control algorithm, illustrating how conventional task completion metrics in robotics overlook key human cognitive and interaction principles. We thus position humanoid factors as a foundational framework for designing, evaluating, and governing sustained human-humanoid coexistence.

摘要（中文）: 人类工效学研究长期以来一直致力于优化环境、工具和系统，以适应人类表现。然而，随着人形机器人开始进入我们的工作场所、家庭和公共空间，设计挑战也随之扩大。我们现在不仅要考虑人类的因素，还要考虑人形机器人的因素，因为两者将在相同的环境中共存和互动。与传统机器不同，人形机器人会引发对类人行为、沟通和社会存在的期望，从而重塑了可用性、信任和安全方面的考虑。在本文中，我们引入了“人形机器人因素”的概念，作为一个围绕四个支柱——物理、认知、社会和伦理——构建的框架，旨在塑造人形机器人的发展，以帮助它们有效地与人类共存和协作。该框架刻画了人类能力与由人工智能基础模型驱动的通用人形机器人能力之间的重叠和差异。为了展示我们框架的实际效用，我们随后应用该框架来评估一个真实世界的人形机器人控制算法，说明了机器人学中传统的任务完成指标如何忽略了关键的人类认知和交互原则。因此，我们将“人形机器人因素”定位为设计、评估和管理可持续的人人-人机共存的基础框架。

Authors: Xinyuan Liu, Eren Sadikoglu, Ransalu Senanayake, Lixiao Huang

General Flexible $f$-divergence for Challenging Offline RL Datasets with Low Stochasticity and Diverse Behavior Policies

Abstract (English): Offline RL algorithms aim to improve upon the behavior policy that produces the collected data while constraining the learned policy to be within the support of the dataset. However, practical offline datasets often contain examples with little diversity or limited exploration of the environment, and from multiple behavior policies with diverse expertise levels. Limited exploration can impair the offline RL algorithm's ability to estimate \textit{Q} or \textit{V} values, while constraining towards diverse behavior policies can be overly conservative. Such datasets call for a balance between the RL objective and behavior policy constraints. We first identify the connection between $f$-divergence and optimization constraint on the Bellman residual through a more general Linear Programming form for RL and the convex conjugate. Following this, we introduce the general flexible function formulation for the $f$-divergence to incorporate an adaptive constraint on algorithms' learning objectives based on the offline training dataset. Results from experiments on the MuJoCo, Fetch, and AdroitHand environments show the correctness of the proposed LP form and the potential of the flexible $f$-divergence in improving performance for learning from a challenging dataset when applied to a compatible constrained optimization algorithm.

摘要（中文）: 离线强化学习算法旨在改进生成已收集数据的行为策略，同时约束学习到的策略在数据集的支持范围内。然而，实际的离线数据集通常包含多样性不足或对环境探索有限的样本，以及来自具有不同专业知识水平的多种行为策略的样本。有限的探索可能会削弱离线强化学习算法估计 *Q* 值或 *V* 值的能力，而约束于多种行为策略可能过于保守。这类数据集需要权衡强化学习目标和行为策略约束。我们首先通过更通用的强化学习线性规划形式和凸共轭，确定了 $f$-散度与贝尔曼残差优化约束之间的联系。在此基础上，我们引入了用于 $f$-散度的一般灵活函数形式，以便基于离线训练数据集将自适应约束纳入算法的学习目标中。在 MuJoCo、Fetch 和 AdroitHand 环境中的实验结果表明，所提出的线性规划形式的正确性以及灵活 $f$-散度应用于兼容的约束优化算法时，在具有挑战性的数据集上学习时提高性能的潜力。

TLDR: This paper introduces a general flexible f-divergence for offline RL to address challenges posed by datasets with low stochasticity and diverse behavior policies, demonstrating improved performance on MuJoCo, Fetch, and AdroitHand environments.

Authors: Jianxun Wang, Grant C. Forbes, Leonardo Villalobos-Arias, David L. Roberts

Interpretable Attention-Based Multi-Agent PPO for Latency Spike Resolution in 6G RAN Slicing

Abstract (English): Sixth-generation (6G) radio access networks (RANs) must enforce strict service-level agreements (SLAs) for heterogeneous slices, yet sudden latency spikes remain difficult to diagnose and resolve with conventional deep reinforcement learning (DRL) or explainable RL (XRL). We propose \emph{Attention-Enhanced Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (AE-MAPPO)}, which integrates six specialized attention mechanisms into multi-agent slice control and surfaces them as zero-cost, faithful explanations. The framework operates across O-RAN timescales with a three-phase strategy: predictive, reactive, and inter-slice optimization. A URLLC case study shows AE-MAPPO resolves a latency spike in $18$ms, restores latency to $0.98$ms with $99.9999\%$ reliability, and reduces troubleshooting time by $93\%$ while maintaining eMBB and mMTC continuity. These results confirm AE-MAPPO's ability to combine SLA compliance with inherent interpretability, enabling trustworthy and real-time automation for 6G RAN slicing.

摘要（中文）: 第六代(6G)无线接入网络(RAN)必须对异构切片强制执行严格的服务级别协议(SLA)，但传统的深度强化学习(DRL)或可解释强化学习(XRL)仍然难以诊断和解决突发的延迟峰值。我们提出了一种\emph{注意力增强的多智能体近端策略优化(AE-MAPPO)}，它将六种专门的注意力机制集成到多智能体切片控制中，并将其作为零成本、忠实的解释呈现出来。该框架在O-RAN时间尺度上运行，采用三阶段策略：预测、反应和切片间优化。 一个URLLC案例研究表明，AE-MAPPO在$18$毫秒内解决了延迟峰值，以$99.9999\%$的可靠性将延迟恢复到$0.98$毫秒，并将故障排除时间减少了$93\%$，同时保持了eMBB和mMTC的连续性。这些结果证实了AE-MAPPO能够将SLA合规性与固有的可解释性相结合，从而为6G RAN切片实现可信赖的实时自动化。

TLDR: This paper introduces Attention-Enhanced Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (AE-MAPPO) for resolving latency spikes in 6G RAN slicing, claiming significant improvements in real-time performance and interpretability compared to traditional methods.

Authors: Kavan Fatehi, Mostafa Rahmani Ghourtani, Amir Sonee, Poonam Yadav, Alessandra M Russo, Hamed Ahmadi, Radu Calinescu

Chain-of-Look Spatial Reasoning for Dense Surgical Instrument Counting

Abstract (English): Accurate counting of surgical instruments in Operating Rooms (OR) is a critical prerequisite for ensuring patient safety during surgery. Despite recent progress of large visual-language models and agentic AI, accurately counting such instruments remains highly challenging, particularly in dense scenarios where instruments are tightly clustered. To address this problem, we introduce Chain-of-Look, a novel visual reasoning framework that mimics the sequential human counting process by enforcing a structured visual chain, rather than relying on classic object detection which is unordered. This visual chain guides the model to count along a coherent spatial trajectory, improving accuracy in complex scenes. To further enforce the physical plausibility of the visual chain, we introduce the neighboring loss function, which explicitly models the spatial constraints inherent to densely packed surgical instruments. We also present SurgCount-HD, a new dataset comprising 1,464 high-density surgical instrument images. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method outperforms state-of-the-art approaches for counting (e.g., CountGD, REC) as well as Multimodality Large Language Models (e.g., Qwen, ChatGPT) in the challenging task of dense surgical instrument counting.

摘要（中文）: 手术室（OR）中对手术器械的准确计数是确保患者手术安全的关键先决条件。尽管大型视觉-语言模型和智能体AI最近取得了进展，但准确计数此类器械仍然极具挑战性，尤其是在器械紧密聚集的密集场景中。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了Chain-of-Look，一个新颖的视觉推理框架，它通过强制执行结构化的视觉链来模拟人类连续的计数过程，而不是依赖于无序的经典目标检测。该视觉链引导模型沿着连贯的空间轨迹进行计数，从而提高复杂场景中的准确性。为了进一步加强视觉链的物理合理性，我们引入了邻域损失函数，该函数明确地对密集堆叠手术器械固有的空间约束进行建模。我们还提出了SurgCount-HD，一个包含1,464张高密度手术器械图像的新数据集。大量实验表明，在具有挑战性的密集手术器械计数任务中，我们的方法优于最先进的计数方法（例如，CountGD、REC）以及多模态大型语言模型（例如，Qwen、ChatGPT）。

TLDR: This paper introduces a novel "Chain-of-Look" spatial reasoning framework for accurate surgical instrument counting in dense operating room scenarios, outperforming SOTA counting methods and Multimodality Large Language Models.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为“Chain-of-Look”的新型空间推理框架，用于在密集的的手术室场景中准确计数手术器械，其性能优于当前最先进的计数方法和多模态大型语言模型。

Authors: Rishikesh Bhyri, Brian R Quaranto, Philip J Seger, Kaity Tung, Brendan Fox, Gene Yang, Steven D. Schwaitzberg, Junsong Yuan, Nan Xi, Peter C W Kim

OSIL: Learning Offline Safe Imitation Policies with Safety Inferred from Non-preferred Trajectories

Abstract (English): This work addresses the problem of offline safe imitation learning (IL), where the goal is to learn safe and reward-maximizing policies from demonstrations that do not have per-timestep safety cost or reward information. In many real-world domains, online learning in the environment can be risky, and specifying accurate safety costs can be difficult. However, it is often feasible to collect trajectories that reflect undesirable or unsafe behavior, implicitly conveying what the agent should avoid. We refer to these as non-preferred trajectories. We propose a novel offline safe IL algorithm, OSIL, that infers safety from non-preferred demonstrations. We formulate safe policy learning as a Constrained Markov Decision Process (CMDP). Instead of relying on explicit safety cost and reward annotations, OSIL reformulates the CMDP problem by deriving a lower bound on reward maximizing objective and learning a cost model that estimates the likelihood of non-preferred behavior. Our approach allows agents to learn safe and reward-maximizing behavior entirely from offline demonstrations. We empirically demonstrate that our approach can learn safer policies that satisfy cost constraints without degrading the reward performance, thus outperforming several baselines.

摘要（中文）: 本研究探讨了离线安全模仿学习（IL）问题，目标是从缺乏每步安全性代价或奖励信息的示范轨迹中学习安全且奖励最大化的策略。在许多现实世界领域，环境中的在线学习可能存在风险，并且指定准确的安全性代价也可能很困难。然而，通常可以收集反映不良或不安全行为的轨迹，从而隐式地传达智能体应避免的内容。我们将这些称为非首选轨迹。我们提出了一种新颖的离线安全IL算法，OSIL，通过非首选示范轨迹推断安全性。我们将安全策略学习形式化为一个约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDP）。OSIL没有依赖显式的安全性代价和奖励标注，而是通过推导最大化奖励目标的下界并学习一个估计非首选行为可能性的代价模型，来重新构建CMDP问题。我们的方法允许智能体完全从离线示范轨迹中学习安全且奖励最大化的行为。我们通过实验证明，我们的方法可以学习更安全的策略，在不降低奖励性能的情况下满足代价约束，从而优于多个基线方法。

TLDR: The paper introduces OSIL, an offline safe imitation learning algorithm that learns safe and reward-maximizing policies from demonstrations and non-preferred trajectories, inferring safety without explicit cost annotations.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 OSIL，一种离线安全模仿学习算法，通过演示和非首选轨迹学习安全且奖励最大化的策略，无需明确的成本注释即可推断安全性。

Authors: Returaj Burnwal, Nirav Pravinbhai Bhatt, Balaraman Ravindran

CLI-Gym: Scalable CLI Task Generation via Agentic Environment Inversion

Abstract (English): Agentic coding requires agents to effectively interact with runtime environments, e.g., command line interfaces (CLI), so as to complete tasks like resolving dependency issues, fixing system problems, etc. But it remains underexplored how such environment-intensive tasks can be obtained at scale to enhance agents' capabilities. To address this, based on an analogy between the Dockerfile and the agentic task, we propose to employ agents to simulate and explore environment histories, guided by execution feedback. By tracing histories of a healthy environment, its state can be inverted to an earlier one with runtime failures, from which a task can be derived by packing the buggy state and the corresponding error messages. With our method, named CLI-Gym, a total of 1,655 environment-intensive tasks are derived, being the largest collection of its kind. Moreover, with curated successful trajectories, our fine-tuned model, named LiberCoder, achieves substantial absolute improvements of +21.1% (to 46.1%) on Terminal-Bench, outperforming various strong baselines. To our knowledge, this is the first public pipeline for scalable derivation of environment-intensive tasks.

摘要（中文）: 自主编码要求智能体能够有效地与运行时环境交互，例如命令行界面 (CLI)，从而完成诸如解决依赖问题、修复系统问题等任务。但如何在规模上获取此类环境密集型任务以增强智能体的能力仍然未被充分探索。为了解决这个问题，基于 Dockerfile 和自主任务之间的类比，我们提出使用智能体来模拟和探索环境历史，并以执行反馈为指导。通过追踪健康环境的历史，其状态可以反转到带有运行时故障的早期状态，从中可以通过打包错误状态和相应的错误消息来派生出一个任务。利用我们名为 CLI-Gym 的方法，一共派生出了 1,655 个环境密集型任务，这是同类任务中规模最大的集合。此外，凭借精心策划的成功轨迹，我们微调后的模型 LiberCoder 在 Terminal-Bench 上取得了显著的绝对提升（+21.1%，达到 46.1%），优于各种强大的基线模型。据我们所知，这是首个用于大规模派生环境密集型任务的公开流程。

TLDR: The paper introduces CLI-Gym, a pipeline for generating environment-intensive tasks for agentic coding by inverting environment states, and demonstrates its effectiveness by fine-tuning LiberCoder which achieves significant improvements on Terminal-Bench.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了CLI-Gym，一种通过反转环境状态来生成智能编码的环境密集型任务的流程，并通过微调LiberCoder展示了其有效性， LiberCoder在Terminal-Bench上取得了显著的改进。

Authors: Yusong Lin, Haiyang Wang, Shuzhe Wu, Lue Fan, Feiyang Pan, Sanyuan Zhao, Dandan Tu

Resource-Efficient Model-Free Reinforcement Learning for Board Games

Abstract (English): Board games have long served as complex decision-making benchmarks in artificial intelligence. In this field, search-based reinforcement learning methods such as AlphaZero have achieved remarkable success. However, their significant computational demands have been pointed out as barriers to their reproducibility. In this study, we propose a model-free reinforcement learning algorithm designed for board games to achieve more efficient learning. To validate the efficiency of the proposed method, we conducted comprehensive experiments on five board games: Animal Shogi, Gardner Chess, Go, Hex, and Othello. The results demonstrate that the proposed method achieves more efficient learning than existing methods across these environments. In addition, our extensive ablation study shows the importance of core techniques used in the proposed method. We believe that our efficient algorithm shows the potential of model-free reinforcement learning in domains traditionally dominated by search-based methods.

摘要（中文）: 棋盘游戏长期以来一直是人工智能领域复杂决策制定的基准。在该领域，诸如AlphaZero等基于搜索的强化学习方法已取得显著成功。然而，其巨大的计算需求已被指出是其可复现性的障碍。在本研究中，我们提出了一种专为棋盘游戏设计的、无需模型的强化学习算法，以实现更高效的学习。为了验证所提出方法的效率，我们在五种棋盘游戏上进行了全面的实验：动物将棋、加德纳象棋、围棋、六贯棋和奥赛罗。结果表明，在这些环境中，所提出的方法比现有方法实现了更高效的学习。此外，我们广泛的消融研究表明了所提出方法中使用的核心技术的重要性。我们相信，我们高效的算法展示了无需模型的强化学习在传统上由基于搜索的方法主导的领域中的潜力。

TLDR: This paper introduces a resource-efficient, model-free reinforcement learning algorithm for board games, demonstrating improved learning efficiency compared to existing methods like AlphaZero, with extensive experiments on five different games.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种资源高效的，不基于模型的强化学习算法，用于棋盘游戏，并在五种不同的游戏中进行了广泛的实验，结果表明，与 AlphaZero 等现有方法相比，该算法具有更高的学习效率。

Authors: Kazuki Ota, Takayuki Osa, Motoki Omura, Tatsuya Harada

See, Plan, Snap: Evaluating Multimodal GUI Agents in Scratch

Abstract (English): Block-based programming environments such as Scratch play a central role in low-code education, yet evaluating the capabilities of AI agents to construct programs through Graphical User Interfaces (GUIs) remains underexplored. We introduce ScratchWorld, a benchmark for evaluating multimodal GUI agents on program-by-construction tasks in Scratch. Grounded in the Use-Modify-Create pedagogical framework, ScratchWorld comprises 83 curated tasks spanning four distinct problem categories: Create, Debug, Extend, and Compute. To rigorously diagnose the source of agent failures, the benchmark employs two complementary interaction modes: primitive mode requires fine-grained drag-and-drop manipulation to directly assess visuomotor control, while composite mode uses high-level semantic APIs to disentangle program reasoning from GUI execution. To ensure reliable assessment, we propose an execution-based evaluation protocol that validates the functional correctness of the constructed Scratch programs through runtime tests within the browser environment. Extensive experiments across state-of-the-art multimodal language models and GUI agents reveal a substantial reasoning--acting gap, highlighting persistent challenges in fine-grained GUI manipulation despite strong planning capabilities.

摘要（中文）: 基于Scratch等块状编程环境在低代码教育中发挥着核心作用，然而，评估人工智能体通过图形用户界面（GUI）构建程序的能力仍然未被充分探索。我们引入ScratchWorld，这是一个benchmark，用于评估多模态GUI智能体在Scratch中基于程序构建任务的表现。ScratchWorld基于Use-Modify-Create教学框架，包含83个精选任务，涵盖四个不同的问题类别：创建、调试、扩展和计算。为了严格诊断智能体失败的根源，该benchmark采用两种互补的交互模式：原始模式需要细粒度的拖放操作来直接评估视觉运动控制，而组合模式则使用高级语义API来将程序推理与GUI执行分离。为确保可靠的评估，我们提出了一种基于执行的评估协议，该协议通过浏览器环境中的运行时测试来验证构建的Scratch程序的功能正确性。对最先进的多模态语言模型和GUI智能体进行的大量实验表明，存在显著的推理-行动差距，突出了尽管拥有强大的规划能力，但在细粒度GUI操作方面仍然存在持续的挑战。

TLDR: The paper introduces ScratchWorld, a benchmark for evaluating multimodal GUI agents that construct programs in Scratch, using two interaction modes and an execution-based evaluation protocol to diagnose agent failures and reveal challenges in GUI manipulation.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ScratchWorld，一个用于评估多模态GUI智能体在Scratch中构建程序的基准。它采用两种交互模式和一个基于执行的评估协议来诊断智能体故障，并揭示GUI操作中的挑战。

Authors: Xingyi Zhang, Yulei Ye, Kaifeng Huang, Wenhao Li, Xiangfeng Wang

Improving Medical Visual Reinforcement Fine-Tuning via Perception and Reasoning Augmentation

Abstract (English): While recent advances in Reinforcement Fine-Tuning (RFT) have shown that rule-based reward schemes can enable effective post-training for large language models, their extension to cross-modal, vision-centric domains remains largely underexplored. This limitation is especially pronounced in the medical imaging domain, where effective performance requires both robust visual perception and structured reasoning. In this work, we address this gap by proposing VRFT-Aug, a visual reinforcement fine-tuning framework tailored for the medical domain. VRFT-Aug introduces a series of training strategies designed to augment both perception and reasoning, including prior knowledge injection, perception-driven policy refinement, medically informed reward shaping, and behavioral imitation. Together, these methods aim to stabilize and improve the RFT process. Through extensive experiments across multiple medical datasets, we show that our approaches consistently outperform both standard supervised fine-tuning and RFT baselines. Moreover, we provide empirically grounded insights and practical training heuristics that can be generalized to other medical image tasks. We hope this work contributes actionable guidance and fresh inspiration for the ongoing effort to develop reliable, reasoning-capable models for high-stakes medical applications.

摘要（中文）: 虽然最近在强化精调(RFT)方面的进展表明，基于规则的奖励机制可以为大型语言模型实现有效的后训练，但它们在跨模态、以视觉为中心的领域中的扩展仍很大程度上未被探索。这种局限性在医学影像领域尤为突出，因为有效的性能既需要强大的视觉感知能力，也需要结构化的推理能力。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种专为医学领域定制的视觉强化精调框架VRFT-Aug，以弥补这一差距。VRFT-Aug引入了一系列旨在增强感知和推理能力的训练策略，包括先验知识注入、感知驱动的策略优化、医学信息指导的奖励塑造以及行为模仿。这些方法共同旨在稳定和改进RFT过程。 通过在多个医学数据集上进行的大量实验，我们表明我们的方法始终优于标准的监督精调和RFT基线。此外，我们提供了以实证为基础的见解和实用的训练启发式方法，这些方法可以推广到其他医学图像任务。我们希望这项工作能够为开发用于高风险医疗应用的可信赖、具有推理能力的模型提供可操作的指导和新的灵感。

TLDR: The paper introduces VRFT-Aug, a visual reinforcement fine-tuning framework designed to improve the performance of large language models in medical imaging by augmenting perception and reasoning capabilities. It demonstrates improved performance compared to standard fine-tuning and RFT baselines across multiple medical datasets.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了VRFT-Aug，一个视觉强化微调框架，旨在通过增强感知和推理能力来提高大型语言模型在医学图像处理中的性能。实验表明，与标准的微调和RFT基线相比，VRFT-Aug在多个医学数据集上表现更佳。

Authors: Guangjing Yang, ZhangYuan Yu, Ziyuan Qin, Xinyuan Song, Huahui Yi, Qingbo Kang, Jun Gao, Yiyue Li, Chenlin Du, Qicheng Lao

AIvilization v0: Toward Large-Scale Artificial Social Simulation with a Unified Agent Architecture and Adaptive Agent Profiles

Abstract (English): AIvilization v0 is a publicly deployed large-scale artificial society that couples a resource-constrained sandbox economy with a unified LLM-agent architecture, aiming to sustain long-horizon autonomy while remaining executable under rapidly changing environment. To mitigate the tension between goal stability and reactive correctness, we introduce (i) a hierarchical branch-thinking planner that decomposes life goals into parallel objective branches and uses simulation-guided validation plus tiered re-planning to ensure feasibility; (ii) an adaptive agent profile with dual-process memory that separates short-term execution traces from long-term semantic consolidation, enabling persistent yet evolving identity; and (iii) a human-in-the-loop steering interface that injects long-horizon objectives and short commands at appropriate abstraction levels, with effects propagated through memory rather than brittle prompt overrides. The environment integrates physiological survival costs, non-substitutable multi-tier production, an AMM-based price mechanism, and a gated education-occupation system. Using high-frequency transactions from the platforms mature phase, we find stable markets that reproduce key stylized facts (heavy-tailed returns and volatility clustering) and produce structured wealth stratification driven by education and access constraints. Ablations show simplified planners can match performance on narrow tasks, while the full architecture is more robust under multi-objective, long-horizon settings, supporting delayed investment and sustained exploration.

摘要（中文）: AIvilization v0是一个公开部署的大规模人工社会，它将资源受限的沙盒经济与统一的LLM-Agent架构相结合，旨在维持长时程的自主性，同时在快速变化的环境下保持可执行性。为了缓解目标稳定性和反应正确性之间的冲突，我们引入了：（i）一种分层分支思维规划器，将生命目标分解为并行的目标分支，并使用模拟引导的验证和分层重新规划来确保可行性；（ii）一种具有双过程记忆的自适应 Agent 配置文件，将短期执行轨迹与长期语义整合分离，从而实现持久而不断演变的身份；以及（iii）一个人在环路中的引导界面，该界面在适当的抽象级别注入长时程目标和短指令，其效果通过记忆传播，而非脆弱的提示覆盖。环境集成了生理生存成本、不可替代的多层生产、基于 AMM 的价格机制以及门控教育-职业系统。通过使用平台成熟期的高频交易数据，我们发现稳定的市场能够重现关键的程式化事实（重尾收益和波动率聚集），并产生由教育和准入限制驱动的结构化财富分层。消融实验表明，简化的规划器可以在狭窄的任务上匹配性能，而完整的架构在多目标、长时程设置下更具鲁棒性，支持延迟投资和持续探索。

TLDR: The paper introduces AIvilization v0, a large-scale artificial society with LLM-agents in a resource-constrained environment, featuring a hierarchical planner, adaptive agent profiles, and human-in-the-loop steering. It demonstrates stable markets and wealth stratification.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了AIvilization v0，一个大规模的人工社会，其中的LLM智能体在资源受限的环境中运行。它具有分层规划器，自适应智能体配置文件和人机回路指导。 结果表明，市场稳定，且财富分层。

Authors: Wenkai Fan, Shurui Zhang, Xiaolong Wang, Haowei Yang, Tsz Wai Chan, Xingyan Chen, Junquan Bi, Zirui Zhou, Jia Liu, Kani Chen

Blockwise Advantage Estimation for Multi-Objective RL with Verifiable Rewards

Abstract (English): Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) assigns a single scalar advantage to all tokens in a completion. For structured generations with explicit segments and objectives, this couples unrelated reward signals across segments, leading to objective interference and misattributed credit. We propose Blockwise Advantage Estimation, a family of GRPO-compatible methods that assigns each objective its own advantage and applies it only to the tokens in the corresponding text block, reducing reliance on hand-designed scalar rewards and scaling naturally to additional objectives. A key challenge is estimating advantages for later blocks whose rewards are conditioned on sampled prefixes; standard unbiased approaches require expensive nested rollouts from intermediate states. Concretely, we introduce an Outcome-Conditioned Baseline that approximates intermediate state values using only within-group statistics by stratifying samples according to a prefix-derived intermediate outcome. On math tasks with uncertainty estimation, our method mitigates reward interference, is competitive with a state-of-the-art reward-designed approach, and preserves test-time gains from confidence-weighted ensembling. More broadly, it provides a modular recipe for optimizing sequential objectives in structured generations without additional rollouts.

摘要（中文）: 群体相对策略优化（GRPO）为补全序列中的所有token分配一个单独的标量优势值。对于具有显式片段和目标的结构化生成，这会将不相关的奖励信号跨片段耦合，导致目标干扰和错误的信用归属。我们提出分块优势估计，这是一个与GRPO兼容的方法族，它为每个目标分配其自己的优势值，并仅将其应用于相应文本块中的token，从而减少对手工设计的标量奖励的依赖，并自然地扩展到更多目标。一个关键挑战是估计后续块的优势值，这些块的奖励取决于采样的前缀；标准无偏方法需要从中间状态进行昂贵的嵌套展开。具体来说，我们引入了结果条件基线，它仅使用组内统计信息，通过根据前缀派生的中间结果对样本进行分层，从而近似中间状态值。在具有不确定性估计的数学任务上，我们的方法减轻了奖励干扰，与最先进的奖励设计方法具有竞争力，并保留了来自置信度加权集成的测试时增益。更广泛地说，它为优化结构化生成中的顺序目标提供了一种模块化的方法，无需额外的展开。

TLDR: This paper introduces Blockwise Advantage Estimation for multi-objective RL, addressing reward interference in structured generation tasks by assigning separate advantages to different objectives and text blocks, achieving competitive results on math tasks without additional rollouts.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了用于多目标强化学习的块状优势评估方法，通过为不同的目标和文本块分配单独的优势，解决了结构化生成任务中的奖励干扰问题，并在数学任务上取得了具有竞争力的结果，且无需额外的rollout。

Authors: Kirill Pavlenko, Alexander Golubev, Simon Karasik, Boris Yangel

Internalizing Meta-Experience into Memory for Guided Reinforcement Learning in Large Language Models

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has emerged as an effective approach for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). Despite its efficacy, RLVR faces a meta-learning bottleneck: it lacks mechanisms for error attribution and experience internalization intrinsic to the human learning cycle beyond practice and verification, thereby limiting fine-grained credit assignment and reusable knowledge formation. We term such reusable knowledge representations derived from past errors as meta-experience. Based on this insight, we propose Meta-Experience Learning (MEL), a novel framework that incorporates self-distilled meta-experience into the model's parametric memory. Building upon standard RLVR, we introduce an additional design that leverages the LLM's self-verification capability to conduct contrastive analysis on paired correct and incorrect trajectories, identify the precise bifurcation points where reasoning errors arise, and summarize them into generalizable meta-experience. The meta-experience is further internalized into the LLM's parametric memory by minimizing the negative log-likelihood, which induces a language-modeled reward signal that bridges correct and incorrect reasoning trajectories and facilitates effective knowledge reuse. Experimental results demonstrate that MEL achieves consistent improvements on benchmarks, yielding 3.92%--4.73% Pass@1 gains across varying model sizes.

摘要（中文）: 具有可验证奖励的强化学习 (RLVR) 已经成为一种增强大型语言模型 (LLM) 推理能力的有效方法。尽管其有效，但 RLVR 面临一个元学习瓶颈：它缺乏归因错误和内化经验的机制，而这两种机制是人类学习周期中超越实践和验证所固有的，从而限制了细粒度的信用分配和可重用的知识形成。我们将从过去错误中提取的这种可重用的知识表示称为元经验。基于此洞察，我们提出了元经验学习 (MEL)，这是一个新颖的框架，它将自提炼的元经验纳入模型的参数记忆中。在标准 RLVR 的基础上，我们引入了一个额外的设计，利用 LLM 的自验证能力对配对的正确和错误轨迹进行对比分析，识别推理错误产生的精确分叉点，并将其总结为可泛化的元经验。通过最小化负对数似然，元经验会被进一步内化到 LLM 的参数记忆中，从而引发一种语言建模的奖励信号，该信号连接了正确和错误的推理轨迹，并促进了有效知识的重用。实验结果表明，MEL 在基准测试中取得了持续的提升，在不同的模型规模下实现了 3.92%--4.73% 的 Pass@1 得分提升。

TLDR: The paper introduces Meta-Experience Learning (MEL), a framework that enhances Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) by internalizing self-distilled meta-experience into the LLM's parametric memory, improving reasoning capabilities and achieving performance gains on benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了元经验学习 (MEL)，通过将自我提炼的元经验整合到 LLM 的参数化记忆中来增强可验证奖励强化学习 (RLVR)， 从而提高推理能力并在基准测试中取得性能提升。

Authors: Shiting Huang, Zecheng Li, Yu Zeng, Qingnan Ren, Zhen Fang, Qisheng Su, Kou Shi, Lin Chen, Zehui Chen, Feng Zhao

Causality in Video Diffusers is Separable from Denoising

Abstract (English): Causality -- referring to temporal, uni-directional cause-effect relationships between components -- underlies many complex generative processes, including videos, language, and robot trajectories. Current causal diffusion models entangle temporal reasoning with iterative denoising, applying causal attention across all layers, at every denoising step, and over the entire context. In this paper, we show that the causal reasoning in these models is separable from the multi-step denoising process. Through systematic probing of autoregressive video diffusers, we uncover two key regularities: (1) early layers produce highly similar features across denoising steps, indicating redundant computation along the diffusion trajectory; and (2) deeper layers exhibit sparse cross-frame attention and primarily perform intra-frame rendering. Motivated by these findings, we introduce Separable Causal Diffusion (SCD), a new architecture that explicitly decouples once-per-frame temporal reasoning, via a causal transformer encoder, from multi-step frame-wise rendering, via a lightweight diffusion decoder. Extensive experiments on both pretraining and post-training tasks across synthetic and real benchmarks show that SCD significantly improves throughput and per-frame latency while matching or surpassing the generation quality of strong causal diffusion baselines.

摘要（中文）: 因果关系——指的是组件之间在时间上存在单向的因果关系——是许多复杂生成过程的基础，包括视频、语言和机器人轨迹。当前的因果扩散模型将时间推理与迭代去噪相纠缠，在每个去噪步骤、所有层级以及整个上下文中应用因果注意力。在本文中，我们证明了这些模型中的因果推理可以与多步去噪过程分离。通过对自回归视频扩散器进行系统的探测，我们发现了两个关键规律：（1）早期层级在去噪步骤中产生高度相似的特征，表明沿着扩散轨迹存在冗余计算；（2）更深层级表现出稀疏的跨帧注意力，并且主要执行帧内渲染。受这些发现的启发，我们引入了可分离因果扩散（SCD），这是一种新的架构，通过因果 Transformer 编码器，将一次性执行的逐帧时间推理与通过轻量级扩散解码器进行的多步逐帧渲染显式地解耦。在合成和真实基准上的预训练和后训练中的大量实验表明，SCD 显著提高了吞吐量和单帧延迟，同时匹配或超过了强大的因果扩散基线的生成质量。

TLDR: This paper introduces Separable Causal Diffusion (SCD), which decouples causal reasoning from denoising in video diffusion models, leading to improved throughput and latency without sacrificing generation quality.

简要说明: 本文介绍了可分离因果扩散（SCD），它将视频扩散模型中的因果推理与去噪分离，从而在不牺牲生成质量的情况下提高了吞吐量和延迟。

Authors: Xingjian Bai, Guande He, Zhengqi Li, Eli Shechtman, Xun Huang, Zongze Wu

AurigaNet: A Real-Time Multi-Task Network for Enhanced Urban Driving Perception

Abstract (English): Self-driving cars hold significant potential to reduce traffic accidents, alleviate congestion, and enhance urban mobility. However, developing reliable AI systems for autonomous vehicles remains a substantial challenge. Over the past decade, multi-task learning has emerged as a powerful approach to address complex problems in driving perception. Multi-task networks offer several advantages, including increased computational efficiency, real-time processing capabilities, optimized resource utilization, and improved generalization. In this study, we present AurigaNet, an advanced multi-task network architecture designed to push the boundaries of autonomous driving perception. AurigaNet integrates three critical tasks: object detection, lane detection, and drivable area instance segmentation. The system is trained and evaluated using the BDD100K dataset, renowned for its diversity in driving conditions. Key innovations of AurigaNet include its end-to-end instance segmentation capability, which significantly enhances both accuracy and efficiency in path estimation for autonomous vehicles. Experimental results demonstrate that AurigaNet achieves an 85.2% IoU in drivable area segmentation, outperforming its closest competitor by 0.7%. In lane detection, AurigaNet achieves a remarkable 60.8% IoU, surpassing other models by more than 30%. Furthermore, the network achieves an mAP@0.5:0.95 of 47.6% in traffic object detection, exceeding the next leading model by 2.9%. Additionally, we validate the practical feasibility of AurigaNet by deploying it on embedded devices such as the Jetson Orin NX, where it demonstrates competitive real-time performance. These results underscore AurigaNet's potential as a robust and efficient solution for autonomous driving perception systems. The code can be found here https://github.com/KiaRational/AurigaNet.

摘要（中文）: 自动驾驶车辆在减少交通事故、缓解交通拥堵和提升城市交通出行方面具有巨大的潜力。然而，开发用于自动驾驶车辆的可靠人工智能系统仍然是一项重大挑战。在过去的十年中，多任务学习已经成为解决驾驶感知中复杂问题的强大方法。多任务网络具有多种优势，包括更高的计算效率、实时处理能力、优化的资源利用率和改进的泛化能力。在本研究中，我们提出了一种先进的多任务网络架构AurigaNet，旨在突破自动驾驶感知的界限。AurigaNet集成了三个关键任务：目标检测、车道线检测和可行驶区域实例分割。该系统使用BDD100K数据集进行训练和评估，该数据集以其驾驶条件的多样性而闻名。AurigaNet的关键创新包括其端到端的实例分割能力，这显著提高了自动驾驶车辆路径估计的准确性和效率。实验结果表明，AurigaNet在可行驶区域分割中达到了85.2%的IoU，比最接近的竞争者高出0.7%。在车道线检测中，AurigaNet达到了惊人的60.8%的IoU，超过其他模型30%以上。此外，该网络在交通目标检测中实现了47.6%的mAP@0.5:0.95，超过了下一个领先模型2.9%。我们通过将其部署在Jetson Orin NX等嵌入式设备上，验证了AurigaNet的实际可行性，并在这些设备上展示了具有竞争力的实时性能。这些结果突显了AurigaNet作为自动驾驶感知系统的一种强大而高效的解决方案的潜力。代码可在https://github.com/KiaRational/AurigaNet找到。

TLDR: AurigaNet is a multi-task network that achieves state-of-the-art results on object detection, lane detection, and drivable area segmentation, while also demonstrating real-time performance on embedded devices.

简要说明: AurigaNet是一个多任务神经网络，在目标检测、车道线检测和可行驶区域分割方面取得了最先进的结果，同时还在嵌入式设备上展示了实时性能。

Authors: Kiarash Ghasemzadeh, Sedigheh Dehghani

What Makes Value Learning Efficient in Residual Reinforcement Learning?

Abstract (English): Residual reinforcement learning (RL) enables stable online refinement of expressive pretrained policies by freezing the base and learning only bounded corrections. However, value learning in residual RL poses unique challenges that remain poorly understood. In this work, we identify two key bottlenecks: cold start pathology, where the critic lacks knowledge of the value landscape around the base policy, and structural scale mismatch, where the residual contribution is dwarfed by the base action. Through systematic investigation, we uncover the mechanisms underlying these bottlenecks, revealing that simple yet principled solutions suffice: base-policy transitions serve as an essential value anchor for implicit warmup, and critic normalization effectively restores representation sensitivity for discerning value differences. Based on these insights, we propose DAWN (Data-Anchored Warmup and Normalization), a minimal approach targeting efficient value learning in residual RL. By addressing these bottlenecks, DAWN demonstrates substantial efficiency gains across diverse benchmarks, policy architectures, and observation modalities.

摘要（中文）: 残余强化学习（RL）通过冻结基策略并仅学习有界修正，从而支持对表现力强的预训练策略进行稳定的在线优化。然而，残余RL中的价值学习面临独特的挑战，这些挑战仍然知之甚少。在这项工作中，我们识别出两个关键瓶颈：冷启动病理，即评论家缺乏对基策略附近价值图景的知识；以及结构性尺度不匹配，即残余贡献被基动作所掩盖。通过系统性研究，我们揭示了这些瓶颈背后的机制，表明简单而有原则的解决方案就足够了：基策略转移充当隐式预热的基本价值锚点，而评论家归一化有效地恢复了表示敏感性，以辨别价值差异。基于这些见解，我们提出DAWN（数据锚定的预热和归一化），这是一种极简方法，旨在提高残余RL中价值学习的效率。通过解决这些瓶颈，DAWN在不同的基准测试、策略架构和观察模态中都展示了显著的效率提升。

TLDR: The paper identifies and addresses two key challenges (cold start and scale mismatch) in value learning for residual reinforcement learning, proposing a simple method called DAWN that significantly improves efficiency.

简要说明: 该论文识别并解决了残差强化学习中价值学习的两个关键挑战（冷启动和尺度不匹配），并提出了一种名为DAWN的简单方法，该方法可以显著提高效率。

Authors: Guozheng Ma, Lu Li, Haoyu Wang, Zixuan Liu, Pierre-Luc Bacon, Dacheng Tao

RadarEye: Robust Liquid Level Tracking Using mmWave Radar in Robotic Pouring

Abstract (English): Transparent liquid manipulation in robotic pouring remains challenging for perception systems: specular/refraction effects and lighting variability degrade visual cues, undermining reliable level estimation. To address this challenge, we introduce RadarEye, a real-time mmWave radar signal processing pipeline for robust liquid level estimation and tracking during the whole pouring process. RadarEye integrates (i) a high-resolution range-angle beamforming module for liquid level sensing and (ii) a physics-informed mid-pour tracker that suppresses multipath to maintain lock on the liquid surface despite stream-induced clutter and source container reflections. The pipeline delivers sub-millisecond latency. In real-robot water-pouring experiments, RadarEye achieves a 0.35 cm median absolute height error at 0.62 ms per update, substantially outperforming vision and ultrasound baselines.

摘要（中文）: 以下是翻译结果： 透明液体机器人倾倒操作中的液体操控对感知系统来说仍然具有挑战性：镜面反射/折射效应和光照变化会降低视觉线索的质量，从而损害可靠的液位估计。为了解决这一难题，我们引入了RadarEye，一个用于稳健液位估计和跟踪的实时毫米波雷达信号处理流程，适用于整个倾倒过程。RadarEye集成了（i）一个高分辨率距离-角度波束成形模块，用于液体水平传感，以及（ii）一个具备物理学知识的中途跟踪器，该跟踪器抑制多径效应，以在水流引起的杂波和源容器反射存在的情况下，持续锁定液体表面。该流程提供亚毫秒级的延迟。在真实机器人水倾倒实验中，RadarEye实现了0.35厘米的中值绝对高度误差，每次更新耗时0.62毫秒，显著优于视觉和超声基线方法。

TLDR: The paper introduces RadarEye, a real-time mmWave radar system for robust liquid level tracking during robotic pouring, outperforming vision and ultrasound baselines in accuracy and latency.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为 RadarEye 的实时毫米波雷达系统，用于在机器人倾倒过程中实现鲁棒的液体水平跟踪，其精度和延迟优于视觉和超声波基线。

Authors: Hongyu Deng, He Chen

Abstraction Generation for Generalized Planning with Pretrained Large Language Models

Abstract (English): Qualitative Numerical Planning (QNP) serves as an important abstraction model for generalized planning (GP), which aims to compute general plans that solve multiple instances at once. Recent works show that large language models (LLMs) can function as generalized planners. This work investigates whether LLMs can serve as QNP abstraction generators for GP problems and how to fix abstractions via automated debugging. We propose a prompt protocol: input a GP domain and training tasks to LLMs, prompting them to generate abstract features and further abstract the initial state, action set, and goal into QNP problems. An automated debugging method is designed to detect abstraction errors, guiding LLMs to fix abstractions. Experiments demonstrate that under properly guided by automated debugging, some LLMs can generate useful QNP abstractions.

摘要（中文）: 定性数值规划（QNP）是广义规划（GP）的一个重要抽象模型，其目标是计算能够一次性解决多个实例的通用计划。最近的研究表明，大型语言模型（LLM）可以作为广义规划器发挥作用。本文研究了LLM是否可以作为GP问题的QNP抽象生成器，以及如何通过自动化调试来修复抽象。我们提出了一种提示协议：将GP域和训练任务输入到LLM中，提示它们生成抽象特征，并进一步将初始状态、动作集和目标抽象成QNP问题。设计了一种自动化调试方法来检测抽象错误，引导LLM修复抽象。实验表明，在自动化调试的适当指导下，一些LLM可以生成有用的QNP抽象。

TLDR: This paper explores using LLMs to generate Qualitative Numerical Planning (QNP) abstractions for generalized planning and introduces an automated debugging method to refine these abstractions, showing promising results under guided debugging.

Authors: Zhenhe Cui, Huaxiang Xia, Hangjun Shen, Kailun Luo, Yong He, Wei Liang

Authenticated Workflows: A Systems Approach to Protecting Agentic AI

Abstract (English): Agentic AI systems automate enterprise workflows but existing defenses--guardrails, semantic filters--are probabilistic and routinely bypassed. We introduce authenticated workflows, the first complete trust layer for enterprise agentic AI. Security reduces to protecting four fundamental boundaries: prompts, tools, data, and context. We enforce intent (operations satisfy organizational policies) and integrity (operations are cryptographically authentic) at every boundary crossing, combining cryptographic elimination of attack classes with runtime policy enforcement. This delivers deterministic security--operations either carry valid cryptographic proof or are rejected. We introduce MAPL, an AI-native policy language that expresses agentic constraints dynamically as agents evolve and invocation context changes, scaling as O(log M + N) policies versus O(M x N) rules through hierarchical composition with cryptographic attestations for workflow dependencies. We prove practicality through a universal security runtime integrating nine leading frameworks (MCP, A2A, OpenAI, Claude, LangChain, CrewAI, AutoGen, LlamaIndex, Haystack) through thin adapters requiring zero protocol modifications. Formal proofs establish completeness and soundness. Empirical validation shows 100% recall with zero false positives across 174 test cases, protection against 9 of 10 OWASP Top 10 risks, and complete mitigation of two high impact production CVEs.

摘要（中文）: 自主人工智能系统能自动化企业工作流程，但现有防御措施——如安全防护栏、语义过滤器——具有概率性且经常被绕过。我们引入了认证工作流，这是首个面向企业自主人工智能的完整信任层。安全性归结为保护四个基本边界：提示词、工具、数据和上下文。我们在每个边界穿越处强制执行意图（操作满足组织策略）和完整性（操作具有密码学上的真实性），将密码学消除攻击类别与运行时策略执行相结合。这实现了确定性安全——操作要么带有有效的密码学证明，要么被拒绝。我们引入了MAPL，一种人工智能原生策略语言，它可以动态地表达自主智能体的约束条件，随着智能体发展和调用上下文的变化而扩展，通过具有工作流依赖性的密码学认证的分层组合，将策略扩展至O(log M + N)级别，而不是O(M x N)规则级别。我们通过一个通用安全运行时证明了其实用性，该运行时集成了九个领先框架（MCP、A2A、OpenAI、Claude、LangChain、CrewAI、AutoGen、LlamaIndex、Haystack），通过不需要任何协议修改的轻量级适配器实现。形式化证明确立了其完整性和可靠性。经验验证显示，在174个测试用例中，召回率为100%，误报率为零，可防护OWASP Top 10风险中的9项，并完全缓解了两个高影响的生产环境CVE漏洞。

TLDR: The paper introduces a novel "authenticated workflows" system for securing agentic AI by enforcing intent and integrity at fundamental boundaries, achieving deterministic security and demonstrating effectiveness across various frameworks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为"认证工作流"的新型系统，旨在通过在基本边界上强制执行意图和完整性来保护 Agentic AI 的安全，实现确定性安全，并在各种框架中展示了有效性。

Authors: Mohan Rajagopalan, Vinay Rao

SWE-MiniSandbox: Container-Free Reinforcement Learning for Building Software Engineering Agents

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a key paradigm for training software engineering (SWE) agents, but existing pipelines typically rely on per-task containers for isolation. At scale, pre-built container images incur substantial storage overhead, slow environment setup, and require container-management privileges. We propose SWE-MiniSandbox, a lightweight, container-free method that enables scalable RL training of SWE agents without sacrificing isolation. Instead of relying on per-instance containers, SWE-MiniSandbox executes each task in an isolated workspace backed by kernel-level mechanisms, substantially reducing system overhead. It leverages lightweight environment pre-caching techniques to eliminate the need for bulky container images. As a result, our approach lowers disk usage to approximately 5\% of that required by container-based pipelines and reduces environment preparation time to about 25\% of the container baseline. Empirical results demonstrate that SWE-MiniSandbox achieves evaluation performance comparable to standard container-based pipelines. By removing the dependency on heavy container infrastructure, SWE-MiniSandbox offers a practical and accessible foundation for scaling RL-based SWE agents, particularly in resource-constrained research environments.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习(RL)已成为训练软件工程(SWE)智能体的关键范式，但现有流程通常依赖于基于任务的容器进行隔离。在大规模情况下，预构建的容器镜像会导致大量的存储开销、缓慢的环境设置，并且需要容器管理权限。我们提出了SWE-MiniSandbox，这是一种轻量级的、无容器的方法，可以在不牺牲隔离性的前提下，实现SWE智能体可扩展的RL训练。SWE-MiniSandbox并非依赖于每个实例的容器，而是通过内核级机制支持的隔离工作空间中执行每个任务，从而大幅降低系统开销。它利用轻量级的环境预缓存技术，消除了对庞大容器镜像的需求。因此，我们的方法将磁盘使用量降低到基于容器的流程所需磁盘使用量的约5%，并将环境准备时间减少到容器基准的约25%。实证结果表明，SWE-MiniSandbox实现了与标准基于容器的流程相当的评估性能。通过消除对重型容器基础设施的依赖，SWE-MiniSandbox为扩展基于RL的SWE智能体提供了一个实用且易于访问的基础，尤其是在资源受限的研究环境中。

TLDR: The paper introduces SWE-MiniSandbox, a container-free reinforcement learning environment for training software engineering agents, which significantly reduces storage overhead and environment setup time compared to container-based methods while maintaining comparable performance.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了SWE-MiniSandbox， 一种用于训练软件工程代理的无容器强化学习环境。与基于容器的方法相比，它显著降低了存储开销和环境设置时间，同时保持了相当的性能水平。

Authors: Danlong Yuan, Wei Wu, Zhengren Wang, Xueliang Zhao, Huishuai Zhang, Dongyan Zhao

LaSSM: Efficient Semantic-Spatial Query Decoding via Local Aggregation and State Space Models for 3D Instance Segmentation

Abstract (English): Query-based 3D scene instance segmentation from point clouds has attained notable performance. However, existing methods suffer from the query initialization dilemma due to the sparse nature of point clouds and rely on computationally intensive attention mechanisms in query decoders. We accordingly introduce LaSSM, prioritizing simplicity and efficiency while maintaining competitive performance. Specifically, we propose a hierarchical semantic-spatial query initializer to derive the query set from superpoints by considering both semantic cues and spatial distribution, achieving comprehensive scene coverage and accelerated convergence. We further present a coordinate-guided state space model (SSM) decoder that progressively refines queries. The novel decoder features a local aggregation scheme that restricts the model to focus on geometrically coherent regions and a spatial dual-path SSM block to capture underlying dependencies within the query set by integrating associated coordinates information. Our design enables efficient instance prediction, avoiding the incorporation of noisy information and reducing redundant computation. LaSSM ranks first place on the latest ScanNet++ V2 leaderboard, outperforming the previous best method by 2.5% mAP with only 1/3 FLOPs, demonstrating its superiority in challenging large-scale scene instance segmentation. LaSSM also achieves competitive performance on ScanNet, ScanNet200, S3DIS and ScanNet++ V1 benchmarks with less computational cost. Extensive ablation studies and qualitative results validate the effectiveness of our design. The code and weights are available at https://github.com/RayYoh/LaSSM.

摘要（中文）: 基于查询的点云三维场景实例分割已经取得了显著的性能。然而，现有方法由于点云的稀疏性而面临查询初始化的困境，并且依赖于查询解码器中计算密集型的注意力机制。因此，我们提出了LaSSM，在保持具有竞争力的性能的同时，优先考虑简洁性和效率。具体而言，我们提出了一种分层语义-空间查询初始化器，通过同时考虑语义线索和空间分布，从超点中导出查询集，从而实现全面的场景覆盖和加速收敛。我们进一步提出了一种坐标引导的状态空间模型（SSM）解码器，该解码器逐步细化查询。这种新颖的解码器具有局部聚合方案，限制模型关注几何上连贯的区域，以及空间双路径SSM块，通过整合相关的坐标信息来捕获查询集中的潜在依赖关系。我们的设计能够实现高效的实例预测，避免掺杂噪声信息并减少冗余计算。LaSSM在最新的ScanNet++ V2排行榜上排名第一，以仅1/3的FLOPs超越了先前最佳方法2.5%的mAP，证明其在具有挑战性的大规模场景实例分割中的优越性。LaSSM还在ScanNet、ScanNet200、S3DIS和ScanNet++ V1基准测试中以更低的计算成本实现了具有竞争力的性能。大量的消融研究和定性结果验证了我们设计的有效性。代码和权重可在https://github.com/RayYoh/LaSSM获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces LaSSM, a computationally efficient method for 3D instance segmentation using a hierarchical semantic-spatial query initializer and a coordinate-guided state space model decoder, achieving state-of-the-art performance on ScanNet++ V2 with significantly reduced FLOPs.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了LaSSM，一种计算高效的3D实例分割方法，它使用分层的语义-空间查询初始化器和坐标引导的状态空间模型解码器，在ScanNet++ V2上实现了最先进的性能，并显著降低了FLOPs。

Authors: Lei Yao, Yi Wang, Yawen Cui, Moyun Liu, Lap-Pui Chau

Interpretable Vision Transformers in Monocular Depth Estimation via SVDA

Abstract (English): Monocular depth estimation is a central problem in computer vision with applications in robotics, AR, and autonomous driving, yet the self-attention mechanisms that drive modern Transformer architectures remain opaque. We introduce SVD-Inspired Attention (SVDA) into the Dense Prediction Transformer (DPT), providing the first spectrally structured formulation of attention for dense prediction tasks. SVDA decouples directional alignment from spectral modulation by embedding a learnable diagonal matrix into normalized query-key interactions, enabling attention maps that are intrinsically interpretable rather than post-hoc approximations. Experiments on KITTI and NYU-v2 show that SVDA preserves or slightly improves predictive accuracy while adding only minor computational overhead. More importantly, SVDA unlocks six spectral indicators that quantify entropy, rank, sparsity, alignment, selectivity, and robustness. These reveal consistent cross-dataset and depth-wise patterns in how attention organizes during training, insights that remain inaccessible in standard Transformers. By shifting the role of attention from opaque mechanism to quantifiable descriptor, SVDA redefines interpretability in monocular depth estimation and opens a principled avenue toward transparent dense prediction models.

摘要（中文）: 单目深度估计是计算机视觉中的一个核心问题，在机器人、增强现实和自动驾驶等领域有着广泛的应用，然而驱动现代Transformer架构的自注意力机制仍然不透明。我们将受奇异值分解启发的注意力机制（SVD-Inspired Attention, SVDA）引入到密集预测Transformer（Dense Prediction Transformer, DPT）中，为密集预测任务提供了首个具有谱结构形式的注意力机制。SVDA通过将可学习的对角矩阵嵌入到归一化的查询-键交互中，将方向对齐与谱调制解耦，使得注意力图具有内在的可解释性，而非事后近似。在KITTI和NYU-v2上的实验表明，SVDA在仅增加少量计算开销的同时，保持或略微提高了预测精度。更重要的是，SVDA解锁了六个谱指标，用于量化熵、秩、稀疏性、对齐性、选择性和鲁棒性。这些指标揭示了在训练过程中注意力如何组织的跨数据集和深度方向上的一致模式，而这些洞见在标准Transformer中是无法获得的。通过将注意力的作用从不透明的机制转变为可量化的描述符，SVDA重新定义了单目深度估计中的可解释性，并为透明的密集预测模型开辟了一条有原则的途径。

TLDR: This paper introduces SVD-Inspired Attention (SVDA) for monocular depth estimation, offering improved interpretability and spectral analysis of attention mechanisms while maintaining or slightly improving accuracy.

简要说明: 本文介绍了用于单目深度估计的SVD启发式注意力机制(SVDA)，提供了改进的可解释性和注意力机制的频谱分析，同时保持或略微提高了精度。

Authors: Vasileios Arampatzakis, George Pavlidis, Nikolaos Mitianoudis, Nikos Papamarkos

DMP-3DAD: Cross-Category 3D Anomaly Detection via Realistic Depth Map Projection with Few Normal Samples

Abstract (English): Cross-category anomaly detection for 3D point clouds aims to determine whether an unseen object belongs to a target category using only a few normal examples. Most existing methods rely on category-specific training, which limits their flexibility in few-shot scenarios. In this paper, we propose DMP-3DAD, a training-free framework for cross-category 3D anomaly detection based on multi-view realistic depth map projection. Specifically, by converting point clouds into a fixed set of realistic depth images, our method leverages a frozen CLIP visual encoder to extract multi-view representations and performs anomaly detection via weighted feature similarity, which does not require any fine-tuning or category-dependent adaptation. Extensive experiments on the ShapeNetPart dataset demonstrate that DMP-3DAD achieves state-of-the-art performance under few-shot setting. The results show that the proposed approach provides a simple yet effective solution for practical cross-category 3D anomaly detection.

摘要（中文）: 针对3D点云的跨类别异常检测旨在仅利用少量正常样本来判断一个未见过的对象是否属于目标类别。现有的大多数方法依赖于类别相关的训练，这限制了它们在少样本场景下的灵活性。在本文中，我们提出了一种基于多视角真实深度图投影的无训练跨类别3D异常检测框架DMP-3DAD。具体来说，通过将点云转换为一组固定的真实深度图像，我们的方法利用一个冻结的CLIP视觉编码器来提取多视角表征，并通过加权特征相似度执行异常检测，这不需要任何微调或类别相关的适应。在ShapeNetPart数据集上的大量实验表明，DMP-3DAD在少样本设置下实现了最先进的性能。实验结果表明，所提出的方法为实际的跨类别3D异常检测提供了一种简单而有效的解决方案。

TLDR: The paper introduces DMP-3DAD, a training-free framework for cross-category 3D anomaly detection using multi-view realistic depth map projection and a frozen CLIP visual encoder, achieving SOTA performance in few-shot settings on ShapeNetPart.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了DMP-3DAD，一个无需训练的跨类别3D异常检测框架，它利用多视角真实深度图投影和一个冻结的CLIP视觉编码器，在ShapeNetPart上实现了少样本设置下的SOTA性能。

Authors: Zi Wang, Katsuya Hotta, Koichiro Kamide, Yawen Zou, Jianjian Qin, Chao Zhang, Jun Yu

4RC: 4D Reconstruction via Conditional Querying Anytime and Anywhere

Abstract (English): We present 4RC, a unified feed-forward framework for 4D reconstruction from monocular videos. Unlike existing approaches that typically decouple motion from geometry or produce limited 4D attributes such as sparse trajectories or two-view scene flow, 4RC learns a holistic 4D representation that jointly captures dense scene geometry and motion dynamics. At its core, 4RC introduces a novel encode-once, query-anywhere and anytime paradigm: a transformer backbone encodes the entire video into a compact spatio-temporal latent space, from which a conditional decoder can efficiently query 3D geometry and motion for any query frame at any target timestamp. To facilitate learning, we represent per-view 4D attributes in a minimally factorized form by decomposing them into base geometry and time-dependent relative motion. Extensive experiments demonstrate that 4RC outperforms prior and concurrent methods across a wide range of 4D reconstruction tasks.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了4RC，一个统一的前馈框架，用于从单目视频中进行4D重建。与通常将运动与几何解耦或产生有限4D属性（如稀疏轨迹或双视图场景流）的现有方法不同，4RC学习一种整体的4D表示，该表示联合捕捉密集的场景几何和运动动态。其核心是，4RC引入了一种新颖的编码一次、随处随时查询的范式：一个 Transformer 主干网络将整个视频编码成一个紧凑的时空潜在空间，一个条件解码器可以从中高效地查询任意查询帧在任意目标时间戳的3D几何和运动信息。为了方便学习，我们通过将每个视角的4D属性分解为基础几何和时间相关的相对运动，以最小化的分解形式表示它们。大量的实验表明，在各种4D重建任务中，4RC都优于先前和同期的方法。

TLDR: 4RC is a novel feed-forward framework for 4D reconstruction from monocular videos, using a transformer-based architecture for encoding video and querying geometry and motion at any time. It demonstrates superior performance on 4D reconstruction tasks.

简要说明: 4RC是一个新颖的前馈框架，用于从单目视频中进行4D重建，使用基于Transformer的架构来编码视频，并可在任何时间查询几何形状和运动。 它在4D重建任务上表现出卓越的性能。

Authors: Yihang Luo, Shangchen Zhou, Yushi Lan, Xingang Pan, Chen Change Loy

Rising Multi-Armed Bandits with Known Horizons

Abstract (English): The Rising Multi-Armed Bandit (RMAB) framework models environments where expected rewards of arms increase with plays, which models practical scenarios where performance of each option improves with the repeated usage, such as in robotics and hyperparameter tuning. For instance, in hyperparameter tuning, the validation accuracy of a model configuration (arm) typically increases with each training epoch. A defining characteristic of RMAB is em horizon-dependent optimality: unlike standard settings, the optimal strategy here shifts dramatically depending on the available budget $T$. This implies that knowledge of $T$ yields significantly greater utility in RMAB, empowering the learner to align its decision-making with this shifting optimality. However, the horizon-aware setting remains underexplored. To address this, we propose a novel CUmulative Reward Estimation UCB (CURE-UCB) that explicitly integrates the horizon. We provide a rigorous analysis establishing a new regret upper bound and prove that our method strictly outperforms horizon-agnostic strategies in structured environments like ``linear-then-flat'' instances. Extensive experiments demonstrate its significant superiority over baselines.

摘要（中文）: 以下是摘要的中文翻译： 上升多臂老虎机（RMAB）框架模拟了臂的期望回报随着播放次数增加的环境，这模拟了每个选项的性能会随着重复使用而提高的实际场景，例如在机器人技术和超参数调优中。例如，在超参数调优中，模型配置（臂）的验证准确率通常会随着每个训练epoch而增加。RMAB的一个决定性特征是其具有依赖于时域的优化性：与标准设置不同，此处的最佳策略会根据可用预算$T$而发生显著变化。这意味着有关$T$的知识在RMAB中产生更大的效用，从而使学习器能够使其决策与这种变化的优化性对齐。然而，时域感知的设置仍未得到充分探索。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种新颖的累积奖励估计UCB（CURE-UCB），它显式地集成了时域。我们提供了严格的分析，建立了新的遗憾上限，并证明了我们的方法在诸如“线性然后平坦”的结构化环境中严格优于时域不可知的策略。大量的实验证明了其相对于基线的显著优越性。

TLDR: This paper introduces a horizon-aware algorithm for Rising Multi-Armed Bandits (RMAB), demonstrating improved performance compared to horizon-agnostic methods through theoretical analysis and experiments, with potential benefits for robotics and hyperparameter tuning.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种针对 Rising Multi-Armed Bandits (RMAB) 的 horizon-aware 算法，通过理论分析和实验证明，与 horizon-agnostic 方法相比，该算法具有更好的性能，并具有在机器人技术和超参数调优方面的潜在应用。

Authors: Seockbean Song, Chenyu Gan, Youngsik Yoon, Siwei Wang, Wei Chen, Jungseul Ok

Beyond Task Performance: A Metric-Based Analysis of Sequential Cooperation in Heterogeneous Multi-Agent Destructive Foraging

Abstract (English): This work addresses the problem of analyzing cooperation in heterogeneous multi-agent systems which operate under partial observability and temporal role dependency, framed within a destructive multi-agent foraging setting. Unlike most previous studies, which focus primarily on algorithmic performance with respect to task completion, this article proposes a systematic set of general-purpose cooperation metrics aimed at characterizing not only efficiency, but also coordination and dependency between teams and agents, fairness, and sensitivity. These metrics are designed to be transferable to different multi-agent sequential domains similar to foraging. The proposed suite of metrics is structured into three main categories that jointly provide a multilevel characterization of cooperation: primary metrics, inter-team metrics, and intra-team metrics. They have been validated in a realistic destructive foraging scenario inspired by dynamic aquatic surface cleaning using heterogeneous autonomous vehicles. It involves two specialized teams with sequential dependencies: one focused on the search of resources, and another on their destruction. Several representative approaches have been evaluated, covering both learning-based algorithms and classical heuristic paradigms.

摘要（中文）: 本研究探讨了在异构多智能体系统中，智能体在部分可观测和时间角色依赖下进行协作的问题，并将其置于一种破坏性的多智能体觅食环境中。与以往主要关注任务完成的算法性能的研究不同，本文提出了一套通用的协作指标，旨在不仅表征效率，还表征团队和智能体之间的协调性、依赖性、公平性和敏感性。这些指标旨在可迁移到与觅食类似的不同多智能体序列化领域。所提出的指标套件被构建为三个主要类别，共同提供对协作的多层次表征：一级指标、团队间指标和团队内指标。这些指标已通过一个真实的破坏性觅食场景进行了验证，该场景的灵感来自于使用异构自主车辆进行动态水面清洁。该场景涉及两个具有顺序依赖性的专业团队：一个专注于资源搜索，另一个专注于资源破坏。已经评估了几种具有代表性的方法，涵盖了基于学习的算法和经典的启发式范例。

TLDR: This paper introduces a set of metrics to analyze cooperation in heterogeneous multi-agent systems, going beyond task performance to assess coordination, dependency, fairness, and sensitivity in a destructive foraging scenario.

简要说明: 本文提出了一系列指标，用于分析异构多智能体系统中的合作，超越了单纯的任务性能，评估了破坏性觅食场景中的协调性、依赖性、公平性和敏感性。

Bayesian Inference of Contextual Bandit Policies via Empirical Likelihood

Abstract (English): Policy inference plays an essential role in the contextual bandit problem. In this paper, we use empirical likelihood to develop a Bayesian inference method for the joint analysis of multiple contextual bandit policies in finite sample regimes. The proposed inference method is robust to small sample sizes and is able to provide accurate uncertainty measurements for policy value evaluation. In addition, it allows for flexible inferences on policy comparison with full uncertainty quantification. We demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed inference method using Monte Carlo simulations and its application to an adolescent body mass index data set.

摘要（中文）: 策略推断在上下文老虎机问题中扮演着至关重要的角色。在本文中，我们使用经验似然开发了一种贝叶斯推断方法，用于在有限样本机制下对多个上下文老虎机策略进行联合分析。所提出的推断方法对小样本量具有鲁棒性，并且能够为策略价值评估提供精确的不确定性度量。此外，它允许对策略比较进行灵活的推断，并具备完整的不确定性量化能力。我们通过蒙特卡洛模拟验证了所提出的推断方法的有效性，并将其应用于青少年体重指数数据集。

Authors: Jiangrong Ouyang, Mingming Gong, Howard Bondell

ACE-RTL: When Agentic Context Evolution Meets RTL-Specialized LLMs

Abstract (English): Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have sparked growing interest in applying them to hardware design automation, particularly for accurate RTL code generation. Prior efforts follow two largely independent paths: (i) training domain-adapted RTL models to internalize hardware semantics, (ii) developing agentic systems that leverage frontier generic LLMs guided by simulation feedback. However, these two paths exhibit complementary strengths and weaknesses. In this work, we present ACE-RTL that unifies both directions through Agentic Context Evolution (ACE). ACE-RTL integrates an RTL-specialized LLM, trained on a large-scale dataset of 1.7 million RTL samples, with a frontier reasoning LLM through three synergistic components: the generator, reflector, and coordinator. These components iteratively refine RTL code toward functional correctness. We further introduce a parallel scaling strategy that significantly reduces the number of iterations required to reach correct solutions. On the Comprehensive Verilog Design Problems (CVDP) benchmark, ACE-RTL achieves up to a 44.87% pass rate improvement over 14 competitive baselines while requiring only four iterations on average.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLM）的最新进展激发了对其应用于硬件设计自动化的日益增长的兴趣，特别是针对精确的RTL代码生成。先前的尝试主要遵循两条独立的路径：（i）训练领域自适应的RTL模型以内部化硬件语义，（ii）开发由仿真反馈指导的、利用前沿通用LLM的自主体系统(agentic systems)。然而，这两条路径表现出互补的优势和劣势。在这项工作中，我们提出了ACE-RTL，它通过自主体上下文演化（ACE）统一了这两个方向。ACE-RTL集成了一个RTL专业 LLM，该模型在包含170万个RTL样本的大规模数据集上进行训练，并通过三个协同组件（生成器、反射器和协调器）与前沿推理 LLM 集成。这些组件迭代地改进RTL代码，使其达到功能正确性。我们进一步引入了一种并行扩展策略，可以显著减少达到正确解决方案所需的迭代次数。在综合Verilog设计问题（CVDP）基准测试中，ACE-RTL的通过率比14个有竞争力的基线模型提高了高达44.87%，并且平均只需要四次迭代。

TLDR: ACE-RTL combines an RTL-specialized LLM with a frontier reasoning LLM using an agentic context evolution approach, achieving significant improvements in RTL code generation correctness compared to existing methods.

简要说明: ACE-RTL 结合了 RTL 专用 LLM 和前沿推理 LLM，采用 Agentic Context Evolution 方法，与现有方法相比，在 RTL 代码生成正确性方面取得了显著改进。
