Authors: Chenhui Deng, Zhongzhi Yu, Guan-Ting Liu, Nathaniel Pinckney, Haoxing Ren

Omnidirectional Dual-Arm Aerial Manipulator with Proprioceptive Contact Localization for Landing on Slanted Roofs

Abstract (English): Operating drones in urban environments often means they need to land on rooftops, which can have different geometries and surface irregularities. Accurately detecting roof inclination using conventional sensing methods, such as vision-based or acoustic techniques, can be unreliable, as measurement quality is strongly influenced by external factors including weather conditions and surface materials. To overcome these challenges, we propose a novel unmanned aerial manipulator morphology featuring a dual-arm aerial manipulator with an omnidirectional 3D workspace and extended reach. Building on this design, we develop a proprioceptive contact detection and contact localization strategy based on a momentum-based torque observer. This enables the UAM to infer the inclination of slanted surfaces blindly - through physical interaction - prior to touchdown. We validate the approach in flight experiments, demonstrating robust landings on surfaces with inclinations of up to 30.5 degrees and achieving an average surface inclination estimation error of 2.87 degrees over 9 experiments at different incline angles.

摘要（中文）: 在城市环境中操作无人机通常意味着它们需要在屋顶上着陆，而屋顶可能具有不同的几何形状和表面不规则性。使用传统的传感方法（如基于视觉或声学的技术）来准确检测屋顶倾斜度可能不太可靠，因为测量质量受到天气条件和表面材料等外部因素的强烈影响。为了克服这些挑战，我们提出了一种新型无人机空中机械臂形态，其特点是具有全向3D工作空间和扩展臂展的双臂空中机械臂。基于此设计，我们开发了一种基于动量扭矩观测器的本体感受接触检测和接触定位策略。这使得无人机空中机械臂能够在着陆前，通过物理交互盲目地推断倾斜表面的倾斜度。我们在飞行实验中验证了该方法，证明其能够在倾斜度高达30.5度的表面上稳健着陆，并且在不同倾斜角度的9次实验中，实现平均表面倾斜度估计误差为2.87度。

TLDR: This paper proposes a dual-arm aerial manipulator with proprioceptive contact localization for robust landing on slanted roofs, achieving accurate inclination estimation through physical interaction.

Free-Flying Crew Cooperative Robots on the ISS: A Joint Review of Astrobee, CIMON, and Int-Ball Operations

Abstract (English): Intra-vehicular free-flying robots are anticipated to support various work in human spaceflight while working side-by-side with astronauts. Authors: Seiko Piotr Yamaguchi, Andres Mora Vargas, Till Eisenberg, Christian Rogon, Tatsuya Yamamoto, Shona Inoue, Christoph Kössl, Brian Coltin, Trey Smith, Jose V. Benavides

An Ontology-driven Dynamic Knowledge Base for Uninhabited Ground Vehicles

Abstract (English): In this paper, the concept of Dynamic Contextual Mission Data (DCMD) is introduced to develop an ontology-driven dynamic knowledge base for Uninhabited Ground Vehicles (UGVs) at the tactical edge. The dynamic knowledge base with DCMD is added to the UGVs to: support enhanced situation awareness; improve autonomous decision making; and facilitate agility within complex and dynamic environments. As UGVs are heavily reliant on the a priori information added pre-mission, unexpected occurrences during a mission can cause identification ambiguities and require increased levels of user input. Updating this a priori information with contextual information can help UGVs realise their full potential. To address this, the dynamic knowledge base was designed using an ontology-driven representation, supported by near real-time information acquisition and analysis, to provide in-mission on-platform DCMD updates. This was implemented on a team of four UGVs that executed a laboratory based surveillance mission. The results showed that the ontology-driven dynamic representation of the UGV operational environment was machine actionable, producing contextual information to support a successful and timely mission, and contributed directly to the situation awareness.

摘要（中文）: 本文引入了动态上下文任务数据(DCMD)的概念，旨在为战术边缘的无人地面车辆(UGV)开发一个本体驱动的动态知识库。通过将包含DCMD的动态知识库添加到UGV中，旨在：支持增强的情境感知能力；改进自主决策；以及促进在复杂和动态环境中的敏捷性。由于UGV在很大程度上依赖于任务前添加的先验信息，任务期间发生的意外情况可能会导致识别歧义性，并需要增加用户输入。利用上下文信息更新这些先验信息可以帮助UGV充分发挥其潜力。为了解决这个问题，动态知识库采用了一种本体驱动的表示方法进行设计，并辅以近实时信息采集和分析，以提供任务期间的车载DCMD更新。该方法在一个由四辆UGV组成的团队上进行了基于实验室的监视任务验证。结果表明，UGV运行环境的本体驱动动态表示是机器可操作的，能够生成上下文信息以支持成功且及时的任务，并直接贡献于情境感知。

Authors: Hsan Sandar Win, Andrew Walters, Cheng-Chew Lim, Daniel Webber, Seth Leslie, Tan Doan

Solving Geodesic Equations with Composite Bernstein Polynomials for Trajectory Planning

Abstract (English): This work presents a trajectory planning method based on composite Bernstein polynomials for autonomous systems navigating complex environments. The method is implemented in a symbolic optimization framework that enables continuous paths and precise control over trajectory shape. Trajectories are planned over a cost surface that encodes obstacles as continuous fields rather than discrete boundaries. Regions near obstacles are assigned higher costs, naturally encouraging the trajectory to maintain a safe distance while still allowing efficient routing through constrained spaces. The use of composite Bernstein polynomials preserves continuity while enabling fine control over local curvature to satisfy geodesic constraints. The symbolic representation supports exact derivatives, improving optimization efficiency. The method applies to both two- and three-dimensional environments and is suitable for ground, aerial, underwater, and space systems. In spacecraft trajectory planning, for example, it enables the generation of continuous, dynamically feasible trajectories with high numerical efficiency, making it well suited for orbital maneuvers, rendezvous and proximity operations, cluttered gravitational environments, and planetary exploration missions with limited onboard computational resources. Demonstrations show that the approach efficiently generates smooth, collision-free paths in scenarios with multiple obstacles, maintaining clearance without extensive sampling or post-processing. The optimization incorporates three constraint types: (1) a Gaussian surface inequality enforcing minimum obstacle clearance; (2) geodesic equations guiding the path along locally efficient directions on the cost surface; and (3) boundary constraints enforcing fixed start and end conditions. The method can serve as a standalone planner or as an initializer for more complex motion planning problems.

摘要（中文）: 本文提出了一种基于复合伯恩斯坦多项式的轨迹规划方法，用于自主系统在复杂环境中导航。该方法在一个符号优化框架中实现，能够生成连续路径并精确控制轨迹形状。轨迹规划在一个成本曲面上进行，该曲面将障碍物编码为连续场，而非离散边界。障碍物附近的区域被赋予更高的成本，从而自然地引导轨迹保持安全距离，同时仍然允许高效地通过受限空间。复合伯恩斯坦多项式的使用保持了连续性，并能够精细控制局部曲率以满足测地线约束。符号表示支持精确导数，从而提高优化效率。该方法适用于二维和三维环境，并适用于地面、空中、水下和空间系统。例如，在航天器轨迹规划中，它能够以高数值效率生成连续的、动态可行的轨迹，使其非常适合轨道机动、交会和近距离操作、杂乱引力环境以及机载计算资源受限的行星探测任务。演示表明，该方法能够有效地在具有多个障碍物的场景中生成平滑、无碰撞的路径，无需大量采样或后处理即可保持安全距离。优化过程整合了三种约束类型：（1）实施最小障碍物间隙的高斯曲面不等式；（2）沿着成本曲面上局部高效方向引导路径的测地线方程；以及（3）实施固定起始和结束条件的边界约束。该方法可以作为独立的规划器，也可以作为更复杂的运动规划问题的初始化器。

TLDR: This paper introduces a trajectory planning method using composite Bernstein polynomials and symbolic optimization to generate collision-free paths in complex environments, suitable for various robotic systems, even with limited computational resources.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于复合伯恩斯坦多项式和符号优化的轨迹规划方法，可以在复杂环境中生成无碰撞路径，适用于各种机器人系统，即使在计算资源有限的情况下也能应用。

Authors: Nick Gorman, Gage MacLin, Maxwell Hammond, Venanzio Cichella

Transport, Don't Generate: Deterministic Geometric Flows for Combinatorial Optimization

Abstract (English): Recent advances in Neural Combinatorial Optimization (NCO) have been dominated by diffusion models that treat the Euclidean Traveling Salesman Problem (TSP) as a stochastic $N \times N$ heatmap generation task. In this paper, we propose CycFlow, a framework that replaces iterative edge denoising with deterministic point transport. CycFlow learns an instance-conditioned vector field that continuously transports input 2D coordinates to a canonical circular arrangement, where the optimal tour is recovered from this $2N$ dimensional representation via angular sorting. By leveraging data-dependent flow matching, we bypass the quadratic bottleneck of edge scoring in favor of linear coordinate dynamics. This paradigm shift accelerates solving speed by up to three orders of magnitude compared to state-of-the-art diffusion baselines, while maintaining competitive optimality gaps.

摘要（中文）: 神经组合优化（NCO）领域的最新进展主要由扩散模型主导，这些模型将欧几里得旅行商问题（TSP）视为一个随机的$N \times N$热图生成任务。在本文中，我们提出了CycFlow，一个用确定性点传输取代迭代边缘去噪的框架。CycFlow学习一个实例条件向量场，该向量场连续地将输入2D坐标传输到规范的圆形排列，并通过角度排序从这个$2N$维表示中恢复最优路径。通过利用数据相关的流匹配，我们绕过了边缘评分的二次复杂度瓶颈，转而使用线性坐标动力学。与最先进的扩散基线相比，这种范式转变将求解速度提高了高达三个数量级，同时保持了有竞争力的最优性差距。

TLDR: The paper introduces CycFlow, a novel framework for solving the Traveling Salesman Problem (TSP) using deterministic point transport instead of generative diffusion models, achieving significant speedups with competitive optimality.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为CycFlow 的新框架，用于解决旅行商问题 (TSP)。它采用确定性点传输而非生成扩散模型，在保持竞争性最优性的同时，显著提高了速度。

Authors: Benjy Friedmann, Nadav Dym

ENIGMA: EEG-to-Image in 15 Minutes Using Less Than 1% of the Parameters

Abstract (English): To be practical for real-life applications, models for brain-computer interfaces must be easily and quickly deployable on new subjects, effective on affordable scanning hardware, and small enough to run locally on accessible computing resources. To directly address these current limitations, we introduce ENIGMA, a multi-subject electroencephalography (EEG)-to-Image decoding model that reconstructs seen images from EEG recordings and achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance on the research-grade THINGS-EEG2 and consumer-grade AllJoined-1.6M benchmarks, while fine-tuning effectively on new subjects with as little as 15 minutes of data. ENIGMA boasts a simpler architecture and requires less than 1% of the trainable parameters necessary for previous approaches. Our approach integrates a subject-unified spatio-temporal backbone along with a set of multi-subject latent alignment layers and an MLP projector to map raw EEG signals to a rich visual latent space. We evaluate our approach using a broad suite of image reconstruction metrics that have been standardized in the adjacent field of fMRI-to-Image research, and we describe the first EEG-to-Image study to conduct extensive behavioral evaluations of our reconstructions using human raters. Our simple and robust architecture provides a significant performance boost across both research-grade and consumer-grade EEG hardware, and a substantial improvement in fine-tuning efficiency and inference cost. Finally, we provide extensive ablations to determine the architectural choices most responsible for our performance gains in both single and multi-subject cases across multiple benchmark datasets. Collectively, our work provides a substantial step towards the development of practical brain-computer interface applications.

摘要（中文）: 为了在实际应用中发挥作用，脑机接口模型必须能够轻松快速地部署到新受试者身上，能够在经济实惠的扫描硬件上有效运行，并且足够小，以便在可访问的计算资源上本地运行。为了直接解决这些当前的局限性，我们推出了ENIGMA，一种多受试者脑电图(EEG)到图像解码模型，它可以从脑电图记录中重构所看到的图像，并在研究级THINGS-EEG2和消费级AllJoined-1.6M基准测试中实现最先进(SOTA)的性能，同时能够使用低至15分钟的数据在新受试者身上进行有效的微调。ENIGMA拥有更简单的架构，所需的训练参数不到先前方法的1%。我们的方法集成了一个受试者统一的时空骨干网络，以及一组多受试者潜在对齐层和一个MLP投影器，以将原始脑电信号映射到丰富的视觉潜在空间。我们使用一套广泛的图像重构指标来评估我们的方法，这些指标已经在fMRI到图像研究的相关领域中进行了标准化，并且我们描述了第一个使用人工评估员对我们的重构图像进行广泛行为评估的EEG到图像研究。我们简单而强大的架构在研究级和消费级脑电硬件上都提供了显著的性能提升，并且在微调效率和推理成本方面都有了显著的改进。最后，我们进行了广泛的消融实验，以确定在多个基准数据集的单受试者和多受试者情况下，对我们的性能提升贡献最大的架构选择。总而言之，我们的工作为开发实用的脑机接口应用提供了实质性的一步。

TLDR: The paper introduces ENIGMA, a novel EEG-to-Image decoding model that achieves SOTA performance with significantly fewer parameters and rapid fine-tuning on new subjects, making it more practical for real-life BCI applications.

Authors: Reese Kneeland, Wangshu Jiang, Ugo Bruzadin Nunes, Paul Steven Scotti, Arnaud Delorme, Jonathan Xu

UltraLIF: Fully Differentiable Spiking Neural Networks via Ultradiscretization and Max-Plus Algebra

Abstract (English): Spiking Neural Networks (SNNs) offer energy-efficient, biologically plausible computation but suffer from non-differentiable spike generation, necessitating reliance on heuristic surrogate gradients. This paper introduces UltraLIF, a principled framework that replaces surrogate gradients with ultradiscretization, a mathematical formalism from tropical geometry providing continuous relaxations of discrete dynamics. The central insight is that the max-plus semiring underlying ultradiscretization naturally models neural threshold dynamics: the log-sum-exp function serves as a differentiable soft-maximum that converges to hard thresholding as a learnable temperature parameter $\eps \to 0$. Two neuron models are derived from distinct dynamical systems: UltraLIF from the LIF ordinary differential equation (temporal dynamics) and UltraDLIF from the diffusion equation modeling gap junction coupling across neuronal populations (spatial dynamics). Both yield fully differentiable SNNs trainable via standard backpropagation with no forward-backward mismatch. Theoretical analysis establishes pointwise convergence to classical LIF dynamics with quantitative error bounds and bounded non-vanishing gradients. Experiments on six benchmarks spanning static images, neuromorphic vision, and audio demonstrate improvements over surrogate gradient baselines, with gains most pronounced in single-timestep ($T{=}1$) settings on neuromorphic and temporal datasets. An optional sparsity penalty enables significant energy reduction while maintaining competitive accuracy.

摘要（中文）: 脉冲神经网络(SNNs)提供了高能效、生物学上合理的计算方式，但受到不可微的脉冲产生机制的限制，因此需要依赖启发式替代梯度。本文介绍了一种名为UltraLIF的原则性框架，该框架用超离散化替代了替代梯度，超离散化是一种来自热带几何学的数学形式，提供了离散动力学的连续松弛。核心见解是，超离散化背后的最大加半环自然地建模了神经元阈值动力学：log-sum-exp函数充当可微的软最大值，并且当可学习的温度参数$\eps \to 0$时收敛到硬阈值。从不同的动力学系统推导出两种神经元模型：UltraLIF来自Leaky Integrate-and-Fire (LIF)常微分方程（时间动力学），UltraDLIF来自模拟神经元群体间隙连接耦合的扩散方程（空间动力学）。两者都产生完全可微的SNN，可以通过标准反向传播进行训练，而无需前向-后向不匹配。理论分析建立了与经典LIF动力学的逐点收敛，具有定量的误差界限和有界的非消失梯度。在涵盖静态图像、神经形态视觉和音频的六个基准上的实验表明，与替代梯度基线相比有所改进，在神经形态和时间数据集上的单时间步长 ($T{=}1$) 设置中，收益最为显著。可选的稀疏性惩罚可以在保持竞争性准确率的同时显著降低能量消耗。

TLDR: The paper introduces UltraLIF, a fully differentiable Spiking Neural Network framework utilizing ultradiscretization to replace surrogate gradients, achieving improved performance over surrogate gradient methods on various benchmarks, especially in single-timestep scenarios.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了UltraLIF，一个完全可微分的脉冲神经网络框架，它利用超离散化来替代替代梯度，并在各种基准测试中实现了优于替代梯度方法的性能，尤其是在单时间步长的情况下。

Authors: Jose Marie Antonio Miñoza

ReTracing: An Archaeological Approach Through Body, Machine, and Generative Systems

Abstract (English): We present ReTracing, a multi-agent embodied performance art that adopts an archaeological approach to examine how artificial intelligence shapes, constrains, and produces bodily movement. Drawing from science-fiction novels, the project extracts sentences that describe human-machine interaction. We use large language models (LLMs) to generate paired prompts "what to do" and "what not to do" for each excerpt. A diffusion-based text-to-video model transforms these prompts into choreographic guides for a human performer and motor commands for a quadruped robot. Both agents enact the actions on a mirrored floor, captured by multi-camera motion tracking and reconstructed into 3D point clouds and motion trails, forming a digital archive of motion traces. Through this process, ReTracing serves as a novel approach to reveal how generative systems encode socio-cultural biases through choreographed movements. Through an immersive interplay of AI, human, and robot, ReTracing confronts a critical question of our time: What does it mean to be human among AIs that also move, think, and leave traces behind?

摘要（中文）: 我们展示“重溯 (ReTracing)”，一个多智能体具身表演艺术，它采用考古学方法来考察人工智能如何塑造、约束和生产身体运动。该项目从科幻小说中提取描述人机交互的句子，并使用大型语言模型 (LLMs) 为每个节选生成配对提示：“做什么”和“不做什么”。基于扩散的文本到视频模型将这些提示转化为人体表演者的编舞指南和四足机器人的运动指令。这两个智能体在镜面地板上执行这些动作，通过多摄像头运动追踪捕获，并重建为3D点云和运动轨迹，形成运动痕迹的数字档案。通过这个过程，“重溯”作为一种新颖的方法，揭示了生成系统如何通过编排的动作来编码社会文化偏见。通过人工智能、人类和机器人沉浸式的互动，“重溯”直面我们时代的一个关键问题：在也会移动、思考和留下痕迹的人工智能中，成为一个人意味着什么？

TLDR: ReTracing uses AI to generate choreographic guides for a human and robot, examining how generative systems encode socio-cultural biases through movement, creating a digital archive of their interactions.

简要说明: ReTracing利用人工智能为人类和机器人生成舞蹈指导，从而研究生成系统如何通过运动编码社会文化偏见，并创建其交互的数字档案。

Authors: Yitong Wang, Yue Yao

The Garbage Dataset (GD): A Multi-Class Image Benchmark for Automated Waste Segregation

Abstract (English): This study introduces the Garbage Dataset (GD), a publicly available image dataset designed to advance automated waste segregation through machine learning and computer vision. It's a diverse dataset covering 10 common household waste categories: metal, glass, biological, paper, battery, trash, cardboard, shoes, clothes, and plastic. The dataset comprises 13,348 labeled images collected through multiple methods, including DWaste mobile app and curated web sources. Methods included rigorous validation through checksums and outlier detection, analysis of class imbalance and visual separability via PCA/t-SNE, and assessment of background complexity using entropy and saliency measures. The dataset was benchmarked using state-of-the-art deep learning models (EfficientNetV2M, EfficientNetV2S, MobileNet, ResNet50, ResNet101) evaluated on performance metrics and operational carbon emissions. Experiment results indicate EfficientNetV2S achieved the highest performance with 96.19% accuracy and a 0.96 F1-score, though with a moderate carbon cost. Analysis revealed inherent dataset characteristics including class imbalance, a skew toward high-outlier classes (plastic, cardboard, paper), and brightness variations that require consideration. The main conclusion is that GD provides a valuable, real-world benchmark for waste classification research while highlighting important challenges such as class imbalance, background complexity, and environmental trade-offs in model selection that must be addressed for practical deployment. The dataset is publicly released to support further research in environmental sustainability applications.

摘要（中文）: 本研究介绍了垃圾数据集（GD），这是一个公开可用的图像数据集，旨在通过机器学习和计算机视觉推进自动化垃圾分类。它是一个多样化的数据集，涵盖10种常见的家庭垃圾类别：金属、玻璃、生物、纸张、电池、垃圾、纸板、鞋子、衣服和塑料。该数据集包含13,348张标记图像，通过多种方法收集，包括DWaste移动应用程序和精选的Web资源。方法包括通过校验和及离群值检测进行严格验证，通过PCA/t-SNE分析类别不平衡和视觉可分离性，以及使用熵和显著性测量评估背景复杂性。使用最先进的深度学习模型（EfficientNetV2M、EfficientNetV2S、MobileNet、ResNet50、ResNet101）对数据集进行了基准测试，评估了其性能指标和运行碳排放。实验结果表明，EfficientNetV2S取得了最高的性能，准确率为96.19%，F1分数为0.96，但碳成本适中。分析揭示了数据集固有的特征，包括类别不平衡、向高离群类（塑料、纸板、纸张）的倾斜以及需要考虑的亮度变化。主要结论是，GD为垃圾分类研究提供了一个有价值的、真实的基准，同时强调了重要的挑战，如类别不平衡、背景复杂性和模型选择中的环境权衡，这些挑战必须解决才能实现实际部署。该数据集已公开，以支持环境可持续性应用的进一步研究。

TLDR: The paper introduces a new, publicly available, multi-class image dataset (Garbage Dataset - GD) for automated waste segregation, benchmarking it with several deep learning models and analyzing dataset characteristics like class imbalance.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个新的公开多类别图像数据集（垃圾数据集 - GD），用于自动垃圾分类，并使用几种深度学习模型对其进行基准测试，并分析数据集的特征，如类别不平衡。

Authors: Suman Kunwar

Quantum Multiple Rotation Averaging

Abstract (English): Multiple rotation averaging (MRA) is a fundamental optimization problem in 3D vision and robotics that aims to recover globally consistent absolute rotations from noisy relative measurements. Established classical methods, such as L1-IRLS and Shonan, face limitations including local minima susceptibility and reliance on convex relaxations that fail to preserve the exact manifold geometry, leading to reduced accuracy in high-noise scenarios. We introduce IQARS (Iterative Quantum Annealing for Rotation Synchronization), the first algorithm that reformulates MRA as a sequence of local quadratic non-convex sub-problems executable on quantum annealers after binarization, to leverage inherent hardware advantages. IQARS removes convex relaxation dependence and better preserves non-Euclidean rotation manifold geometry while leveraging quantum tunneling and parallelism for efficient solution space exploration. We evaluate IQARS's performance on synthetic and real-world datasets. While current annealers remain in their nascent phase and only support solving problems of limited scale with constrained performance, we observed that IQARS on D-Wave annealers can already achieve ca. 12% higher accuracy than Shonan, i.e., the best-performing classical method evaluated empirically.

摘要（中文）: 多重旋转平均 (MRA) 是 3D 视觉和机器人领域中的一个基础优化问题，旨在从带噪声的相对测量中恢复全局一致的绝对旋转。诸如 L1-IRLS 和 Shonan 等已确立的经典方法面临着一些局限性，包括容易陷入局部最小值以及依赖于未能保留精确流形几何形状的凸松弛，从而导致在高噪声场景中精度降低。我们引入了 IQARS（用于旋转同步的迭代量子退火），这是首个将 MRA 重构为一系列可在二值化后在量子退火器上执行的局部二次非凸子问题的算法，以利用固有的硬件优势。 IQARS 消除了对凸松弛的依赖，并更好地保留了非欧几里得旋转流形几何形状，同时利用量子隧穿和并行性进行高效的解空间探索。我们评估了 IQARS 在合成和真实世界数据集上的性能。虽然目前的退火器仍处于起步阶段，仅支持求解规模有限且性能受限的问题，但我们观察到，IQARS 在 D-Wave 退火器上已经可以实现比 Shonan（即经验评估中性能最佳的经典方法）高约 12% 的准确率。

TLDR: This paper introduces IQARS, a quantum annealing algorithm for multiple rotation averaging (MRA) that outperforms classical methods by preserving manifold geometry and leveraging quantum hardware advantages, showing promising results despite current hardware limitations.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种用于多重旋转平均（MRA）的量子退火算法IQARS，该算法通过保留流形几何形状和利用量子硬件优势优于经典方法。尽管当前硬件条件有限，但显示出很有前景的结果。

Authors: Shuteng Wang, Natacha Kuete Meli, Michael Möller, Vladislav Golyanik

CMAD: Cooperative Multi-Agent Diffusion via Stochastic Optimal Control

Abstract (English): Continuous-time generative models have achieved remarkable success in image restoration and synthesis. However, controlling the composition of multiple pre-trained models remains an open challenge. Current approaches largely treat composition as an algebraic composition of probability densities, such as via products or mixtures of experts. This perspective assumes the target distribution is known explicitly, which is almost never the case. In this work, we propose a different paradigm that formulates compositional generation as a cooperative Stochastic Optimal Control problem. Rather than combining probability densities, we treat pre-trained diffusion models as interacting agents whose diffusion trajectories are jointly steered, via optimal control, toward a shared objective defined on their aggregated output. We validate our framework on conditional MNIST generation and compare it against a naive inference-time DPS-style baseline replacing learned cooperative control with per-step gradient guidance.

摘要（中文）: 连续时间生成模型在图像修复和合成方面取得了显著成功。然而，控制多个预训练模型的组合构成仍然是一个开放性挑战。现有方法主要将组合视为概率密度的代数组合，例如通过乘积或专家混合。这种观点假设目标分布是显式已知的，而这几乎是不可能的。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种不同的范式，将组合生成 формули的表达为一个合作的随机最优控制问题。我们不是组合概率密度，而是将预训练的扩散模型视为交互代理，这些代理的扩散轨迹通过最优控制共同引导至一个在它们的聚合输出上定义的共享目标。我们在条件MNIST生成上验证了我们的框架，并将其与一个朴素的推理时DPS风格的基线进行比较，该基线用每步梯度指导代替了学习到的合作控制。

TLDR: This paper proposes a cooperative Stochastic Optimal Control framework (CMAD) for composing multiple pre-trained diffusion models, treating them as interacting agents driven by a shared objective, instead of manipulating probability densities directly.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种合作随机最优控制框架 (CMAD)，用于组合多个预训练的扩散模型。该框架将这些模型视为由共同目标驱动的交互代理，而不是直接操作概率密度。

Authors: Riccardo Barbano, Alexander Denker, Zeljko Kereta, Runchang Li, Francisco Vargas

Domain Knowledge Guided Bayesian Optimization For Autonomous Alignment Of Complex Scientific Instruments

Abstract (English): Bayesian Optimization (BO) is a powerful tool for optimizing complex non-linear systems. However, its performance degrades in high-dimensional problems with tightly coupled parameters and highly asymmetric objective landscapes, where rewards are sparse. In such needle-in-a-haystack scenarios, even advanced methods like trust-region BO (TurBO) often lead to unsatisfactory results. We propose a domain knowledge guided Bayesian Optimization approach, which leverages physical insight to fundamentally simplify the search problem by transforming coordinates to decouple input features and align the active subspaces with the primary search axes. We demonstrate this approach's efficacy on a challenging 12-dimensional, 6-crystal Split-and-Delay optical system, where conventional approaches, including standard BO, TuRBO and multi-objective BO, consistently led to unsatisfactory results. When combined with an reverse annealing exploration strategy, this approach reliably converges to the global optimum. The coordinate transformation itself is the key to this success, significantly accelerating the search by aligning input co-ordinate axes with the problem's active subspaces. As increasingly complex scientific instruments, from large telescopes to new spectrometers at X-ray Free Electron Lasers are deployed, the demand for robust high-dimensional optimization grows. Our results demonstrate a generalizable paradigm: leveraging physical insight to transform high-dimensional, coupled optimization problems into simpler representations can enable rapid and robust automated tuning for consistent high performance while still retaining current optimization algorithms.

摘要（中文）: 贝叶斯优化（BO）是优化复杂非线性系统的强大工具。然而，在高维问题中，当参数紧密耦合且目标函数呈现高度不对称的 landscape，以及奖励稀疏时，其性能会下降。在这样的“大海捞针”场景中，即使是诸如信任区域贝叶斯优化（TurBO）等先进方法也常常导致不理想的结果。我们提出了一种领域知识引导的贝叶斯优化方法，该方法利用物理洞察力，通过转换坐标来解耦输入特征，并将 active subspace 与主搜索轴对齐，从而从根本上简化搜索问题。我们在一个具有挑战性的 12 维、6 晶体分束延迟光学系统中演示了这种方法的有效性，在该系统中，包括标准 BO、TuRBO 和多目标 BO 在内的传统方法始终导致不尽人意的结果。当与反向退火探索策略相结合时，该方法能够可靠地收敛到全局最优解。坐标变换本身是成功的关键，它通过将输入坐标轴与问题的 active subspace 对齐，显著加速了搜索过程。随着从大型望远镜到 X 射线自由电子激光器上的新型光谱仪等日益复杂的科学仪器的部署，对稳健的高维优化的需求也在增长。我们的结果展示了一种可推广的范例：利用物理洞察力将高维、耦合的优化问题转换为更简单的表示形式，能够实现快速而稳健的自动调谐，从而持续保持高性能，同时仍然保留当前的优化算法。

TLDR: This paper introduces a domain knowledge-guided Bayesian Optimization approach that uses physical insights to simplify high-dimensional optimization problems in scientific instruments, demonstrating improved performance on a complex optical system.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种领域知识引导的贝叶斯优化方法，利用物理洞察力来简化科学仪器中的高维优化问题，并在一个复杂的光学系统上展示了改进的性能。

Authors: Aashwin Mishra, Matt Seaberg, Ryan Roussel, Daniel Ratner, Apurva Mehta

Distributed Online Convex Optimization with Nonseparable Costs and Constraints

Abstract (English): This paper studies distributed online convex optimization with time-varying coupled constraints, motivated by distributed online control in network systems. Most prior work assumes a separability condition: the global objective and coupled constraint functions are sums of local costs and individual constraints. In contrast, we study a group of agents, networked via a communication graph, that collectively select actions to minimize a sequence of nonseparable global cost functions and to stratify nonseparable long-term constraints based on full-information feedback and intra-agent communication. We propose a distributed online primal-dual belief consensus algorithm, where each agent maintains and updates a local belief of the global collective decisions, which are repeatedly exchanged with neighboring agents. Unlike the previous consensus primal-dual algorithms under separability that ask agents to only communicate their local decisions, our belief-sharing protocol eliminates coupling between the primal consensus disagreement and the dual constraint violation, yielding sublinear regret and cumulative constraint violation (CCV) bounds, both in $O({T}^{1/2})$, where $T$ denotes the time horizon. Such a result breaks the long-standing $O(T^{3/4})$ barrier for CCV and matches the lower bound of online constrained convex optimization, indicating the online learning efficiency at the cost of communication overhead.

摘要（中文）: 本文研究具有时变耦合约束的分布式在线凸优化问题，其动机来源于网络系统中的分布式在线控制。 现有的大部分工作都假设了可分离性条件：即全局目标函数和耦合约束函数是局部代价和个体约束的总和。 与此相反，我们研究了一组通过通信图连接的智能体，它们集体选择行动以最小化一系列不可分离的全局代价函数，并基于全信息反馈和智能体间通信来满足不可分离的长期约束。 我们提出了一种分布式在线原始-对偶置信度一致算法，其中每个智能体维护并更新对全局集体决策的局部置信度，这些置信度会与相邻智能体反复交换。 不同于以往在可分离性条件下要求智能体仅通信其局部决策的一致性原始-对偶算法，我们的置信度共享协议消除了原始一致性差异与对偶约束违反之间的耦合，从而产生了亚线性遗憾和累积约束违反（CCV）界限，两者均为 $O({T}^{1/2})$，其中 $T$ 表示时间范围。 这样的结果打破了 CCV 长期存在的 $O(T^{3/4})$ 壁垒，并与在线约束凸优化的下界相匹配，表明以通信开销为代价实现了在线学习效率。

TLDR: This paper presents a distributed online primal-dual belief consensus algorithm for online convex optimization with nonseparable costs and constraints, achieving sublinear regret and cumulative constraint violation bounds of $O({T}^{1/2})$.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种分布式在线原始-对偶置信共识算法，用于具有不可分离成本和约束的在线凸优化，实现了 $O({T}^{1/2})$ 的次线性后悔和累积约束违反界。

Authors: Zhaoye Pan, Haozhe Lei, Fan Zuo, Zilin Bian, Tao Li

Digging for Data: Experiments in Rock Pile Characterization Using Only Proprioceptive Sensing in Excavation

Abstract (English): Characterization of fragmented rock piles is a fundamental task in the mining and quarrying industries, where rock is fragmented by blasting, transported using wheel loaders, and then sent for further processing. This field report studies a novel method for estimating the relative particle size of fragmented rock piles from only proprioceptive data collected while digging with a wheel loader. Rather than employ exteroceptive sensors (e.g., cameras or LiDAR sensors) to estimate rock particle sizes, the studied method infers rock fragmentation from an excavator's inertial response during excavation. This paper expands on research that postulated the use of wavelet analysis to construct a unique feature that is proportional to the level of rock fragmentation. We demonstrate through extensive field experiments that the ratio of wavelet features, constructed from data obtained by excavating in different rock piles with different size distributions, approximates the ratio of the mean particle size of the two rock piles. Full-scale excavation experiments were performed with a battery electric, 18-tonne capacity, load-haul-dump (LHD) machine in representative conditions in an operating quarry. The relative particle size estimates generated with the proposed sensing methodology are compared with those obtained from both a vision-based fragmentation analysis tool and from sieving of sampled materials.

摘要（中文）: 破碎岩堆的表征是采矿和采石行业的一项基本任务，在该行业中，岩石通过爆破破碎，使用轮式装载机运输，然后送去进一步处理。这份现场报告研究了一种新方法，仅根据轮式装载机挖掘时收集的本体感受数据来估算破碎岩堆的相对粒度。该方法并非采用外部感受传感器（如摄像头或激光雷达传感器）来估算岩石颗粒大小，而是从挖掘机在挖掘过程中的惯性响应推断岩石破碎情况。本文扩展了之前的一项研究，该研究假设使用小波分析构建与岩石破碎程度成比例的独特特征。我们通过大量的现场实验证明，由不同粒径分布岩堆的挖掘数据构建的小波特征的比率，近似于两个岩堆平均粒径的比率。在运营采石场的代表性条件下，使用一台电池驱动的、18吨容量的铲运机（LHD）进行了全面的挖掘实验。将使用所提出的传感方法生成的相对粒度估计值与使用基于视觉的破碎分析工具和筛分采样材料获得的估计值进行比较。

TLDR: This paper explores a novel method for estimating rock particle size in mining using proprioceptive data from a wheel loader. It infers fragmentation from inertial response during excavation, showing the ratio of wavelet features approximates the ratio of mean particle size.

简要说明: 该论文探索了一种新方法，利用轮式装载机的本体感觉数据来估计采矿中的岩石颗粒大小。它通过挖掘过程中的惯性响应来推断破碎程度，表明小波特征的比率接近平均颗粒大小的比率。

Authors: Unal Artan, Martin Magnusson, Joshua A. Marshall

Design, Development, and Use of Maya Robot as an Assistant for the Therapy/Education of Children with Cancer: a Pilot Study

Abstract (English): This study centers around the design and implementation of the Maya Robot, a portable elephant-shaped social robot, intended to engage with children undergoing cancer treatment. Initial efforts were devoted to enhancing the robot's facial expression recognition accuracy, achieving a 98% accuracy through deep neural networks. Two subsequent preliminary exploratory experiments were designed to advance the study's objectives. The first experiment aimed to compare pain levels experienced by children during the injection process, with and without the presence of the Maya robot. Twenty-five children, aged 4 to 9, undergoing cancer treatment participated in this counterbalanced study. The paired T-test results revealed a significant reduction in perceived pain when the robot was actively present in the injection room. The second experiment sought to assess perspectives of hospitalized children and their mothers during engagement with Maya through a game. Forty participants, including 20 children aged 4 to 9 and their mothers, were involved. Post Human-Maya Interactions, UTAUT questionnaire results indicated that children experienced significantly less anxiety than their parents during the interaction and game play. Notably, children exhibited higher trust levels in both the robot and the games, presenting a statistically significant difference in trust levels compared to their parents (P-value < 0.05). This preliminary exploratory study highlights the positive impact of utilizing Maya as an assistant for therapy/education in a clinical setting, particularly benefiting children undergoing cancer treatment. The findings underscore the potential of social robots in pediatric healthcare contexts, emphasizing improved pain management and emotional well-being among young patients.

摘要（中文）: 本研究专注于便携式大象造型社交机器人Maya Robot的设计与实现，旨在与接受癌症治疗的儿童互动。最初的工作致力于提高机器人面部表情识别的准确性，通过深度神经网络实现了98%的准确率。随后设计了两个初步探索性实验，以推进研究目标。第一个实验旨在比较儿童在注射过程中有和没有Maya Robot陪伴时所经历的疼痛程度。25名年龄在4至9岁的接受癌症治疗的儿童参与了这项平衡对照研究。配对T检验结果显示，当机器人在注射室中处于活动状态时，感知到的疼痛显著降低。第二个实验旨在通过游戏评估住院儿童及其母亲与Maya互动期间的看法。共计40名参与者，包括20名年龄在4至9岁的儿童及其母亲。人机互动后，UTAUT问卷结果表明，在互动和游戏过程中，儿童的焦虑程度明显低于他们的父母。值得注意的是，儿童对机器人和游戏的信任度均较高，与他们的父母相比，信任度存在统计学上的显著差异（P值 < 0.05）。这项初步探索性研究强调了在临床环境中利用Maya作为治疗/教育助手所产生的积极影响，尤其是有益于接受癌症治疗的儿童。研究结果突出了社交机器人在儿科医疗保健领域的潜力，强调了改善年轻患者的疼痛管理和情绪健康。

Biomimetic Mantaray robot toward the underwater autonomous -- Experimental verification of swimming and diving by flapping motion -

Abstract (English): This study presents the development and experimental verification of a biomimetic manta ray robot for underwater autonomous exploration. Inspired by manta rays, the robot uses flapping motion for propulsion to minimize seabed disturbance and enhance efficiency compared to traditional screw propulsion. The robot features pectoral fins driven by servo motors and a streamlined control box to reduce fluid resistance. The control system, powered by a Raspberry Pi 3B, includes an IMU and pressure sensor for real-time monitoring and control. Experiments in a pool assessed the robot's swimming and diving capabilities. Results show stable swimming and diving motions with PD control. The robot is suitable for applications in environments like aquariums and fish nurseries, requiring minimal disturbance and efficient maneuverability. Our findings demonstrate the potential of bio-inspired robotic designs to improve ecological monitoring and underwater exploration.

Authors: Kenta Tabata, Ryosuke Oku, Jun Ito, Renato Miyagusuku, Koichi Ozaki

3D-Printed Anisotropic Soft Magnetic Coating for Directional Rolling of a Magnetically Actuated Capsule Robot

Abstract (English): Capsule robots are promising tools for minimally invasive diagnostics and therapy, with applications from gastrointestinal endoscopy to targeted drug delivery and biopsy sampling. Conventional magnetic capsule robots embed bulky permanent magnets at both ends, reducing the usable cavity by about 10-20 mm and limiting integration of functional modules. We propose a compact, 3D-printed soft capsule robot with a magnetic coating that replaces internal magnets, enabling locomotion via a thin, functional shell while preserving the entire interior cavity as a continuous volume for medical payloads. The compliant silicone-magnetic composite also improves swallowability, even with a slightly larger capsule size. Magnetostatic simulations and experiments confirm that programmed NSSN/SNNS pole distributions provide strong anisotropy and reliable torque generation, enabling stable bidirectional rolling, omnidirectional steering, climbing on 7.5 degree inclines, and traversal of 5 mm protrusions. Rolling motion is sustained when the magnetic field at the capsule reaches at least 0.3 mT, corresponding to an effective actuation depth of 30 mm in our setup. Future work will optimize material composition, coating thickness, and magnetic layouts to enhance force output and durability, while next-generation robotic-arm-based field generators with closed-loop feedback will address nonlinearities and expand maneuverability. Together, these advances aim to transition coating-based capsule robots toward reliable clinical deployment and broaden their applications in minimally invasive diagnostics and therapy.

Authors: Jin Zhou, Chongxun Wang, Zikang Shen, Fangzhou Xia

Pitch Angle Control of a Magnetically Actuated Capsule Robot with Nonlinear FEA-based MPC and EKF Multisensory Fusion

Abstract (English): Magnetically actuated capsule robots promise minimally invasive diagnosis and therapy in the gastrointestinal (GI) tract, but existing systems largely neglect control of capsule pitch, a degree of freedom critical for contact-rich interaction with inclined gastric walls. This paper presents a nonlinear, model-based framework for magnetic pitch control of an ingestible capsule robot actuated by a four-coil electromagnetic array. Angle-dependent magnetic forces and torques acting on embedded permanent magnets are characterized using three-dimensional finite-element simulations and embedded as lookup tables in a control-oriented rigid-body pitching model with rolling contact and actuator dynamics. A constrained model predictive controller (MPC) is designed to regulate pitch while respecting hardware-imposed current and slew-rate limits. Experiments on a compliant stomach-inspired surface demonstrate robust pitch reorientation from both horizontal and upright configurations, achieving about three to five times faster settling and reduced oscillatory motion than on-off control. Furthermore, an extended Kalman filter (EKF) fusing inertial sensing with intermittent visual measurements enables stable closed-loop control when the camera update rate is reduced from 30 Hz to 1 Hz, emulating clinically realistic imaging constraints. These results establish finite-element-informed MPC with sensor fusion as a scalable strategy for pitch regulation, controlled docking, and future multi-degree-of-freedom capsule locomotion.

摘要（中文）: 磁驱动胶囊机器人有望在胃肠道实现微创诊断和治疗，但现有系统在很大程度上忽略了胶囊俯仰姿态的控制，而俯仰姿态是与倾斜胃壁进行接触式交互的关键自由度。本文提出了一种基于非线性模型的磁性俯仰控制框架，用于控制由四线圈电磁阵列驱动的可吞咽胶囊机器人。利用三维有限元仿真对作用于嵌入式永磁体的角度相关磁力和磁扭矩进行表征，并将其作为查找表嵌入到面向控制的刚体俯仰模型中，该模型考虑了滚动接触和执行器动力学。设计了一种约束模型预测控制器（MPC）来调节俯仰姿态，同时兼顾硬件施加的电流和转换速率限制。在类胃顺应性表面上的实验表明，该方法能够从水平和垂直结构实现鲁棒的俯仰姿态重定向，与开关控制相比，实现了约三到五倍更快的稳定时间和减少的振荡运动。此外，扩展卡尔曼滤波器（EKF）融合了惯性传感与间歇性视觉测量，即使在相机更新速率从 30 Hz 降至 1 Hz 的情况下也能实现稳定的闭环控制，模拟了临床真实的成像约束。这些结果表明，基于有限元信息的 MPC 与传感器融合是俯仰调节、受控对接以及未来多自由度胶囊运动的可扩展策略。

Authors: Chongxun Wang, Zikang Shen, Apoorav Rathore, Akanimoh Udombeh, Harrison Teng, Fangzhou Xia

Transforming Policy-Car Swerving for Mitigating Stop-and-Go Traffic Waves: A Practice-Oriented Jam-Absorption Driving Strategy

Abstract (English): Stop-and-go waves, as a major form of freeway traffic congestion, cause severe and long-lasting adverse effects, including reduced traffic efficiency, increased driving risks, and higher vehicle emissions. Amongst the highway traffic management strategies, jam-absorption driving (JAD), in which a dedicated vehicle performs "slow-in" and "fast-out" maneuvers before being captured by a stop-and-go wave, has been proposed as a potential method for preventing the propagation of such waves. However, most existing JAD strategies remain impractical mainly due to the lack of discussion regarding implementation vehicles and operational conditions. Inspired by real-world observations of police-car swerving behavior, this paper first introduces a Single-Vehicle Two-Detector Jam-Absorption Driving (SVDD-JAD) problem, and then proposes a practical JAD strategy that transforms such behavior into a maneuver capable of suppressing the propagation of an isolated stop-and-go wave. Five key parameters that significantly affect the proposed strategy, namely, JAD speed, inflow traffic speed, wave width, wave speed, and in-wave speed, are identified and systematically analyzed. Using a SUMO-based simulation as an illustrative example, we further demonstrate how these parameters can be measured in practice with two stationary roadside traffic detectors. The results show that the proposed JAD strategy successfully suppresses the propagation of a stop-and-go wave, without triggering a secondary wave. This paper is expected to take a significant step toward making JAD practical, advancing it from a theoretical concept to a feasible and implementable strategy. To promote reproducibility in the transportation domain, we have also open-sourced all the code on our GitHub repository https://github.com/gotrafficgo.

摘要（中文）: 走走停停波是高速公路交通拥堵的主要形式，会造成严重且持久的不利影响，包括降低交通效率、增加驾驶风险以及提高车辆排放。在高速公路交通管理策略中，拥堵吸收驾驶（JAD）已被提出作为一种潜在的防止此类波传播的方法，其中专用车辆在被走走停停波捕获之前执行“慢进快出”的操作。然而，由于缺乏关于实施车辆和运营条件的讨论，大多数现有的JAD策略仍然不切实际。受到警车转向行为的实际观察启发，本文首先引入了一种单车双检测器拥堵吸收驾驶（SVDD-JAD）问题，然后提出了一种实用的JAD策略，该策略将此类行为转变为能够抑制孤立的走走停停波传播的操作。确定并系统地分析了显著影响所提策略的五个关键参数，即JAD速度、流入交通速度、波宽、波速和波内速度。以基于SUMO的模拟作为示例，我们进一步展示了如何在实践中使用两个固定的路侧交通检测器测量这些参数。结果表明，所提出的JAD策略成功地抑制了走走停停波的传播，而没有触发二次波。本文有望朝着使JAD实用化迈出重要一步，将其从一个理论概念发展成为一个可行且可实施的策略。为了促进交通运输领域的重现性，我们还在我们的GitHub存储库https://github.com/gotrafficgo上开源了所有代码。

TLDR: This paper proposes a practical jam-absorption driving strategy using police-car swerving behavior to mitigate stop-and-go traffic waves, validated through SUMO simulations and open-sourced code.

Authors: Zhengbing He

A Swap-Adversarial Framework for Improving Domain Generalization in Electroencephalography-Based Parkinson's Disease Prediction

Abstract (English): Electroencephalography (ECoG) offers a promising alternative to conventional electrocorticography (EEG) for the early prediction of Parkinson's disease (PD), providing higher spatial resolution and a broader frequency range. However, reproducible comparisons has been limited by ethical constraints in human studies and the lack of open benchmark datasets. To address this gap, we introduce a new dataset, the first reproducible benchmark for PD prediction. It is constructed from long-term ECoG recordings of 6-hydroxydopamine (6-OHDA)-induced rat models and annotated with neural responses measured before and after electrical stimulation. In addition, we propose a Swap-Adversarial Framework (SAF) that mitigates high inter-subject variability and the high-dimensional low-sample-size (HDLSS) problem in ECoG data, while achieving robust domain generalization across ECoG and EEG-based Brain-Computer Interface (BCI) datasets. The framework integrates (1) robust preprocessing, (2) Inter-Subject Balanced Channel Swap (ISBCS) for cross-subject augmentation, and (3) domain-adversarial training to suppress subject-specific bias. ISBCS randomly swaps channels between subjects to reduce inter-subject variability, and domain-adversarial training jointly encourages the model to learn task-relevant shared features. We validated the effectiveness of the proposed method through extensive experiments under cross-subject, cross-session, and cross-dataset settings. Our method consistently outperformed all baselines across all settings, showing the most significant improvements in highly variable environments. Furthermore, the proposed method achieved superior cross-dataset performance between public EEG benchmarks, demonstrating strong generalization capability not only within ECoG but to EEG data. The new dataset and source code will be made publicly available upon publication.

摘要（中文）: 脑电皮层电极记录（ECoG）为帕金森病（PD）的早期预测提供了一种优于传统脑电图（EEG）的有前景的替代方案，具有更高的空间分辨率和更宽的频率范围。然而，由于人体研究中的伦理限制以及缺乏开放的基准数据集，可重复的比较一直受到限制。为了弥补这一差距，我们引入了一个新的数据集，这是PD预测的第一个可重复的基准。它构建于6-羟基多巴胺（6-OHDA）诱导的大鼠模型的长期ECoG记录，并标注了电刺激前后测量的神经反应。此外，我们提出了一个Swap-Adversarial框架（SAF），该框架缓解了ECoG数据中较高个体间差异以及高维度低样本量（HDLSS）问题，同时实现了跨ECoG和基于EEG的脑机接口（BCI）数据集的鲁棒域泛化。该框架集成了（1）鲁棒的预处理，（2）用于跨受试者增强的受试者间平衡通道交换（ISBCS），以及（3）抑制受试者特定偏差的域对抗训练。ISBCS随机交换受试者之间的通道以减少个体间差异，而域对抗训练共同鼓励模型学习与任务相关的共享特征。我们通过在跨受试者、跨会话和跨数据集设置下的广泛实验验证了所提出方法的有效性。我们的方法在所有设置下始终优于所有基线方法，在高度可变的环境中表现出最显著的改进。此外，所提出的方法在公共EEG基准之间实现了卓越的跨数据集性能，表明了强大的泛化能力，不仅在ECoG中，而且在EEG数据中。新的数据集和源代码将在发表后公开提供。

TLDR: This paper introduces a new ECoG dataset for Parkinson's Disease prediction in rat models and proposes a Swap-Adversarial Framework (SAF) for improved domain generalization, demonstrating strong performance across ECoG and EEG datasets.

Authors: Seongwon Jin, Hanseul Choi, Sunggu Yang, Sungho Park, Jibum Kim

A Dual-Stream Physics-Augmented Unsupervised Architecture for Runtime Embedded Vehicle Health Monitoring

Abstract (English): Runtime quantification of vehicle operational intensity is essential for predictive maintenance and condition monitoring in commercial and heavy-duty fleets. Traditional metrics like mileage fail to capture mechanical burden, while unsupervised deep learning models detect statistical anomalies, typically transient surface shocks, but often conflate statistical stability with mechanical rest. We identify this as a critical blind spot: high-load steady states, such as hill climbing with heavy payloads, appear statistically normal yet impose significant drivetrain fatigue. To resolve this, we propose a Dual-Stream Architecture that fuses unsupervised learning for surface anomaly detection with macroscopic physics proxies for cumulative load estimation. This approach leverages low-frequency sensor data to generate a multi-dimensional health vector, distinguishing between dynamic hazards and sustained mechanical effort. Validated on a RISC-V embedded platform, the architecture demonstrates low computational overhead, enabling comprehensive, edge-based health monitoring on resource-constrained ECUs without the latency or bandwidth costs of cloud-based monitoring.

摘要（中文）: 车辆运行强度的实时量化对于商用和重型车队的预测性维护和状态监测至关重要。传统的指标，如里程数，无法捕捉机械负荷；而无监督深度学习模型虽然能够检测统计异常，通常是瞬态表面冲击，但常常将统计稳定性与机械静止混淆。我们认为这是一个关键的盲点：高负荷稳态，例如重载爬坡，在统计上看似正常，但会对动力总成造成显著的疲劳。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种双流架构，它融合了用于表面异常检测的无监督学习和用于累积负荷估计的宏观物理代理。这种方法利用低频传感器数据生成多维健康向量，区分动态危险和持续机械应力。该架构已在RISC-V嵌入式平台上进行了验证，证明其计算开销较低，能够在资源受限的ECU上实现全面的、基于边缘的健康监测，而无需基于云的监测的延迟或带宽成本。

TLDR: This paper introduces a dual-stream unsupervised learning architecture that combines anomaly detection with physics-based load estimation for vehicle health monitoring, addressing the limitations of traditional methods in identifying high-load steady states. The system is designed for edge deployment on resource-constrained embedded systems.

Authors: Enzo Nicolas Spotorno, Antonio Augusto Medeiros Frohlich

Quantum Integrated Sensing and Computation with Indefinite Causal Order

Abstract (English): Quantum operations with indefinite causal order (ICO) represent a framework in quantum information processing where the relative order between two events can be indefinite. In this paper, we investigate whether sensing and computation, two canonical tasks in quantum information processing, can be carried out within the ICO framework. We propose a scheme for integrated sensing and computation that uses the same quantum state for both tasks. The quantum state is represented as an agent that performs state observation and learns a function of the state to make predictions via a parametric model. Under an ICO operation, the agent experiences a superposition of orders, one in which it performs state observation and then executes the required computation steps, and another in which the agent carries out the computation first and then performs state observation. This is distinct from prevailing information processing and machine intelligence paradigms where information acquisition and learning follow a strict causal order, with the former always preceding the latter. We provide experimental results and we show that the proposed scheme can achieve small training and testing losses on a representative task in magnetic navigation.

摘要（中文）: 具有非确定因果顺序（ICO）的量子操作代表一种量子信息处理框架，在此框架中，两个事件之间的相对顺序可以是不确定的。本文探讨了诸如传感和计算这两种量子信息处理中的经典任务是否可以在ICO框架内执行。我们提出了一种集成传感和计算的方案，其中同一量子态用于执行这两项任务。该量子态被表示为一个代理，它执行状态观测并学习状态的函数，进而通过参数模型进行预测。在ICO操作下，该代理经历顺序的叠加，在一个顺序中，它先执行状态观测，然后执行所需的计算步骤；而在另一个顺序中，该代理先执行计算，然后再执行状态观测。这与流行的信息处理和机器智能范式不同，在那些范式中，信息获取和学习遵循严格的因果顺序，前者始终先于后者。我们提供了实验结果，并表明所提出的方案可以在磁导航中的一个代表性任务上实现较小的训练和测试损失。

TLDR: This paper explores a novel framework for integrated quantum sensing and computation using indefinite causal order (ICO), where the same quantum state is used for both tasks in a superposition of orders. They demonstrate experimental results in magnetic navigation.

简要说明: 该论文探索了一种新的量子传感和计算集成框架，利用不确定因果顺序（ICO），其中相同的量子态以顺序叠加的方式用于两个任务。他们展示了磁导航方面的实验结果。

Authors: Ivana Nikoloska

Viewpoint Recommendation for Point Cloud Labeling through Interaction Cost Modeling

Abstract (English): Semantic segmentation of 3D point clouds is important for many applications, such as autonomous driving. To train semantic segmentation models, labeled point cloud segmentation datasets are essential. Meanwhile, point cloud labeling is time-consuming for annotators, which typically involves tuning the camera viewpoint and selecting points by lasso. To reduce the time cost of point cloud labeling, we propose a viewpoint recommendation approach to reduce annotators' labeling time costs. We adapt Fitts' law to model the time cost of lasso selection in point clouds. Using the modeled time cost, the viewpoint that minimizes the lasso selection time cost is recommended to the annotator. We build a data labeling system for semantic segmentation of 3D point clouds that integrates our viewpoint recommendation approach. The system enables users to navigate to recommended viewpoints for efficient annotation. Through an ablation study, we observed that our approach effectively reduced the data labeling time cost. We also qualitatively compare our approach with previous viewpoint selection approaches on different datasets.

摘要（中文）: 三维点云的语义分割对于许多应用（如自动驾驶）至关重要。为了训练语义分割模型，标注的点云分割数据集必不可少。同时，点云标注对于标注者来说非常耗时，通常需要调整相机视角并使用套索选择点。为了减少点云标注的时间成本，我们提出了一种视角推荐方法，以降低标注者的标注时间成本。我们采用菲茨定律来建模点云中套索选择的时间成本。利用所建模的时间成本，向标注者推荐能够最小化套索选择时间成本的视角。我们构建了一个用于三维点云语义分割的数据标注系统，该系统集成了我们的视角推荐方法。该系统允许用户导航到推荐的视角，以实现高效标注。通过消融研究，我们观察到我们的方法有效地降低了数据标注的时间成本。我们还在不同的数据集上，将我们的方法与先前的视角选择方法进行了定性比较。

TLDR: This paper proposes a viewpoint recommendation system for 3D point cloud labeling that models the labeling time cost using Fitts' law to suggest optimal viewpoints, aiming to improve annotation efficiency.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种三维点云标注的视角推荐方法，该方法利用Fitts定律对标注时间成本进行建模，从而推荐最佳视角，旨在提高标注效率。

Authors: Yu Zhang, Xinyi Zhao, Chongke Bi, Siming Chen

Resource-Efficient RGB-Only Action Recognition for Edge Deployment

Abstract (English): Action recognition on edge devices poses stringent constraints on latency, memory, storage, and power consumption. While auxiliary modalities such as skeleton and depth information can enhance recognition performance, they often require additional sensors or computationally expensive pose-estimation pipelines, limiting practicality for edge use. In this work, we propose a compact RGB-only network tailored for efficient on-device inference. Our approach builds upon an X3D-style backbone augmented with Temporal Shift, and further introduces selective temporal adaptation and parameter-free attention. Extensive experiments on the NTU RGB+D 60 and 120 benchmarks demonstrate a strong accuracy-efficiency balance. Moreover, deployment-level profiling on the Jetson Orin Nano verifies a smaller on-device footprint and practical resource utilization compared to existing RGB-based action recognition techniques.

摘要（中文）: 在边缘设备上进行动作识别对延迟、内存、存储和功耗提出了严格的约束。虽然骨骼和深度信息等辅助模态可以提高识别性能，但它们通常需要额外的传感器或计算成本高昂的姿态估计流程，从而限制了其在边缘设备上的实用性。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种紧凑的仅使用RGB的网络，专为高效的设备端推理而定制。我们的方法基于一个带有时间移位的X3D风格骨干网络，并进一步引入了选择性时间适应和无参数注意力机制。在NTU RGB+D 60和120基准数据集上的大量实验证明了我们的方法在准确性和效率之间的强大平衡。此外，在Jetson Orin Nano上的部署级分析验证了与现有的基于RGB的动作识别技术相比，我们提出的方法具有更小的设备端占用空间和更合理的资源利用率。

TLDR: This paper presents a resource-efficient RGB-only action recognition network designed for edge deployment, achieving a strong accuracy-efficiency balance on standard benchmarks and demonstrating practical resource utilization on the Jetson Orin Nano.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种为边缘部署设计的资源高效的纯RGB动作识别网络，在标准基准测试上实现了强大的精度-效率平衡，并在Jetson Orin Nano上展示了实际的资源利用率。

Authors: Dongsik Yoon, Jongeun Kim, Dayeon Lee

Fast Person Detection Using YOLOX With AI Accelerator For Train Station Safety

Abstract (English): Recently, Image processing has advanced Faster and applied in many fields, including health, industry, and transportation. In the transportation sector, object detection is widely used to improve security, for example, in traffic security and passenger crossings at train stations. Some accidents occur in the train crossing area at the station, like passengers uncarefully when passing through the yellow line. So further security needs to be developed. Additional technology is required to reduce the number of accidents. This paper focuses on passenger detection applications at train stations using YOLOX and Edge AI Accelerator hardware. the performance of the AI accelerator will be compared with Jetson Orin Nano. The experimental results show that the Hailo-8 AI hardware accelerator has higher accuracy than Jetson Orin Nano (improvement of over 12%) and has lower latency than Jetson Orin Nano (reduced 20 ms).

Authors: Mas Nurul Achmadiah, Novendra Setyawan, Achmad Arif Bryantono, Chi-Chia Sun, Wen-Kai Kuo

PMMA: The Polytechnique Montreal Mobility Aids Dataset

Abstract (English): This study introduces a new object detection dataset of pedestrians using mobility aids, named PMMA. The dataset was collected in an outdoor environment, where volunteers used wheelchairs, canes, and walkers, resulting in nine categories of pedestrians: pedestrians, cane users, two types of walker users, whether walking or resting, five types of wheelchair users, including wheelchair users, people pushing empty wheelchairs, and three types of users pushing occupied wheelchairs, including the entire pushing group, the pusher and the person seated on the wheelchair. To establish a benchmark, seven object detection models (Faster R-CNN, CenterNet, YOLOX, DETR, Deformable DETR, DINO, and RT-DETR) and three tracking algorithms (ByteTrack, BOT-SORT, and OC-SORT) were implemented under the MMDetection framework. Experimental results show that YOLOX, Deformable DETR, and Faster R-CNN achieve the best detection performance, while the differences among the three trackers are relatively small. The PMMA dataset is publicly available at https://doi.org/10.5683/SP3/XJPQUG, and the video processing and model training code is available at https://github.com/DatasetPMMA/PMMA.

摘要（中文）: 本研究介绍了一个新的使用辅助行动设备的行人目标检测数据集，命名为PMMA。该数据集在户外环境中收集，志愿者使用轮椅、手杖和助行器，产生了九类行人：行人、手杖使用者、两种类型的助行器使用者（包括行走和休息状态）、五种类型的轮椅使用者（包括轮椅使用者、推空轮椅的人，以及三种类型的推坐有人的轮椅使用者，包括整个推动群体、推动者和坐在轮椅上的人）。为了建立基准，我们在MMDetection框架下实现了七种目标检测模型（Faster R-CNN、CenterNet、YOLOX、DETR、Deformable DETR、DINO和RT-DETR）和三种跟踪算法（ByteTrack、BOT-SORT和OC-SORT）。实验结果表明，YOLOX、Deformable DETR和Faster R-CNN取得了最佳的检测性能，而三种跟踪器之间的差异相对较小。PMMA数据集可在https://doi.org/10.5683/SP3/XJPQUG公开获取，视频处理和模型训练代码可在https://github.com/DatasetPMMA/PMMA获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces PMMA, a new object detection dataset focusing on pedestrians using mobility aids, with benchmark results from several object detection and tracking models. The dataset and code are publicly available.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个新的目标检测数据集PMMA，专注于使用辅助移动设备的行人，并提供了几种目标检测和跟踪模型的基准测试结果。数据集和代码已公开。

Authors: Qingwu Liu, Nicolas Saunier, Guillaume-Alexandre Bilodeau

Motion Capture is Not the Target Domain: Scaling Synthetic Data for Learning Motion Representations

Abstract (English): Synthetic data offers a compelling path to scalable pretraining when real-world data is scarce, but models pretrained on synthetic data often fail to transfer reliably to deployment settings. We study this problem in full-body human motion, where large-scale data collection is infeasible but essential for wearable-based Human Activity Recognition (HAR), and where synthetic motion can be generated from motion-capture-derived representations. We pretrain motion time-series models using such synthetic data and evaluate their transfer across diverse downstream HAR tasks. Our results show that synthetic pretraining improves generalisation when mixed with real data or scaled sufficiently. We also demonstrate that large-scale motion-capture pretraining yields only marginal gains due to domain mismatch with wearable signals, clarifying key sim-to-real challenges and the limits and opportunities of synthetic motion data for transferable HAR representations.

摘要（中文）: 合成数据为现实世界数据稀缺情况下的可扩展预训练提供了一条引人注目的途径，但基于合成数据预训练的模型通常无法可靠地迁移到部署环境中。我们在全身人体运动中研究了这个问题，在该领域，大规模数据收集是不可行的，但对于基于可穿戴设备的动作识别（HAR）至关重要，并且可以从动捕派生的表示中生成合成运动。我们使用这类合成数据预训练运动时序模型，并评估它们在各种下游HAR任务中的迁移能力。我们的结果表明，当与真实数据混合或充分扩展规模时，合成预训练能够提高泛化能力。我们还证明了，由于与可穿戴信号存在领域不匹配，大规模动捕预训练只能产生微小的增益，从而阐明了关键的模拟-现实挑战，以及合成运动数据在可迁移HAR表示方面的局限性和机遇。

TLDR: The paper investigates the effectiveness of synthetic motion data for pretraining models used in wearable-based Human Activity Recognition (HAR). It finds synthetic pretraining beneficial when mixed with real data or scaled significantly, and highlights the limitations of motion-capture data due to domain mismatch.

简要说明: 该论文研究了合成运动数据对在可穿戴设备上进行人体活动识别 (HAR) 的模型预训练的有效性。研究发现，当与真实数据混合或充分扩展时，合成预训练是有益的，并强调了由于领域不匹配，运动捕捉数据的局限性。

Authors: Firas Darwish, George Nicholson, Aiden Doherty, Hang Yuan

Lie Group Variational Integrator for the Geometrically Exact Rod with Circular Cross-Section Incorporating Cross-Sectional Deformation

Abstract (English): In this paper, we derive the continuous space-time equations of motion of a three-dimensional geometrically exact rod, or the Cosserat rod, incorporating planar cross-sectional deformation. We then adopt the Lie group variational integrator technique to obtain a discrete model of the rod incorporating both rotational motion and cross-sectional deformation as well. The resulting discrete model possesses several desirable features: it ensures volume conservation of the discrete elements by considering cross-sectional deformation through a local dilatation factor, it demonstrates the beneficial properties associated with the variational integrator technique, such as the preservation of the rotational configuration, and energy conservation with a bounded error. An exhaustive set of numerical results under various initial conditions of the rod demonstrates the efficacy of the model in replicating the physics of the system.

摘要（中文）: 本文推导了三维几何精确杆（或称Cosserat杆）的连续时空运动方程，其中考虑了平面截面变形。然后，我们采用李群变分积分器技术，获得了杆的离散模型，该模型同样包含了旋转运动和截面变形。所得离散模型具有几个理想的特性：它通过一个局部膨胀因子来考虑截面变形，从而确保离散单元的体积守恒；它展示了变分积分器技术所具有的优势，例如保持旋转配置和有界误差下的能量守恒。在一系列不同的杆的初始条件下的详尽数值结果表明，该模型在复制系统物理特性方面的有效性。

TLDR: This paper presents a Lie group variational integrator for simulating geometrically exact rods with circular cross-sections, incorporating cross-sectional deformation and demonstrating good conservation properties.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种李群变分积分器，用于模拟具有圆形截面的几何精确杆，考虑了截面变形，并展示了良好的守恒特性。

Authors: Srishti Siddharth, Vivek Natarajan, Ravi N. Banavar

Stability Analysis of Geometric Control for a Canonical Class of Underactuated Aerial Vehicles with Spurious Forces

Abstract (English): Standard geometric control relies on force-moment decoupling, an assumption that breaks down in many aerial platforms due to spurious forces naturally induced by control moments. While strategies for such coupled systems have been validated experimentally, a rigorous theoretical certification of their stability is currently missing. This work fills this gap by providing the first formal stability analysis for a generic class of floating rigid bodies subject to spurious forces. We introduce a canonical model and construct a Lyapunov-based proof establishing local exponential stability of the hovering equilibrium. Crucially, the analysis explicitly addresses the structural challenges - specifically the induced non-minimum-phase behavior - that prevent the application of standard cascade arguments.

摘要（中文）: 标准几何控制依赖于力-力矩解耦，但这一假设在许多飞行平台上失效，原因是控制力矩自然诱导的虚假力。虽然针对此类耦合系统的策略已通过实验验证，但目前缺乏对其稳定性的严格理论证明。本工作填补了这一空白，为一类受虚假力影响的通用漂浮刚体提供了首个正式的稳定性分析。我们引入了一个规范模型，并构建了一个基于李雅普诺夫的证明，证明了悬停平衡的局部指数稳定性。至关重要的是，该分析明确解决了阻碍标准级联论证应用的结构性挑战——特别是诱导的非最小相位行为。

TLDR: This paper provides a formal stability analysis for underactuated aerial vehicles experiencing spurious forces due to force-moment coupling, a common problem not rigorously addressed previously, by developing a Lyapunov-based proof for local exponential stability around hovering equilibrium.

简要说明: 本文针对由于力矩耦合而产生杂散力的欠驱动飞行器，通过开发基于李雅普诺夫的证明，针对悬停平衡点的局部指数稳定性，提供了严谨的稳定性分析，而先前没有对这一常见问题进行严格讨论。
